title": "Agnello in agrodolce (sweet and sour lamb)",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Agnello in agrodolce (sweet and sour lamb) an Italian recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#lamb #oliveoil #onions #tomato #duck #cream #whitewinevinegar #spaghetti #tomatopaste #granulatedsugar #lambtenderloin \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Eastern influences can be found in all agrodolce recipes, not least, this lamb dish. This is a delightful recipe\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 3346\n|PortionCalories = 836\n|DatePublished=29th July 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 1 hour 30 minutes\n |PrepTime = 10 minutes\n |CookTime = 1 hour 20 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Agnello in agrodolce recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">An unusual pasta dish</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">And it was lovely too.</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Sue_spins|Susie]] </span></span>\n}}\nEastern influences can be found in all [[Agrodolce|agrodolce]] recipes, not least, this [[Lamb|lamb]] dish.\n\nThis is a delightful recipe, but don't expect it to be the same as the bright [[Orange|orange]] Chinese version that you may be familiar with! \n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 large [[Onion|onion]], peeled and thinly sliced\n| 5 tablespoons of [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 5 tablespoons full [[Cream|cream]] [[Milk|milk]]\n| 3 tablespoons [[Tomato|tomato]] pur\u00e9e\n| 1 kg (2 lb) [[Lamb|lamb]] [[Shoulder|shoulder]], cut into bite-sized cubes\n| 125 ml high quality [[White wine vinegar|white wine vinegar]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Granulated sugar|granulated sugar]]\n| 6 fresh [[Basil leaves|basil leaves]], roughly chopped\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| [[Fry]] the [[Onions|onions]] in half of the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] until golden [[Brown|brown]] and reserve.\n| Meanwhile, mix the [[Milk|milk]] and [[Tomato paste|tomato paste]] together.\n| [[Brown]] the [[Lamb|lamb]] in the remaining [[Oil|oil]].\n| Season the [[Meat|meat]] with a little [[Salt|salt]], add the [[Onions|onions]] back to the pan and pour in the [[Tomato|tomato]] mixture.  I added just a few tablespoons of water at this stage as it looked as though it would not survive an hour of simmering.\n| [[Simmer]] gently for about an hour.\n| After an hour, add the [[Vinegar|vinegar]], [[Sugar|sugar]] and a good grind of [[Black pepper|black pepper]] then cook for the final 15 minutes.\n| Chop the [[Basil|basil]] and add just before serving.\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Agnello in agrodolce simmering.jpg|Agnello in agrodolce, simmering\nImage:Agnello in agrodolce, the ingredients.jpg|Agnello in agrodolce, the ingredients\n</gallery>\n===Variations===\nTry this with [[Duck|duck]] or [[Rabbit|rabbit]].\n===Chef's notes===\nMaking this for 2 people, I used 350g of [[Lamb tenderloin|lamb shoulder fillet]], but kept the remaining ingredients the same. I reduced the simmering time to 30 minutes as it was nice tender fillet.\n===Serving suggestions===\nWhile [[Plain boiled rice|plain boiled rice]] is probably the thing to serve with this, it went really well with [[spaghetti]].\n==See also==\n* [[Sweet and sour recipes]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Lamb recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]][[Category:Boiled or simmered]][[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#lamb #oliveoil #onions #tomato #duck #cream #whitewinevinegar #spaghetti #tomatopaste #granulatedsugar #lambtenderloin </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }

Saw this idea in a Gordon Ramsey Sunday Dinners TV program and as we always make our [[French fries]] in an [[Air Fryer|air fryer]], this was a no-brainer.\n\nA full bulb of [[Garlic|garlic]] sliced in half is plenty - wrap the other half in [[Cling Film|cling film]] for the next time!\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| Half a bulb of [[Garlic|garlic]] - sliced sideways to reveal all the [[Cloves|cloves]]\n| 4 medium sized [[Potatoes|potatoes]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| Pinch of [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| Pinch of [[Ground black pepper|ground black pepper]]\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Peel the [[Potatoes|potatoes]]\n| Cut them into [[French fries]] - we use a [[Sopito Stainless Steel Potato Cutter]]\n| Rinse the [[Chips|chips]] well under running water\n| Leave them soaking in [[Salted|salted]] water until you are ready to cook them\n| [[Dry]] the [[Potato chips|potato chips]] in a [[Tea-towel|tea-towel]] or a [[Salad spinner|salad spinner]]\n| Cook them at your [[Air Fryer|air fryer]]'s hottest temperature [200\u00b0 C / 220\u00b0] for 35 minutes or until golden.\n| Shake the [[Cloves|cloves]] out of the 'shell' of the [[Garlic|garlic]] bulb. Discard the shell and keep the golden [[Garlic cloves|garlic cloves]] to serve with the [[Chips|chips]] - Yum!\n}}\n\n\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Air fried garlic French fries chips.jpg|Cooked to perfection - don't waste the lovely garlic cloves!\nImage:Air fried garlic French fries ready to cook.jpg|Ready to cook\nImage:Kuhn Rikon Salad Spinner.jpg|Use a salad spinner to dry the French fries\nImage:Potato chipper.jpg|This comes highly recommended - [[Sopito Stainless Steel Potato Cutter][\n</gallery>\n\n===Chef's notes===\nThis time of year, locally we are limited to [[New Potatoes|new potatoes]] but in season, Cara, [[Markies]], Agria, Mozart and Maris Piper make the best [[Chips|chips]]. &#127839;&#127839;&#127839;\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:French recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Potato recipes]]\n[[Category:Air fried recipes]]\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:12032020'>#airfriedgarlicfrenchfries #chips #friedgarlic #garlicpotatoes #airfryer #garlicfrenchfries #dry #garlicfies</code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Here's a lovely recipe we had last night.\n\nWe bought a selection of vegetables on Saturday, divided them into three portions and have had Air fried roasted vegetables for the last two days.  I thought we should try something different for the last day, so I knocked this up.\n\nIn short, cut the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] into similar sized pieces ([[Butternut squash|butternut squash]] and [[Carrots|carrots]] take the longest time in the [[Air fryer|air fryer]] so you need to cut them thinly. [[Roast]] the vegetables for about 25 minutes, then pop the cooked [[Pasta|pasta]], [[Mozzarella|mozzarella]] and [[Ham|ham]] in for the final 5 minutes.  You might have to adjust the 25 minutes depending upon how you like your vegetables cooked and how thinly you sliced them.\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 1 tablespoon [[Chilli|chilli]] infused [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 1 small [[Red onion|red onion]], peeled and chopped into rings\n| A third of a [[Butternut squash|butternut squash]], peeled and cut into 10 mm square [[Chips|chips]]\n| 1 [[Courgette|courgette]] cut into 15 mm discs\n| 1 red or green [[Sweet Pepper|sweet pepper]], cored and cut into slices\n| 1 large [[Carrot|carrot]] cut into 10mm [[Chips|chips]]\n| 15 [[Cherry tomatoes|cherry tomatoes]] (whole)\n| 130g [[Dried pasta|dried pasta]] ([[Macaroni|macaroni]])\n| 4 [[Cloves of garlic|cloves of garlic]], peeled and chopped\n| Pinch each of [[Dried mixed herbs|dried mixed herbs]], [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| 100g sliced [[Ham|ham]]\n| 1 ball of [[Mozzarella cheese|mozzarella cheese]], torn into pieces\n}}\n\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Air fried roasted vegetables butternut squash cooker perfectly.jpg|Adding the pasta, ham and mozzarella\nImage:Air fried roasted vegetables - added to the Tefal air fryer.jpg|Vegetables added to the Tefal air fryer\nImage:Air fried roasted vegetables - the ingredients.jpg|thumb|The ingredients cut into similar sizes\n</gallery>\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Add the [[Olive oil|olive oil]], all of the [[Vegetables|vegetables]], slat, [[Pepper|pepper]] and [[Mixed herbs|mixed herbs]] to the [[Air fryer|air fryer]] pan\n| Toss to mix well and air [[Fry|fry]] for 20 to 25 minutes until the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] have softened a little.  Once you add the remaining items [[Whey|whey]] won't cook too much more.\n| Cook the [[Pasta|pasta]] so it's ready to add.  reserve a few tablespoons of the cooking liquid to add to the mixture if you need to loosen it\n| After 25 minutes add the [[Mozzarella|mozzarella]], [[Ham|ham]] and cooked [[Pasta|pasta]] and maybe a few tablespoons of the cooking water\n| Air [[Fry|fry]] for a further 5 minutes or until the [[Cheese|cheese]] has melted. Total cooking time is about 30 minutes.\n}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pasta recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Air fried recipes]]\n[[Category:Cookery cheats]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#vegetables #pasta #ham #chips #airfriedroastedvegetablesmozzarellahamandpasta #butternutsquash #airfryer #fry #oliveoil #mozzarella #carrot </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Since it is always made with chickpea flour, it naturally gluten free. In this recipe\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 605\n|PortionCalories = 302\n|DatePublished=17th October 2015\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = 2\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  1 hour, 40 minutes\n|PrepTime =  1 hour, 10 minutes\n|CookTime =  30 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Allergy free and gluten free sausage farinata with red onions and rosemary recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Didn't rise much for me?</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">3</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Looks as though it should really be like a Yorkshire pudding, but mine didn't rise at all. Help! </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>}}\n[[Image:Harrogate-pork-sausages.png|300px|thumb|right|[[Debbie and Andrew's Harrogate 97% Gluten Free Pork Sausages]]]]\nFarinata is a rustic Italian flat bread from Liguria. Since it is always made with chickpea flour, it naturally gluten free. In this recipe, [[debbie&andrew\u0092s sausages]] are added for extra flavour.\n\nFor a full Italianate experience, this should be called \"[[Farinata|farinata]] con salsiccia e cipolle rosse\".\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 100g of [[Chickpea flour|chickpea flour]]\n| 1&#8260;2 a teaspoon of [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| 260mls water\n| 2 [[debbie&andrew\u0092s Harrogate 97% Pork sausages]] with the meat removed and broken into chunks\n| 1&#8260;2 [[Red onion|red onion]] thinly sliced\n| 2 tablespoons of [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 2 sprigs of fresh [[Rosemary|rosemary]] (or the equivalent [[Dried|dried]])\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Preheat your [[Oven|oven]] to 200\u00b0 C (400\u00b0 F - gas 6), [fan oven 180\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Mix the [[Chickpea flour|chickpea flour]] with the [[Salt|salt]] and water. Whisk well to form a smooth [[Batter|batter]] and leave at room temperature for 1-4 hours for the [[Chickpea|chickpea]] to soak.\n| 2 Preheat [[Oven|oven]] to 200&#9702;C (fan)\n| 3 Close to the end of the soaking time, cook the sliced [[Onions|onions]] and a teaspoon of\n| [[Oil|oil]] in a [[Frying pan|frying pan]] on a moderate heat until softened (approx 12 mins). Remove the [[Onions|onions]] from the pan and then [[Fry|fry]] the [[Sausage meat|sausage meat]] until [[Browned|browned]] all over - (approx 4 mins)\n| 4 Take a deep sided [[Baking|baking]] pan about 22cm x 22cm and pour in 2 tablespoons of [[Olive oil|olive oil]]. Place in the [[Oven|oven]] for 3 mins to prepare for cooking the [[Farinata|farinata]]. Carefully remove from the oven and pour the [[Batter|batter]] into the hot pan, then evenly scatter over the [[Sausage meat|sausage meat]], [[Onions|onions]] and [[Rosemary|rosemary]]. Return the tray back into the oven and cook for 15 minutes till [[Brown|brown]] on top and firm to touch\n| Remove from [[Oven|oven]], allow to cool then cut into slices and serve\n}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Gluten free recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Debbie&andrew's sausage recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n{{Template:DebbieAndAndrew attribution}}\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#onions #sausagemeat #oliveoil #allergyfreeandglutenfreesausagefarinatawithredonionsandrosemary #batter #rosemary #farinata #chickpeaflour #baking #miseenplace #browned </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Not dissimilar to a sophisticated Slush Puppy.\n\nDelicious in small amounts but if you're a pig, it will make your head and teeth ache. I know from experience!\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 250 g [[Blanched|blanched]], peeled [[Almonds|almonds]].\n| 600 ml water.\n| 125 g [[Castor sugar|castor sugar]].\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add the [[Sugar|sugar]], water and [[Almonds|almonds]] to a [[Food processor|food processor]] with a metal blade and blitz until very smooth.\n| Strain this [[Almond|almond]] milk through a [[Jelly-bag|jelly-bag]] or a [[Cheesecloth|cheesecloth]] over a [[Sieve|sieve]]. Leave overnight to drip through.\n| Leave the resulting milk to cool in the [[Refrigerator|refrigerator]] for a few hours.\n| Place in your [[Ice-cream maker|ice-cream maker]] (60 minutes is perfect in our [[Ice-cream maker|Cuisinart model]]).\n| [[Freeze]] in an airtight [[Lock&Lock-type box]].\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nUsing an [[Ice-cream scoop]], scrape off any layers of ice-crystals and serve on a pre-chilled plate.\n\n{{Soft ice cream}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Ice-cream recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Sweets and desserts]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n[[Category:Frozen]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#almondgranita #almonds #granita #almond #frozen #freeze #cheesecloth #foodprocessor #sieve #blanched #dessert </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Artichokes, Olive and Roasted Pepper Trofie",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Artichokes, Olive and Roasted Pepper Trofie a cheese recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#pasta #oliveoil #artichokes #diced #fry #halloumi #chilli #preservedlemon #artichokesoliveandroastedpeppertrofie #peppers #avocado \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=An interesting way to combine halloumi cheese, artichokes, sundried peppers and trofie pasta\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2550\n|PortionCalories = 637\n|DatePublished=5th April 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 25 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 10 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Broad Beans with Preserved Lemon recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Lovely lemons</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Tangy and different</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Carla_Cancio-Bello,_J.D.,_on_behalf_of_Cuban_Cuisine_UK|Carla]] </span></span>\n}}\nAn interesting way to combine [[halloumi cheese]], [[artichokes]], sundried [[peppers]] and trofie [[pasta]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 315g trofie or other [[Dried|dried]] short [[Pasta|pasta]] - ([[Gallery of pasta types]])\n| 2 tablespoons of [[Olive oil|olive oil]] or [[Avocado|avocado]] [[Oil|oil]] \n| 1 x 250g pack [[Halloumi|halloumi]], cut into 1cm [[Dice|dice]] \n| A large handful of pitted [[Green olives|green olives]], halved \n| 1 red [[Chilli|chilli]], deseeded and finely [[Diced|diced]] (more or less to taste) \n| 1 x 280g jar [[Artichokes|artichokes]] hearts in [[Olive oil|olive oil]], drained and halved but reserving the [[Oil|oil]] \n| 1 x 280g jar [[Italian]] mixed [[Pepper|pepper]] [[Antipasto|antipasto]], drained \n| 1 [[Preserved lemon|preserved lemon]], [[Diced|diced]] and the pips discarded\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Bring a pan of lightly [[Salted|salted]] water to the [[Boil|boil]] and cook the [[Pasta|pasta]] according to the packet instructions, then drain, reserving 120 ml of the cooking water.\n| Meanwhile, heat the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] or [[Avocado|avocado]] [[Oil|oil]] in a wide [[Deep frying|deep frying]] pan, add the [[Halloumi|halloumi]] and [[Fry|fry]] over a moderate heat for 2-3 minutes or until golden [[Brown|brown]].\n| Add the [[Olives|olives]] and [[Chilli|chilli]] and [[Fry|fry]] until they sizzle, then add the [[Artichokes|artichokes]] and [[Peppers|peppers]] and warm through.\n| Add the still-hot [[Pasta|pasta]] to the pan with the reserved cooking water and the [[Preserved lemon|preserved lemon]].\n| Toss together, season to taste and divide among 4 warmed bowls. Drizzle on some of the reserved [[Oil|oil]] and serve.\n}}\n\n{{Template:Belazu attribution}}\n\n* [http://www.mybelazu.com/details/belazu-chargrilled-artichokes.html artichokes hearts in olive oil]\n* [http://www.mybelazu.com/details/belazu-sundried-duo-peppers.html Italian mixed pepper antipasto]\n* [http://www.mybelazu.com/details/belazu-pickled-lemons.html Belazu Preserved Lemon]\n==See also ==\n* [[Gallery of pasta types]]\n\n{{Template:YoutubePastaDough}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Belazu recipes]]\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Pasta recipes]]\n[[Category:Pasta salad recipes]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]][[Category:Grilled, griddled or barbecued]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#pasta #oliveoil #artichokes #diced #fry #halloumi #chilli #preservedlemon #artichokesoliveandroastedpeppertrofie #peppers #avocado </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Avocado oil bread (TM)",

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Avocado oil bread - A Thermomix recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#dough #avocadooil #oliveoil #dried #semolina #rocksalt #oregano #yeast #garlic #oliveoilbread #avocado \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This recipe is the same as that for Olive oil bread except that I have substituted avocado oil for olive oil and have adapted it for preparation in a\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1485\n|PortionCalories = 148\n|DatePublished=20th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 10 - Makes 1 loaf\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 2 hours 30 minutes\n |PrepTime = 2 hours plus overnight\n |CookTime = 30 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Avocado oil bread recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Different</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Turned out softer than I expected</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis recipe is the same as that for [[Olive oil bread]] except that I have substituted [[Avocado oil|avocado oil]] for [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and have adapted it for preparation in a [[Thermomix]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredientsTM\n| 15g fresh [[Yeast|yeast]] or 1x7g sachet of fast-action [[Dried yeast|dried yeast]] \n| 320g [[Sparkling mineral water|sparkling mineral water]] \n| 500g [[Strong white bread flour|strong white bread flour]] \n| 20g [[Semolina|semolina]] \n| 10g [[Salt|salt]] \n| 50g [[Avocado oil|avocado oil]] + 4 tablespoons, plus a little extra for greasing and [[Brushing|brushing]]\n| Coarse [[Rock|rock]] or [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] (I used Himalayan Pink [[Rock salt|rock salt]])\n| [[Dried]] or fresh [[Oregano|oregano]], to taste\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Place the [[Yeast|yeast]] and the water in the TM bowl and if using fresh yeast, allow it to dissolve in the water.\n| Add the [[Flour|flour]], [[Semolina|semolina]], [[Salt|salt]] and [[Avocado oil|avocado oil]] and mix for '''20 seconds / Speed 4'''.\n| Put on '''Knead''' setting for '''4 minutes'''.\n| Leave to rest until the [[Dough|dough]] is touching the '''MC'''.\n| Use a little [[Avocado oil|avocado oil]] to grease a bowl and turn out the [[Dough|dough]] onto a floured surface.\n| Shape the [[Dough|dough]] into a ball, place in the bowl and cover.\n| Leave until almost doubled in size and turn out the [[Dough|dough]].\n| Lightly [[Oil|oil]] a [[Pie dish|pie dish]] (see Tips/Hints below) and place the [[Dough|dough]] in the pie dish. \n| Drizzle the 4 tablespoons [[Avocado|avocado]] over the top and push the [[Dough|dough]] gently towards the sides of the dish. \n| Cover and leave to prove for 45 minutes. \n| Dimple the [[Dough|dough]] sporadically and prove for a further 30 minutes. \n| Meanwhile, preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 220\u00b0 C (425\u00b0 F - gas 7), [fan oven 200\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]. \n| Sprinkle the [[Dough|dough]] with the [[Oregano|oregano]] and coarse sea or [[Rock salt|rock salt]]. \n| [[Bake]] in the [[Oven|oven]] for 25-30 minutes. \n| Slide onto a wire rack and [[Brush|brush]] with a little more [[Olive oil|olive oil]] whilst still hot. \n| Allow to cool before cutting or tearing.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nThis is delicious on its own, no [[Butter|butter]] needed so very healthy! Good with [[Cheese|cheese]] and [[Salad|salad]]\n===Variations===\nYou can add other ingredients to it such as [[Herbs|herbs]], Crushed [[Garlic|garlic]] or [[Dried|dried]] [[Chilli flakes|chilli flakes]]. Also use different [[Oils|oils]] such as [[Olive oil|olive oil]], but make sure they have a fairly high smoke point. \n===Chef's notes===\nThe tin I used to make this bread is made by Falcon, It is an '''[http://www.amazon.co.uk/Falcon-Enamel-24cm-Oblong-Dish/dp/B000TAVXYI/ref=sr_1_3?ie=UTF8&qid=1310850610&sr=8-3 enamel pie dish]''' measuring 24cm and is just right for this bread. These dishes are easy to clean - if anything sticks, just soak in hot water for a short while. They are also very inexpensive. \n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#dough #avocadooil #oliveoil #dried #semolina #rocksalt #oregano #yeast #garlic #oliveoilbread #avocado </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Baked aubergines with tomatoes and Parmesan",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Baked aubergines with tomatoes and Parmesan a cheese recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#aubergines #tomatoes #bakedaubergineswithtomatoesandparmesan #tomato #cheese #aubergine #parmesan #bake #oliveoil #miseenplace #blackpepper \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=I decided to make an effort to become fond of the blighters by doing something a little different with them\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 199\n|PortionCalories = 49\n|DatePublished=18th January 2013\n|Author = JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime = 1 hour\n|PrepTime = 25 minutes\n|CookTime = 35 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Baked aubergines with tomatoes and Parmesan recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Nice one, Julia</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">My thoughts exactly.  I found aubergines dull unless grilled on a barbecue. This is lovely though.  Thank you!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nI don't really have any feelings about [[Aubergines|aubergines]] as they are tasteless.  However, I decided to make an effort to become fond of the blighters by doing something a little different with them.  Here is the result, which is based on an [[Italian]] influenced Nigel Slater recipe in his book ''Tender: Volume I, A cook and his vegetable patch'' (ISBN 0007248490).  I will certainly make this little dish again.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 2 large [[Aubergines|aubergines]], thickly sliced, but NOT peeled\n| [[Olive oil]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| [[Black pepper]], freshly [[Ground|ground]]\n| 1-2 bulbs [[Garlic, crushed|garlic, crushed]] or finely chopped\n| 2 or more hot [[Red chillies|red chillies]], finely chopped\n| 500 g [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], chopped\n| [[Parmesan cheese]], to taste, finely [[Grated|grated]]\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 220\u00b0 C (425\u00b0 F - gas 7), placing a shelf at the top of the oven.\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Place the [[Aubergine|aubergine]] slices on a [[baking tray]] so that they do not overlap - use more than one try if necessary.\n| [[Brush]] the slices with plenty of [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and lightly sprinkle the [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]] over them.\n| Turn them over and do the same to the other sides.\n| [[Bake]] at the top of the [[Oven|oven]] for about 25 minutes.\n| Meanwhile, heat a little [[Oil|oil]] in a pan, add the [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Chillies|chillies]] and quickly [[Fry|fry]], without them turning [[Brown|brown]].\n| Add the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] and cook until any liquid has almost evaporated and you have a thick sludge of [[Tomato|tomato]] mixture.\n| When the [[Aubergines|aubergines]] are ready spread the [[Tomato|tomato]] mixture over each slice.\n| Finally, sprinkle the [[Parmesan]] over each slice and [[Bake|bake]] for a further 10 minutes or until the [[Cheese|cheese]] has cooked.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Ciabatta|ciabatta]].\n===Chef's notes===\nIf you find that the skins of the [[Aubergines|aubergines]] are tough, just remove the skins as you eat the slices.  Do not peel them before cooking or the slices will lose their shape and become mushy.\n\nYou may find that you need more or less of the given [[Tomato|tomato]] quantity as it will depend on how juicy the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] are.  If they are fairly solid, you can use less.\n\nThe amount of [[Parmesan]] you use is up to you.  Just grate a reasonable quantity of it and see how much you can [[Pile|pile]] onto the [[Aubergine|aubergine]] slices.  Any left over [[Cheese|cheese]] can be kept in the [[Fridge|fridge]] in an airtight container.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Aubergines with tomatoes and parmesan]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Aubergines with tomatoes and parmesan]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes|Aubergines with tomatoes and parmesan]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes|Aubergines with tomatoes and parmesan]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes|Aubergines with tomatoes and parmesan]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes|Aubergines with tomatoes and parmesan]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Aubergines with tomatoes and parmesan]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Aubergines with tomatoes and parmesan]]\n[[Category:Starters|Aubergines with tomatoes and parmesan]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes|Aubergines with tomatoes and parmesan]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Aubergines with tomatoes and parmesan]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted|Aubergines with tomatoes and parmesan]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n{{Template:PottersDontEat}}\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#aubergines #tomatoes #bakedaubergineswithtomatoesandparmesan #tomato #cheese #aubergine #parmesan #bake #oliveoil #miseenplace #blackpepper </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Using [[Mushroom soup|mushroom soup]] is a  clever [[Cheat|cheat]] that takes all of the hard work out of this recipe.\n\nThis dish will serve from 2 to 6 people using the same basic ingredients, just add more [[prawns]] and [[basa]], you'll just have more sauce if you're feeding 2 people with it.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 1 small [[Onion|onion]], peeled and finely chopped\n| 1 tablespoon [[Butter|butter]]\n| 225 g (8 oz) peeled cooked [[Prawns|prawns]]\n| 2 tablespoons of [[Dry sherry|dry sherry]]\n| 1 can of [[Mushroom soup|mushroom soup]]\n| 4 [[Basa fillets|basa fillets]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| Freshly chopped [[Parsley|parsley]] to garnish\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 4), [fan [[Oven|oven]] 160\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Using a small pan or [[Wok|wok]],[[Saute|saute]] the [[Onions|onions]] in the [[Butter|butter]] over a gentle heat for 5 minutes.\n| Add the [[Sherry|sherry]] and [[Prawns|prawns]] for the last minute.\n| Mix in the [[Mushroom soup|mushroom soup]].\n| Pour a little of the [[Soup|soup]] mix into the bottom of an ovenproof dish, lay the fillets over the [[Sauce|sauce]] and cover with the remaining [[Sauce|sauce]].\n| Season and [[Bake|bake]] for 25 minutes.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[pasta]] or [[Plain boiled rice|plain boiled rice]] and garnish with [[Parsley|parsley]].\n===Variations===\nUse [[Cod|cod]], [[Basa|basa]], [[Sole|sole]] or any firm fleshed [[white fish]].\n\nI added a handful of chopped oyster mushrooms a the prawn stage to make this dish moor mushroomy!\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Freshwater fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Sea fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Shellfish recipes]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Student recipes]]\n[[Category:Cookery cheats]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#bakedbasafilletsinaprawnandmushroomsauce #mushroomsoup #prawns #sauce #butter #basafillets #basa #parsley #onion #pasta #drysherry </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Baked ribbon pasta with stilton, mushrooms, mozzarella and walnuts",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Baked ribbon pasta with stilton, mushrooms, mozzarella and walnuts\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#pasta #mushrooms #butter #egg #walnut #parsley #sauce #mozzarella #bake #doublecream #stilton\n|hashtagrev=12032020\n|description=A lovely stilton cheesy pasta dish with mushrooms, baked with melted mozzarella. A rather rich dish, but its nice to spoil yourself now and then.\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|DatePublished=20th November 2021\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  40 minutes\n|PrepTime =  10 minutes\n|CookTime =  30 minutes\n|TotalCalories = 1420\n|PortionCalories = 710 \n|Image = [[Image:Baked ribbon pasta with stilton, mushrooms and mozzarella cheeses recipe served.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">An October treat!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Perfect for the local walnuts that are everywhere at the moment</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Chef|Chef]] </span></span>\n}}\nA lovely [[Stilton|stilton]] cheesy [[Pasta|pasta]] dish with [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]], [[Baked|baked]] with melted [[Mozzarella|mozzarella]].  A rather rich dish, but it's nice to spoil yourself now and then.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 225 g fresh [[Egg|egg]] ribbon [[Pasta|pasta]]\n| [[Freshly ground black pepper]]\n| 1 teaspoon of [[Taste Sensation fajita seasoning]]\n| 18 g [[Butter|butter]]\n| 1 teaspoon of [[olive oil]]\n| 3 [[Garlic cloves|garlic cloves]]. peeled and crushed\n| 225 g sliced [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]]\n| 50 g [[Stilton cheese|stilton cheese]]\n| 60 ml [[Double Cream|double cream]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] \n| 1 fresh [[Egg|egg]], lightly beaten\n| 125 g ball of [[Mozzarella cheese|mozzarella cheese]]\n| 4 [[Walnut|walnut]] kernels, broken into small pieces\n| Freshly chopped [[Parsley|parsley]]\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Preheat your [[Oven|oven]] to 180\u00b0 C\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Cook the the ribbon [[Pasta|pasta]] for about 4 minutes in lightly [[Salted|salted]] [[Boiling|boiling]] water until [[Al-dente|al-dente]]\n| While that's cooking melt the [[Butter|butter]] together with a teaspoon of [[olive oil]], the [[Black pepper|black pepper]], [[Taste Sensation fajita seasoning]] and [[Saute|saute]] the [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]] for a few minutes until soft over a gentle heat so as not to burn the garlic\n| [[Crumble]] the [[Stilton|stilton]] over the [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]] and mix well\n| Add the [[Double Cream|double cream]] while stirring  and season to taste\n| Drain the [[Pasta|pasta]], reserving a the water if needed to thin the [[Sauce|sauce]].  See Chef's notes.\n| Mix the [[Pasta|pasta]] into the [[Mushroom|mushroom]] [[Sauce|sauce]] and stir in the beaten [[Egg|egg]]\n| Pour the mixture into a [[Butter|buttered]] ovenproof dish, top with the torn [[Mozzarella|mozzarella]] and cover with [[Tin foil|tin foil]] and [[Bake|bake]] for 15 minutes at 180\u00b0\n| Remove the [[Foil|foil]] and [[Bake|bake]] uncovered for a further 10 minutes until [[Browned|browned]]\n| Garnish with chopped [[Parsley|parsley]] and [[Walnut|walnut]] pieces\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Baked ribbon pasta with stilton, mushrooms and mozzarella cheeses baked.jpg|Baked, but a little dry\nImage:Baked ribbon pasta with stilton, mushrooms and mozzarella cheeses added.jpg|Mozzarella cheese topping added\nImage:Baked ribbon pasta with stilton, mushrooms and mozzarella cheeses ready to bake.jpg|Really should have used a smaller, deeper oven dish\nImage:Baked ribbon pasta with stilton, mushrooms pasta added.jpg|Creamy pasta and mushrooms\nImage:Baked ribbon pasta with stilton, mushrooms frying.jpg|Frying off the garlic and mushrooms\nImage:Baked ribbon pasta with stilton, mushrooms and mozzarella cheeses recipe ingredients.jpg|The ingredients for this lovely vegetarian dish\n</gallery>\n\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with a [[Green vegetable|green vegetable]]\n\n===Chef's notes===\nAfter making this, next time I would add a lot more of the pasta cooking liquid, probably 3 large serving spoon's worth.  After baking, even when covered with tin foil, it was quite dry.  I would also bake it in a smaller, deeper dish, so moisture is retained.  Very nice meal anyway and we will definitely be having this again.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Pasta recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Taste Sensation recipes]]\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:12032020'>#pasta #mushrooms #butter #egg #walnut #parsley #sauce #mozzarella #bake #doublecream #stilton</code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

and cover with the remaining ingredients\n| [[Bake]] for 30 minutes\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with slices of [[Lemon|lemon]] and a small [[Bitter|bitter]] leaf title": "Basic gnocchi recipe",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Basic gnocchi, an Italian recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#flour #potatoes #gnocchi #egg #boiling #simmer #mash #dough #boiledorsimmered #sauces #litres \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This dish is the basic recipe for making potato gnocchi to which you can add a sauces of your choice\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 635\n|PortionCalories = 158\n|DatePublished=12th April 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = Preparing gnocchi\n|Servings = Serves 4 as a [[starter]]\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime = 1 hour\n|PrepTime = 20 minutes \n|CookTime = 40 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Preparing gnocchi.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">I prefer pasta!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">3</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">A lot of work for an indifferent result - I much prefer home-made pasta to this.</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\n\nThis dish is the basic recipe for making potato gnocchi to which you can add a [[sauces]] of your choice.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 275 g (10 oz) [[potatoes]], ideally Desiree or King Edward\n| 1 [[egg]], beaten\n| 95 g (3&frac12; oz) [[plain flour]], sifted\n| [[Salt]] and [[freshly ground black pepper]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| In a large pan, cover the unpeeled [[potatoes]] with [[boiling]] water [[salted]] water\n| ([[Boiling]] in their skins prevents too much water being absorbed into the [[potatoes]] so try not to damage the skins)\n| Bring back to the [[boil]], cover and [[simmer]] for 25 minutes\n| Drain, pat dry on a tea-towel and allow to cool so they can be handled safely\n| Run the skins off and pass through a [[potato ricer]] or use a hand whisk to break up into a very fine [[mash]].  It's worth taking care over this you will have lumpy [[gnocchi]]\n| Add the sifted [[flour]] and half of the beaten [[egg]]\n| Knead with your hands to a soft [[dough]], correcting with extra [[egg]] or [[flour]] if too wet or dry\n| Transfer to a [[flour]]ed cutting board, dry and dust your hands with extra [[flour]]\n| Divide into four and roll each piece into a sausage about 1 cm (1/2\") diameter then cut into 2.5 cm (1\") sections\n| Using the times of a fork, press flat into each piece to make the [[sauce]]-holding pattern, the rougher the better, we want rustic!\n| Cover and chill until required\n| ([[Gnocchi]] does not keep well without discolouring so only make what you are going to use on the day)\n| Warm a serving dish in the oven\n| In a large pan, bring 4 [[litres]] (7 [[pints]]) of water to a [[simmer]]\n| Add the [[gnocchi]] and cook for 3 minutes, they will float after 2 but still need another minute\n| Drain, transfer to the warm serving dish\n| Drizzle your chosen sauce over the gnocchi and serve immediately\n}}\n{{Gnocchi-See also}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Pasta recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#flour #potatoes #gnocchi #egg #boiling #simmer #mash #dough #boiledorsimmered #sauces #litres </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }

title": "Basic risotto",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Basic risotto a cheese recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#basicrisotto #rice #stock #diced #parmesancheese #onions #celery #butter #garlic #fry #oliveoil \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This is a light adaptation of Jamie Oliver's basic risotto recipe from his book The Return of the Naked Chef\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2334\n|PortionCalories = 389\n|DatePublished=24th October 2012\n|Author = JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 6\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 45 minutes\n |PrepTime = 10 minutes\n |CookTime = 35 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Basic risotto recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Don't forget the Parmesan</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.4</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">..but don't add too much!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis is a light adaptation of Jamie Oliver's basic [[Risotto|risotto]] recipe from his book '''The Return of the Naked Chef''' (ISBN 0140292616)\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 60ml [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 2 medium [[Onions|onions]], finely [[Diced|diced]]\n| [[Garlic]] to taste, finely [[Diced|diced]]\n| &frac12; head of [[Celery|celery]], finely [[Diced|diced]]\n| 400g [[Arborio rice|arborio rice]]\n| 250ml [[Dry white wine|dry white wine]]\n| 1 litre hot [[Vegetable Stock|vegetable stock]]\n| Seasoning\n| 80g [[Butter|butter]]\n| 130g [[Parmesan cheese]], freshly [[Grated|grated]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a large saucepan and slowly [[Fry|fry]] the [[Onions|onions]], [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Celery|celery]] until soft.\n| Increase the heat add the [[Rice|rice]] and [[Fry|fry]], stirring constantly for about a minute until it looks slightly translucent.\n| Add the [[Wine|wine]], and still stirring, cook until it has been absorbed by the [[Rice|rice]].\n| Next, add a pinch of [[Salt|salt]] and add a ladle of the hot [[Stock|stock]].\n| Reduce the heat so that the liquid simmers quite vigorously, but does not [[Boil|boil]].\n| As the [[Rice|rice]] absorbs the [[Stock|stock]], keep adding more, a ladleful at a time, constantly stirring the rice gently.\n| When all the [[Stock|stock]] has been used and absorbed, the [[Rice|rice]] should be soft, but still be slightly [[Al dente|al dente]].\n| Remove from the heat and stir in the [[Butter|butter]] and the [[Parmesan]] and check seasoning.\n| Cover and leave to rest before serving.\n}}\n===Variations===\nThis is just a basic recipe.  You can add other ingredients of your choice to personalise it to you taste.\n===Chef's notes===\n[[Parmesan cheese]] is quite [[Salt|salt]]y, so do not be heavy handed with the salt.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Rice recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#basicrisotto #rice #stock #diced #parmesancheese #onions #celery #butter #garlic #fry #oliveoil </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }

title": "Basic risotto (TM)",
                "revisions": [

                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Basic risotto - A Thermomix recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#garlic #parmesancheese #onions #parmesan #oliveoil #butter #celery #wine #risotto #thermomix #stock \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This is Jamie Oliver's basic risotto recipe from his book The Return of the Naked Chef adapted for making in a Thermomix\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2222\n|PortionCalories = 370\n|DatePublished=12th January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 6\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 35 minutes\n |PrepTime = 10 minutes\n |CookTime = 25 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Basic risotto (TM).jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Love that I can make this in my Thermy</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">It makes cooking this so easy!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The&nbsp;Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis is Jamie Oliver's basic [[Risotto|risotto]] recipe from his book '''The Return of the Naked Chef''' (ISBN 0140292616) adapted for making in a [[Thermomix]]\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 130g [[Parmesan cheese]], cut into 4 or 5 pieces\n| 2 medium [[Onions|onions]], quartered\n| [[Garlic]] to taste, peeled\n| &frac12; head of [[Celery|celery]], each stick cut into 4\n| 60ml [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 400g [[Arborio rice|arborio rice]]\n| 250ml [[Dry white wine|dry white wine]]\n| 900ml hot [[Vegetable Stock|vegetable stock]]\n| 70g [[Butter|butter]]\n| Seasoning\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Grate the [[Parmesan]] by dropping it onto the running blades at '''Speed 8'''.\n| Tip out and reserve.\n| Add the [[onions]], [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[celery]] and process for a few seconds at '''Speed 4&frac12;''' until they are finely chopped.\n| Scrape down the sides with the spatula, add the [[olive oil]] and saut\u00e9 for '''20-25 minutes/Temp. Varoma/Speed 1/Reverse Blade Direction/Measuring Cup OFF '''. \n| Add the [[rice]] and cook for '''3 minutes/Temp. Varoma/Speed 1/Reverse Blade Direction/Measuring Cup OFF'''.\n| Pour in the [[wine]] and cook for '''2 minutes'''.\n| Add the [[stock]] and cook for '''15-17 minutes/100\u00b0/Speed Spoon/Reverse Blade Direction/Measuring Cup ON'''.\n| Add more water during the last few minutes of cooking time if it looks dry and taste to make sure it is 'al dente'.\n| If it looks too wet, cook with '''Measuring Cup OFF''' for the last few minutes.\n| Empty into a serving bowl\n| Add the [[Parmesan]], [[butter]] and seasoning and stir with the spatula.\n| Serve immediately\n}}\n===Variations===\nThis is just a basic recipe.  You can add other ingredients of your choice to personalise it to you taste.\n===Chef's notes===\n[[Parmesan cheese]] is quite [[Salt|salt]]y, so do not be heavy handed with the salt.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Risotto]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes|Risotto]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes|Risotto]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes|Risotto]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Risotto]]\n[[Category:Rice recipes|Risotto]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes|Risotto]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes|Risotto]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Risotto]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine|Risotto]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#garlic #parmesancheese #onions #parmesan #oliveoil #butter #celery #wine #risotto #thermomix #stock </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

from a large sprig of [[Thyme|thyme]]\n| 250 g [[Italian]] [[Risotto rice|risotto rice]]\n| 100g roll of [[Goats' cheese|goats' cheese]], crumbled\n| 80 g mixed [[Bitter|bitter]] [[Salad|salad]] [[Grated|grated]] [[Beetroot|beetroot]] to a pure\u00e9 in a [[food processor]] and keep the [[Grated|grated]] [[Beetroot|beetroot]] and the beetroot pure\u00e9 separate\n\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Make up the [[Stock|stock]] with [[Boiling|boiling]] water and keep it hot over a very low flame\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a large saucepan and add a allow it to become coated by the [[Oil|oil]]\n| Mix in the [[Grated|grated]] [[Beetroot|beetroot]] and half of the [[Thyme leaves|thyme leaves]]\n| Allow the [[Beetroot|beetroot]] to warm through\n| Start adding the hot [[Stock|stock]] to the [[Rice|rice]], 1 ladleful at a time.  Wait until the previous ladle of [[Stock|stock]] has been completely absorbed before adding the next ladleful.  This will take 25 to 35 minutes.\n| Keep the [[Rice|rice]] [[Simmering|simmering]] during this stage\n| When you are down to the last ladle of [[Stock|stock]], add it with the [[Beetroot|beetroot]] pure\u00e9 and ensure most of the liquid is absorbed into the [[Rice|rice]]\n| Stir in the [[Salad|salad]] leaves and half of the [[Goats' cheese|goats' cheese]], let the leaves wilt and the [[Cheese|cheese]] melt into the [[Rice|rice]], giving it a nice creamy finish\n| Spoon onto serving plates and dress with the remaining [[Goats' cheese|goats' cheese]] and [[Salad|salad]] leaves\n}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Rice recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#rice #beetroot #stock #grated #salad #onion #thymeleaves #vegetablestock #vegetarian #miseenplace #vegetable </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

yellow cornmeal]].\n| Preheat the [[Pizza stone|pizza stone]] under a very hot [[Grill|grill]].\n| With a deft move, slide the [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]] from the [[Pizza peel|pizza peel]], on to the [[Clove|clove]] of [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled and crushed\n| Sea [[Salt|salt]] and freshly ground [[Black pepper|black pepper]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Tear the [[Bread|bread]] up into a bowl and cover with cold water and leave to soak for 10 minutes\n| Squeeze out the water so it's soggy, but not [[Dripping|dripping]] wet!\n| Heat 3 tablespoons of [[Olive|olive]] [[Oil|oil]] in a saucepan, add the [[Borage|borage]] and heat gently until it wilts\n| Beat the [[Eggs|eggs]] together with the [[Parmesan]], the soaked [[Bread|bread]], [[Marjoram|marjoram]] and [[Garlic|garlic]].\n| Season with [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]].\n| Heat the remaining [[Oil|oil]] in a [[Frittata|frittata]] pan or a [[Frying|frying]] pan.\n| Pour in the mixture and pat down.\n| Cook gently for 15 to 20 minutes, turning so both sides are golden [[Brown|brown]].\n}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n{{OmeletteRecipes}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Frittata]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes|Frittata]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Frittata]]\n[[Category:Starters|Frittata]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes|Frittata]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Frittata]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#borage #boragefrittata #bread #frittata #marjoram #garlic #parmesan #olive #eggs #dripping #cheese </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Any type of long [[Pasta|pasta]] would work well.\n\n{{Template:YoutubePastaDough}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Pasta recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]][[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#pasta #garlic #chilliflakes #chilli #spaghetti #parsley #boiling #oliveoil #salted #panfried #chives </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

cup] [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]]\n| 45 ml [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 50g [2 oz] spicy [[Italian sausage]], blitzed in a [[Food processor|food processor]] with a metal blade\n| 2 [[Hard-boiled eggs|hard-boiled eggs]], shelled and halved\n| 1 small [[Onion|onion]], finely chopped and mixed in with the [[Sausage meat|sausage meat]]\n| 50g [2oz / &#188; cup] [[Ricotta cheese]] \n| 75g [[Mozzarella cheese]], finely chopped\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Make the [[Dough|dough]] as instructed and allow to rise for 30 minutes\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] and [[Pizza stone|pizza stone]] to 200\u00b0 C (400\u00b0 F - gas 6), [fan [[Oven|oven]] 180\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Knock the [[Dough|dough]] back\n| Dust a work-surface with fine [[Fine yellow cornmeal|fine yellow cornmeal]] and roll out into two circles, about 20 cm [8\"] diameter\n| Sprinkle half of the [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]] over each [[Pizza|pizza]] base and drizzle with half of the [[Oil|oil]] over each [[Pizza|pizza]]\n| Sprinkle half of the of the spicy [[Sausage|sausage]] / [[Onion|onion]] mix over each [[Pizza|pizza]]\n| mix the [[Mozzarella]] [[Ricotta cheese]] together and spread on one half of each [[Pizza|pizza]]\n| Place the [[Hard-boiled egg|hard-boiled egg]] halves on one side of the [[Pizza|pizza]] base (so it can be folded without drama!)\n| Fold the [[Pizza|pizza]] over and pinch the edges together, rolling the seal over as you go\n| [[Brush]] with a little water and [[Bake|bake]] for 15 to 20 minutes until golden\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with fresh [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] and a [[Green salad|green salad]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Pizza recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#pizza #calzoneripienoalforno #breadcrumbs #fineyellowcornmeal #onion #dough #ricottacheese #bake #miseenplace #pizzastone #italiansausage </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

We use our local Russells steak burgers but any good quality \u00bc pounder burger will work..\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n\n{{recipesummary\n|DatePublished=25th September 2022\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime =  25 minutes\n|PrepTime =  10 minutes\n|CookTime =  15 minutes\n|TotalCalories = 1852\n|PortionCalories = 926\n|Image = [[Image:Cambozola mushroom burgers recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Love Cambozola</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Especially as it doesn't melt too much, like some cheeses</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Cambozola mushroom burgers ready to cook.jpg|thumb|right|Two mushroom burgers ready to air-fry. One burger lifted on one to show the preparation.]]\nA lovely easy recipe that's oddly different and very tasty.\n\nWe use our local butcher, [[Russell's Butchers of Upwell, Norfolk|Russell's]] steak burgers, but any good quality &#188; pounder [[Burger|burger]] will work well.\n\nThe orange pepper happened to be a left over so we added that for a little extra colour.\n\nWe cooked these in our [[Air-fryer|air-fryer]], but a [[Conventional oven|conventional oven]] will do just as well.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] & [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| 2 large [[Portobello mushrooms|portobello mushrooms]], stems removed\n| 1 medium [[Red onion|red onion]], finely chopped\n| 1 large [[Clove|clove]] of [[Garlic|garlic]], finely chopped\n| 1 teaspoon [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 2 50g slices of [[Cambozola cheese|cambozola cheese]]\n| 2 &#188; pounder [[Beef burgers|beef burgers]] or preferably 2 [[Russell's of Upwell steakburgers]]\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Preheat your [[Oven|oven]] to 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 4), [fan oven 160\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Chop the [[Onions|onions]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] very finely\n| Season with [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]]\n| Add the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and mix well\n| Remove the stems of the [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]] to make a little more room\n| Spoon the [[Onion|onion]] mix into the [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]]\n| Top each [[Mushroom|mushroom]] with a slice of cambozola\n| Pop a [[Beef burger|beef burger]] on top of each [[Mushroom|mushroom]]\n| [[Oven]] [[Bake|bake]] for about 15 minutes at 180\u00b0 C\n| Leave to [[Rest for|rest for]] 5 minutes then serve\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\n</gallery>\n\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with curly fries, [[Onion|onion]] rings and [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n===Variations===\nUse [[Stilton cheese|stilton cheese]] for a nice change\n===See also===\n* [[Russell's Butchers of Upwell, Norfolk]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Beef recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Air fried recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:12032020'>#cambozolamushroomburgers #mushroom #oliveoil #onion #garlic #mushrooms #onions #bake #tomatoes #beefburger #burger</code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Cheese pasta recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#flour #cheesepasta #eggs #egg #dough #pastarecipe #foodprocessor #kneadingbread #rollingpin #maturecheesepowder #plainflour \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Handmade cheese pasta from just flour, eggs and mature cheese powder\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 133\n|PortionCalories = 67\n|DatePublished=22nd July 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = Blended until 'rice-like'\n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime = 20 minutes plus 30 minutes drying time\n|PrepTime = 15 minutes\n|CookTime = 5 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:RecipeFresh pasta.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Wow - Spookily good \ud83d\udc7d</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\">\n\n<span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Uncannily cheesy \ud83d\udc7b</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Artisan pasta.jpg|thumb|right|300px|'Artisan pasta' - roll out and slash into strips with a knife.  Thank you Jamie.]]\n</div>\nThis is basically our tried and tested [[pasta recipe]] using the fabulous [[Taste Sensation Well Matured Cheese Powder]] to give a lovely cheesy tang.  Unlike using grated cheese, the powder mixes perfectly into the pasta dough.\n\nIt's easier with a pasta machine, but by no means impossible without.  Use Jamie Oliver's trick, with a [[rolling pin]], roll the pasta into a few sheets at the thickness you require, then slice into rustic strips with a knife. Simple.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 100 g [[Italian grade 'OO' flour]] or [[plain flour]]\n| 1 whole [[:Category:Egg recipes|free range egg]]\n| 1 [[:Category:Egg recipes|free range egg yolk]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add all of the [[flour]] and 2 tablespoons of [[Mature cheese powder]] into a [[food processor]] and give it a whizz\n| Add the whole [[egg]] and the [[yolk]] and blitz it until it resembles rice grains, about 2 minutes or so\n| If it turns floury add a tiny drop of water\n| Likewise, if it stays as wet [[dough]], add a little more [[flour]]\n| Once it's rice-like, knock out onto a lightly dusted worktop and [[Kneading bread|knead]] into a ball, place in a bowl and cover with a dampened tea-towel for an hour or so\n| Divide into 3 or 4 balls, placing unused balls back in the covered bowl\n| With a rolling pin, roughly roll out each ball so it fits into your pasta machine, and  repeatedly run through the machine, from the thickest setting, to the final thickness\n| It's useful if you can hang the pasta over a skewer until it's ready to use or it tends to stick together\n| In the biggest pan you have (10 pints water / 1 lb pasta) bring water with a pinch of [[salt]], to the boil - no oil required\n| Once on a rolling boil, add the pasta, a quick stir with a chop-stick or long spoon to prevent sticking\n| The texture you should be aiming for is [[al-dente]] - a little resistance when you bite; rabbit like! This only takes a few minutes with fresh pasta\n| Once [[al-dente]], remove, drain and serve\n}}\n===By weight: ratio of [[flour]] to [[eggs]]===\nTo calculate the exact amount of [[eggs]] to [[flour]], by weight, use 3 parts [[flour]] to 2 parts [[egg]].  To make a rich ''Royal pasta dough'', use only the egg yolks, reserving a little of the white should you need to moisten the dough a little.\n\nIf using this method, weigh the eggs first and then multiply that by 1.5 to calculate the amount of flour you will need.\n===Variations===\n\nTo make whole wheat pasta use three quarters of durum wheat flour and one quarter of chickpea flour with a little bit of water and olive oil, no eggs. \n\nWhole wheat flour and spelt flour can be used as well, always with a little bit of water and oil. Once you have done the dough, leave it in the fridge for half an hour: it will be easier to roll it out. Follow instruction above. Whole wheat pasta has a slightly harder texture and it's ideal for [[Pasta e fagioli|pasta e fagioli]].\n===Drying hand-made pasta===\nSince this recipe was written, I've found a far easier way to dry hand rolled pasta, especially if you're just going to rustically hand cut it.  Shake a generous amount of [[fine yellow cornmeal]] onto a work surface and lay the pasta sheets on the cornmeal once it has been rolled out to your desired thickness. Leave it an hour or more to dry out and then you can then cut it to any shape you want.  The cornmeal prevents it from sticking to the work surface and unlike flour, most of the cornmeal falls off as you handle the pasta.  What doesn't fall off, separates during the boiling process.\n\n===Dried pasta===\nDried pasta is fresh pasta that has been air dried to remove all moisture.  Most dried pasta is not made with egg so will keep for years.  If pasta has been made with egg it will only keep for a few days and should be refrigerated whilst it is being stored.\n===Cooked rice and food safety===\nCooked pasta and cooked rice is a primary source of [[bacillus cereus food poisoning]]. Once pasta or rice is cooked it should be promptly consumed or kept hot (over 60\u00b0C [140\u00b0F]) or refrigerated (below 4\u00b0C [40\u00b0F]).  It must not be left at room temperature.\n== How much does one cup of pasta weigh? ==\n\n''Estimated [[Generic_conversion_table#Volume|US cup]] to weight equivalents:''\n\n<table border=\"0\" cellpadding=\"2\" width=\"500\">\n\n  <tr>\n\n    <td colspan=\"2\"><strong>Ingredient</strong></td>\n\n    <td><strong>US Cups </strong></td>\n\n    <td><strong>Grams</strong></td>\n\n    <td><strong>Ounces</strong></td>\n\n  </tr>\n\n    \n\n  <tr>\n\n    <td>Pasta</td>\n\n    <td>short cut - dry</td>\n\n    <td><div align=\"center\">1</div></td>\n\n    <td>100 grams</td>\n\n    <td>4 ounces</td>\n\n  </tr>\n\n    \n\n  <tr>\n\n    <td>Pasta</td>\n\n    <td>short cut - cooked</td>\n\n    <td><div align=\"center\">1</div></td>\n\n    <td>200 grams</td>\n\n    <td>7 ounces</td>\n\n  </tr>\n</table>\n\n'''Conversion notes:'''<br />\n\nEvery [[ingredient]] has a cups to ounces or grams conversion table.                         "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Cheese polenta, an Italian recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#polenta #cornmeal #boil #parmesan #refrigerate #cheesepolentarecipe #cheese #fry #bake #boiling #brush \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Polenta is very easy to cook, if you can boil water and put ingredients in a saucepan, you can make this\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1930\n|PortionCalories = 482\n|DatePublished=23rd October 2012\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = Fried polenta stars\n |Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 40 minutes plus chilling time\n |PrepTime = 5 minutes\n |CookTime = 35 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Fried polenta recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Not cheesy enough for me</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">More cheeese Grommit!</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Baked polenta recipe.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Baked polenta]]\n[[Polenta]] is very easy to cook, if you can [[Boil|boil]] water and put ingredients in a saucepan, you can make this. However, it requires constant stirring, so make it on a cool day when you need to be by the stove 30 minutes continuously.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 cup [[Cornmeal|cornmeal]]\n| 1 cup cold water\n| 1 teaspoon [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| 3 cups [[Boiling|boiling]] water\n| 1 cup of mature [[cheese]], grated. [[Parmesan]] or [[Cheddar]] are ideal.\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Combine the cold water, [[Cornmeal|cornmeal]] and [[Salt|salt]] in a bowl. Mix well.\n| A the remaining 3 cups of water to a pan and bring to the [[Boil|boil]]\n| Mix in the [[Cornmeal|cornmeal]], bring to the [[Boil|boil]]\n| Reduce the heat, stir in the cheese and [[Simmer|simmer]] for 30 minutes or until it thickens, stirring often.\n| Scoop the mixture into a greased loaf tin or suitable container and [[Refrigerate|refrigerate]] for 4 hours before serving. A plastic [[Lock & Lock]] container is good for this.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nCut the 'loaf' into slices, [[brush]] or [[spray]] with [[olive oil]] then [[Fry|fry]] or [[bake]] until golden brown.\n\nServe as a [[Mashed|mashed]]-[[Potato|potato]] substitute.\n===Chef's notes===\nInstant [[Polenta|polenta]] may take less time - Please follow the manufacturers instructions.\n==See also==\n* [[Polenta]]\n* [[Barbecued polenta and sweetcorn patties]]\n* [[Polenta and sweetcorn patties]]\n* [[Basic polenta recipe]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]][[Category:Pan fried]][[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#polenta #cornmeal #boil #parmesan #refrigerate #cheesepolentarecipe #cheese #fry #bake #boiling #brush </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

[[Dried|dried]] dill will do at a push\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]], [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| [[Juice]] from half a [[Lemon|lemon]]\n| 1 [[Egg|egg]], beaten\n}}\n====for the sauce====\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 200 ml [[Double Cream|double cream]]\n| 2 teaspoons of [[Dijon Mustard|dijon mustard]]\n| The [[Zest|zest]] from half a [[Lemon|lemon]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]], [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| A tablespoon of [[Capers|capers]]\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Preheat your [[Oven|oven]] to 200\u00b0 C (400\u00b0 F - gas 6), [fan oven 180\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Lay out your sheets of [[Puff pastry|puff pastry]] (or roll it out)\n| Pop the [[Fish|fish]] slices into a bowl, sprinkle with [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]] and season with [[Salt|salt]] and [[Black pepper|black pepper]].\n| Allow to [[Marinate|marinate]] for 30 minutes.\n| Sprinkle the insides of the [[Puff pastry|puff pastry]] with [[Panko]] [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]] and lay the [[Fish|fish]] fillets on top.\n| Coat with [[Mustard|mustard]] and then sprinkle with [[Grated|grated]] [[:Category:D\u017eiugas cheese recipes|D\u017eiugas cheese]].\n| Fold the [[Pastry|pastry]] up and pinch the edges to make a good seal.\n| Cut a slot in the top of the [[Pastry|pastry]] so [[Steam|steam]] can escape.\n| [[Brush]] with the beaten [[Egg|egg]].\n| [[Bake]] on a non-stick [[Baking tray|baking tray]] at 200\u00b0 C for 15 minutes then reduce the heat to 160\u00b0 C (325\u00b0 F - gas 3), [fan [[Oven|oven]] 140\u00b0 C] and bake for a further 15 minutes or until nicely [[Browned|browned]].\n}}\n====sauce====\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add the [[Cream|cream]] to a small pan together with the [[Zest|zest]] from half a [[Lemon|lemon]], season with [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]] and gently [[Simmer|simmer]].\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe the [[Fish|fish]] pasties with the creamy [[Sauce|sauce]] and sprinkle with [[Capers|capers]].\n===Variations===\nFor a nice change (and an economical one) try using [[Basa fillets|basa fillets]] instead of [[Cod|cod]].\n\nIf you can't get [[D\u017eiugas cheese]], try Parmesan cheese, it's quite similar.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:French recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Sea fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Pies tarts and flans]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:D\u017eiugas cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#puffpastry #fish #lemon #cheesycodbitesinpuffpastryparcels #dijonmustard #zest #grated #panko #pastry #cod #breadcrumbs </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Butter cream and shallots.\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|DatePublished=1st January 2023\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime =  35 minutes\n|PrepTime =  10 minutes\n|CookTime =  25 minutes\n|TotalCalories = 1120\n|PortionCalories = 560\n|Image = [[Image:Chicken and shallots in cream sherry and sherry vinegar.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Delicious</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Could have done with more of the lovely sauce though!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:NonLoggedInUser|NonLoggedInUser]] </span></span>\n}}\nA nice way to cook [[Chicken breasts|chicken breasts]], in what seems like a lot of [[Vinegar|vinegar]].  However it works very well, especially with the [[Shallots|shallots]].\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 2 medium sized [[Chicken breasts|chicken breasts]], bone and skin removed\n| 6 [[Shallots|shallots]], peeled and finely chopped\n| [[Freshly ground black pepper]]\n| 25 g [[Butter|butter]]\n| A splash of [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 110 ml [[Cream Sherry]]\n| 80 ml [[Sherry vinegar]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Dried|dried]] [[Parsley|parsley]]\n| 3 tablespoon [[Double Cream|double cream]]\n| Pinch of [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Flatten the [[Chicken breasts|chicken breasts]] by covering with [[Cling-film|cling-film]] and beating with a [[Rolling pin|rolling pin]] so they are of an even thickness\n| Heat the [[Butter|butter]] together with the [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]] in a heavy based [[Frying pan|frying pan]] and [[Brown|brown]] the [[Chicken breasts|chicken breasts]] on both sides - about 4 minutes\n| Reduce the heat to low, cover and cook for 15 minutes until properly cooked. Discard any condensed water, remove the chicken pieces and keep warm.\n| Add the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] to the same pan and gently saut\u00e9 the chopped [[Shallots|shallots]]\n| Pour the [[Vinegar|sherry vinegar]] and [[cream sherry]] over the cooked [[Shallots|shallots]], add the [[Parsley|parsley]], season with [[Salt|salt]] an [[Pepper|pepper]] and reduce by about half the amount\n| Allow the pan to cool a little so the cream does not seperate.                         "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Chicken liver vermicelli, Italian recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#chickenliververmicelli #butter #pasta #truffleoil #chickenlivers #drysherry #oliveoil #peas #freshpasta #parmesancheese #spaghetti \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This is a poor mans version of a recipe I saw Antonio Carluccio & Gennaro Contaldo make on TV yesterday\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2038\n|PortionCalories = 1019\n|DatePublished=21st March 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  20 minutes\n|PrepTime =  10 minutes\n|CookTime =  10 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Chicken liver vermicelli recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Not everyones 'Cup of Liver'!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.6</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">..But I'll eat it.  Lovely!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis is a poor mans version of a recipe I saw [[Celebrity_Chefs_on_Desert_Island_Discs#Antonio_Carluccio_-_broadcast_6th_July_2008|Antonio Carluccio]] & Gennaro Contaldo make on TV yesterday.  It was probably from the Two Greedy Italians series.  This is the way to eat chicken livers!\n\nUnfortunately I don't have any Piedmont [[Truffles|truffles]] to enliven the dish so we'll use [[Truffle oil|truffle oil]] and slices of mushroom instead.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 400g [[Chicken livers|chicken livers]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Butter|butter]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 1 medium [[Onion|onion]], finely chopped\n| 1 [[Clove|clove]] of [[Garlic, crushed|garlic, crushed]]\n| A small handful of [[Wild mushrooms|wild mushrooms]], sliced - see variations\n| 75 g frozen [[peas]], cooked for a few minutes in the [[microwave oven]].\n| A good splash of [[Dry sherry|dry sherry]]\n| 250 g [[Fresh pasta|fresh pasta]] (vermicelli, [[Spaghetti|spaghetti]] etc)\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| 1 teaspoon of [[truffle oil]]\n| 35 g freshly shaved [[Parmesan cheese|parmesan cheese]] to serve\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Trim the [[chicken livers]] of any veins etc and chop into sugar-cube sized chunks.  Rinse in a [[Colander|colander]] and pat dry with a [[Paper towel|paper towel]].\n| Cook the [[Pasta|pasta]] in plenty of [[Boiling|boiling]] [[Salted|salted]] water.  [[Fresh pasta]] will only take a few minutes and you'll see it change when it's ready - it just looks bigger and softer! Drain and reserve a few tablespoons of the cooking liquid.\n| Meanwhile melt the [[Butter|butter]] in a [[Frying pan|frying pan]], add a good grind of [[Black pepper|black pepper]] and add 1 tablespoon of [[Olive oil|olive oil]].\n| Add the chopped [[Onions|onions]] and sliced [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]] and saut\u00e9 for 2 or 3 minutes.\n| Add the chopped [[Liver|liver]], the [[peas]] and the [[Garlic|garlic]] and saut\u00e9  for about 3 minutes, stirring often.\n| [[Deglaze]] the pan with a splash of [[Dry sherry|dry sherry]] then stir in the [[Pasta|pasta]].\n| Add a knob of [[Butter|butter]], a teaspoon of [[truffle oil]] and two or three tablespoons of the water in which the [[Pasta|pasta]] was cooked, this helps to make a little sauce.  Mix well, season to taste and serve immediately.\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Chicken liver vermicelli_waiting pasta.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Ready for the pasta\nImage:Chicken liver vermicelli_ingredients.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Chicken liver vermicelli, the ingredients\n</gallery>\n\n===Serving suggestions===\nTop with shavings of [[Parmesan cheese]].\n===Recipe source===\n\n* Adapted from a recipe cooked by Antonio Carluccio & Gennaro Contaldo: Two Greedy Italians - BBC\n===Variations===\nTo add a little texture and flavour, I re hydrated a handful of [[Dried|dried]] [[Shiitake mushrooms|shitake mushrooms]] by soaking in [[Boiled|boiled]] water for 30 minutes, sliced them thinly and added them at the same time as the [[Chicken livers|chicken livers]].  Not very authentic, but it was all I had at the time.\n==See also==\n\n* [[Celebrity Chefs on Desert Island Discs]]#Antonio Carluccio - broadcast 6th July 2008\n\n{{Template:YoutubePastaDough}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pasta recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chickenliververmicelli #butter #pasta #truffleoil #chickenlivers #drysherry #oliveoil #peas #freshpasta #parmesancheese #spaghetti </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
