title": "Chicken margherita melt",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Chicken margherita melt recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#chickenmargheritamelt #oliveoil #springonions #roastpotatoes #egg #mexicanoregano #seeds #chickenbreasts #mozzarella #basilleaves #tortillas \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Anne usually take the 'easy way out' when it comes to cooking and gets ready-meals. She loved this so much she asked me to reproduce it\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 954\n|PortionCalories = 477\n|DatePublished=24th October 2014\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  2 hours, 20 minutes\n|PrepTime =  2 hours\n|CookTime =  20 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Chicken margherita melt recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">A sort of one-handed pizza</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">This looks great and tastes as good as any pizza.  And you can eat it with one hand!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n\nWhile I'm away, Anne, my partner usually take the 'easy way out' when it comes to cooking and gets ready-meals.  She was very taken with Morrison's [[Chicken]] margherita melt and asked if I could make it as she enjoyed it so much.\n\nThis is my attempt at reproducing a version of it.   The original ready meal came with [[Roast potatoes|roast potatoes]], but I think it would be nicer in flour or corn [[tortillas]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 2 [[Chicken breasts|chicken breasts]], skin removed\n| 2 tablespoons [[Balsamic vinegar|balsamic vinegar]]\n| 2 fat [[Cloves of Garlic, peeled and crushed|cloves of garlic, peeled and crushed]]\n| [[Salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| Half a teaspoon of [[Mexican oregano]] - Normal [[oregano]] is perfectly good, but not quite a strongly flavoured\n| 1 [[Egg|egg]], beaten\n| [[Flour]] for dredging - I love to use [[Masa Harina|masa harina]] or fine[[Yellow cornmeal|yellow cornmeal]] for this but [[plain flour]] is fine\n| 1 ball of [[Mozzarella cheese|mozzarella cheese]] thinly sliced\n}}\n'''[[Salsa|salsa]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 4 fresh [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n| 1 [[Clove|clove]] of [[Garlic, peeled and crushed|garlic, peeled and crushed]]\n| Small bunch of [[Spring onions|spring onions]]\n| Freshly picked [[Basil leaves|basil leaves]]\n| 1 small [[Red chilli|red chilli]], sliced, [[Seeds|seeds]] removed if preferred\n| 1 small [[Green Indian chilli|green indian chilli]], sliced, [[Seeds|seeds]] removed if preferred\n| [[Zest]] and [[Juice|juice]] of 1 [[Lime|lime]]\n| 2 tablespoons of [[Olive oil]]\n| [[Salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]]\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Flatten the [[chicken breasts]] by bashing them with a rolling pin between a sheet of [[greaseproof paper]]; [[Flattening chicken breasts, aka Jamie Oliver chicken bashing|see here for more detailed steps and a neat tip]]\n* Add the flattened chicken breasts to a [[Lock & Lock box]] together with [[salt]], [[Freshly ground black pepper|pepper]], [[crushed garlic]], [[balsamic vinegar]] and the [[Mexican oregano]]\n* Clip on the lid, shake like mad to mix the marinade and coat the chicken\n* Refrigerate for a few hours if possible\n* Prepare your grill so you can melt the [[mozzarella]] when you are ready to serve\n* Warm a serving platter\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Chicken margherita melt.jpg|Laid out on a flour tortilla, with a little sour cream too!\nImage:Chicken margherita melt not Jamie Oliver.jpg|Serve yourself!  Not up to Jamie Oliver's presentation standards but it worked well for us.\nImage:Chicken margherita melt out of the grill.jpg|Direct from grilling\nImage:Chicken margherita melt ready to grill.jpg|Ready to grill\nImage:Chicken margherita melt pan fried.jpg|Pan fried for 9 minutes\n</gallery>\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Prepare 3 plates, one with your dredging flour, one with the beaten [[egg]] and the last with [[breadcrumbs]]\n| Heat a large [[frying pan]] over a medium heat and add a few tablespoons or [[olive oil]]\n| Dredge both sides of the marinaded chicken in a saucer of your flour to coat.  This helps the beaten egg to stick to the meat \n| Dip the floured chicken in the beaten egg and then pull it through the breadcrumbs and pop them into the hot frying pan\n| Cook for 4 minutes on each side or until the chicken is properly cooked and pop them onto a paper towel\n| Slice the cooked chicken into 2.5 cm (1\") thick strips and place on a baking tray.  I've used a [[silicone baking mat]] as it's easier to clean and does not stick\n| Place the [[mozzarella]] on top of the cooked [[chicken]]  and grill until it's nice and gooey  \n}}\n'''salsa and tortillas'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Chop the [[tomatoes]] into eight slices\n| Slice the [[spring onions]] on the diagonal\n| Roughly tear the [[basil leaves]] into pieces to release their aromatics\n| Add these to a bowl together with the chopped [[chillies]], [[lime juice]] and [[zest]], [[olive oil]] and seasoning and mix well\n| Microwave the corn [[tortillas]] for 1 minute to warm them\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe the cheesey chicken from a hot platter and roll up the tortillas together with the salsa\n===Recipe source===\n* My variation on a Morrisons ready meal; Chicken Margherita melt\n===Variations===\nThis would be good with [[rice]], [[roast potatoes]], even as a filling for [[taco shells]].\n===Chef's notes===\nMy original choice was to serve this with pitta breads, that would probably have been a bit easier to eat and less messy than soft tortillas.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Grilled, griddled or barbecued]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chickenmargheritamelt #oliveoil #springonions #roastpotatoes #egg #mexicanoregano #seeds #chickenbreasts #mozzarella #basilleaves #tortillas </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Chicken pasta in a herby 6 vegetable ragu - Jamie Oliver 15 minute meals",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Chicken pasta in herby 6 vegetable ragu - Jamie Oliver recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#pasta #bacon #chicken #vegetables #oliveoil #chickenbreasts #carrot #cheese #pastasauce #leek #blackpepper \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Another of my takes on Jamie's 15 minute meals.  Keeping it fairly close to his original, except I'm using tagliatelle\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1172\n|PortionCalories = 293\n|DatePublished=11th October 2014\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = Topped with chicken, bacon, pine nuts, Mah\u00f3n-Menorca and a little parsley\n|Servings = 4\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  35 minutes\n|PrepTime =  15 minutes\n|CookTime =  20 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Jamie Oliver herby 6 vegetable ragu recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Your 5 a day fix</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.6</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">If you need your five a day, this will do it in one!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nAnother of my takes on Jamie's 15 minute meals.  Keeping it fairly close to his original, the only differences being that I'll use [[Tagliatelle|tagliatelle]], rather than wholewheat [[Fusilli|fusilli]] as I find fusilli quite a 'heavy' [[Pasta|pasta]], and the wholewheat version even more so.  I'll use my [[Home smoked bacon|home smoked bacon]] and some nice mature Mah\u00f3n-Menorca [[Cheese|cheese]] instead of [[Parmesan|parmesan]].\n\nI think you would be pushed to prep this meal in 15 minutes, let alone prep and cook.  Anyway, a brilliant meal and well worth making.  I've used 3 chicken breasts and this will stretch to 6 servings if your not too greedy.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n}}\n'''[[Pasta sauce|pasta sauce]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 1 [[Carrot|carrot]], trimmed and peeled - sorry Jamie, I have a little more time than you did!\n| 1 [[Leek|leek]], rinsed and trimmed\n| 1 [[Courgette|courgette]], topped and tailed\n| 1 red [[Sweet Pepper|sweet pepper]], deseeded\n| 2 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| 4 sprigs of freshly picked [[Thyme|thyme]]\n| 500 g [[Passata|passata]]\n}}\n'''[[Pasta|pasta]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 320 g [[Tagliatelle|tagliatelle]], smashed into small pieces so they don't remain as 'nests' \n| 2 [[Chicken breasts|chicken breasts]], skin removed\n| 4 rashers of [[Home smoked bacon|home smoked bacon]] or [[Pancetta|pancetta]]\n| 1 [[Green Indian chilli|green indian chilli]] [[Pepper|pepper]] (or to taste)\n| 4 [[Cloves of Garlic, peeled and crushed|cloves of garlic, peeled and crushed]]\n| 1 large [[Sprig of rosemary|sprig of rosemary]]\n| 2 freshly picked [[Bay leaves|bay leaves]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Pine nuts|pine nuts]]\n| [[Balsamic vinegar]]\n}}\n'''to serve'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 35 g Freshly [[Grated|grated]] Mah\u00f3n-Menorca [[Cheese|cheese]]\n| Finely chopped fresh [[parsley]]\n}}\n\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Jamie Oliver herby 6 vegetable ragu in passata.jpg|The [[rag\u00f9]], Vegetables cooked, passata added\nImage:Jamie Oliver herby 6 vegetable ragu chopped.jpg|Chopped vegetables ready to sweat down\nImage:Jamie Oliver herby 6 vegetable ragu ingredients.jpg|The vegetables, sliced lengthwise, ready for shredding\n</gallery>\n===Method===\n'''[[Pasta sauce|pasta sauce]]'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Quarter the [[Leek|leek]] lengthwise, keeping the past part uncut in order to feed through the [[Food processor|food processor]] easily\n| Slice the [[Celery|celery]] into four, lengthwise, leaving the leafy end uncut for the same reason\n| Peel, top and tail the [[Carrot|carrot]] and slice into 4 lengthwise, ditto with the [[Courgette|courgette]]\n| Cut the [[Pepper|pepper]] into strips\n| Feed all of the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] through a [[Food processor|food processor]] with a thin slicing cutter so they are all finely chopped, feed them through a second time if need be\n| Add the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and a grind of [[Black pepper|black pepper]] to an [[Iron|iron]] [[Casserole dish|casserole dish]] and heat over the [[Hob|hob]]\n| Add the [[Thyme leaves|thyme leaves]] picked from the sprig and the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] and pan-[[Fry|fry]] for 10 minutes stirring regularly\n| After the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] have been cooked, stir in the [[Passata|passata]] and [[Simmer|simmer]] gently\n}}\n'''[[Pasta|pasta]]'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Meanwhile cook the [[Pasta|pasta]] in [[Boiling|boiling]] [[Salted|salted]] water for about 6 minutes or  according to the packet instructions\n| Hammer the [[Chicken breasts|chicken breasts]] flat and cut into a 2 cm [[Dice|dice]]\n| Heat a tablespoon of [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and a grind of [[Black pepper|black pepper]] and the [[Sprig of rosemary|sprig of rosemary]] and the [[Bay leaves|bay leaves]] in a separate pan or [[Wok|wok]] and [[Stir-fry|stir-fry]] the [[Chicken|chicken]] until golden and properly cooked\n| Cut the [[Bacon|bacon]] into fine slices, crush the [[Garlic|garlic]] and finely chop the [[Chilli|chilli]]\n| Add these to the [[Chicken|chicken]] and [[Stir fry|stir fry]] with the [[Pine nuts|pine nuts]] until the [[Bacon|bacon]] is [[Browned|browned]]\n| Drain the [[Pasta|pasta]], reserving a little of the cooking [[Liquor|liquor]] to loosen the finished dish\n| Mix the [[Pasta|pasta]] and the [[Sauce|sauce]], adding a little of the [[Liquor|liquor]] to loosen it if needed\n| Scatter the [[Chicken|chicken]] and [[Bacon|bacon]] over the [[Pasta|pasta]] and garnish with finely grated [[Mah\u00f3n-Menorca cheese]] and a little chopped [[parsley]]\n| Serve!\n}}\n===Recipe source===\n\n* Based on a recipe seen on Jamie Oliver's 15 minute meals, but made more leisurely!\n\n{{Template:YoutubePastaDough}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian Perfect with pasta and a green vegetable like broccoli\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 914\n|PortionCalories = 457\n|DatePublished=20th January 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime =  25 minutes\n|PrepTime =  10 minutes\n|CookTime =  15 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Chicken piccata recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Yummmy!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">The are a really special kind of Chicken Fried Steak, only better!</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Chef|Jerry]] </span></span>\n}}\nA simple, yet truly delicious dish.  Perfect with [[Pasta|pasta]] and a [[Green vegetable|green vegetable]] like [[Broccoli|broccoli]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 2 boneless [[Chicken|chicken]] breasts, skin removed\n| 2 tablespoons [[Parmesan cheese]], [[Grated|grated]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Plain flour|plain flour]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Paprika|paprika]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Butter|butter]]\n| 140 ml [[White wine|white wine]] or [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]]\n| [[Juice]] and [[Zest|zest]] of 1 [[Lemon|lemon]]\n| 3 tablespoons [[Capers|capers]], rinsed and drained\n| 3 tablespoons of freshly chopped [[Parsley|parsley]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Butterfly the chicken breasts and hammer them to an even thickness of about 5mm (1/4\")- [[How to butterfly a chicken breast|''details here'']]\n| Season the [[Flour|flour]] with [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]] and [[Paprika|paprika]] and mix in all of the [[Grated|grated]] [[Parmesan cheese]]\n| Moisten the chicken pieces with a little water.\n| Dredge the [[Chicken|chicken]] pieces in the mixture and ensure they are well coated - leave for 5 minutes then dredge again.\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] and 1 tablespoon of [[Butter|butter]] in a large [[Frying pan|frying pan]], season with a grind of [[Pepper|pepper]] and [[Fry|fry]] the [[Chicken|chicken]] for about 3 minutes per side, ensuring they are properly cooked.\n| reserve and keep warm whilst you prepare the [[Sauce|sauce]].\n| [[Deglaze]] the pan with the [[Wine|wine]] or [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]]\n| Stir in the [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]] and [[Capers|capers]] then turn up the heat and reduce by about half.\n| Whisk the [[Butter|butter]] into the [[Sauce|sauce]].\n| Pour over the [[Chicken|chicken]] pieces and garnish with chopped [[Parsley|parsley]] and [[Lemon zest|lemon zest]].\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[pasta]] or [[Spaghetti|spaghetti]] and a [[Green vegetable|green vegetable]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chicken #butter #chickenpiccata #paprika #chickenstock #pasta #grated #parmesancheese #capers #sauce #parsley </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Chilli penne with cheese and garlic",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Chilli penne with cheese and garlic a cheese recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#pasta #garlic #butter #chillipennewithcheeseandgarlic #chilliflakes #cheese #oliveoil #fry #parsley #boil #chilli \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This is a pasta dish which is quick to make and contains some of my favourite ingredients\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2090\n|PortionCalories = 522\n|DatePublished=25th October 2012\n|Author = JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 20 minutes\n |PrepTime = 5 minutes\n |CookTime = 15 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Chilli penne with cheese and garlic recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Heavy pasta, penne</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">I always think it needs lots of sauce</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n\nThis is a [[Pasta|pasta]] dish which is quick to make and contains some of my favourite ingredients.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 400g penne\n| [[Garlic]] to taste, finely chopped\n| Red [[Chilli flakes|chilli flakes]] to taste, finely chopped\n| [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| A generous knob of [[Butter|butter]]\n| 125g [[Grana Padano cheese|Grana Padano cheese]], [[Grated|grated]]\n| [[Flat-leaved parsley]] to taste, chopped\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat a pan of lightly [[Salted|salted]] water until it is [[Boiling|boiling]].\n| Add the [[Pasta|pasta]] and [[Boil|boil]] for 10-12 minutes until the pasta is [[Al dente|al dente]].\n| Meanwhile, gently [[Fry|fry]] the [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Chilli flakes|chilli flakes]] in the [[Olive oil|olive oil]].\n| When the [[Pasta|pasta]] is cooked, drain into a [[Colander|colander]] and return it to the pan with the [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Chilli flakes|chilli flakes]], the [[Oil|oil]] in which they were [[Fried|fried]], the [[Butter|butter]] and the [[Cheese|cheese]].\n| Heat through until the [[Butter|butter]] has melted, stir in the [[Parsley|parsley]] and serve immediately.\n}}\n===Variations===\nYou can use any strongish, hard [[Cheese|cheese]] and vary the [[Pasta|pasta]] shapes.\n===Chef's notes===\nI made the mistake of buying '[[Chilli|chilli]]' penne from Asda.  Although it looks reddish, there is no heat in it whatsover.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Pasta recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#pasta #garlic #butter #chillipennewithcheeseandgarlic #chilliflakes #cheese #oliveoil #fry #parsley #boil #chilli </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Chocolate, fig and rum mattonella",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Chocolate, fig and rum mattonella recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#figs #cream #groundcinnamon #whippingcream #chocolatefigandrummattonella #butter #icingsugar #darkchocolate #dessert #foil #rum \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Mattonella (Italian for brick) is a chilled, Italian dessert which comes in many forms\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|DatePublished=24th November 2016\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 6\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  15 minutes\n|PrepTime =  15 minutes\n|CookTime = None\n|TotalCalories = 3559\n|PortionCalories = 593\n|Image = [[Image:Chocolate, fig and rum mattonella recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Yum\ud83d\ude0b, yum\ud83d\ude0b, yum\ud83d\ude0b</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Better than chocolate!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\nMattonella (Italian for 'brick') is a chilled, [[Italian]] [[Dessert|dessert]] which comes in many forms.  It is quite rich and it is often 'set' in a loaf tin to give it a brick shape.  This version with [[Figs|figs]], is particularly suitable at Christmas time.\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 100g [[Dried|dried]] [[Figs|figs]], stalks removed\n| 100ml [[Dark rum]] (or enough to cover the [[figs]])\n| 250g [[Dark chocolate|dark chocolate]], broken into small squares\n| 125g dark [[Sugar|sugar]]\n| 50g of [[Butter|butter]]\n| 100ml [[Whipping cream|whipping cream]]\n| 125g plain or spiced biscuits, coarsely chopped\n}}\n====To finish====\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 250ml [[Whipping cream|whipping cream]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Icing Sugar|icing sugar]]\n| [[Ground cinnamon]] or [[Cocoa|cocoa]]\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Place the [[Figs|figs]] in a bowl and add enough [[Rum|rum]] to cover (see '''Variations''' below)\n| Leave for at least 30 minutes to [[Marinate|marinate]].\n| Drain thoroughly, chop into small pieces and reserve.\n| In a fresh bowl, over a [[Saucepan|saucepan]] of water, melt the [[Chocolate|chocolate]] with the [[Sugar|sugar]] and [[Butter|butter]].\n| Remove from the heat, add the [[Cream|cream]], [[Figs|figs]] and biscuits.\n| Pour the mixture into a loaf tin which had been lined with [[Foil|foil]] or [[Bake-O-Glide]].\n| Smooth it out and [[Refrigerate|refrigerate]] for several hours.\n| Just before serving, cut the Mattonella into slices and put 2 slices on each plate.\n| Whip the [[Cream|cream]] with the [[Icing Sugar|icing sugar]] and pipe some shapes onto the plates.\n| Sprinkle the [[Cream|cream]] with a little [[Ground cinnamon|ground cinnamon]] or [[Cocoa powder|cocoa powder]].\n}}\n\n===Chef's notes===\nI used a 500g loaf tin with a volume of about 800ml.  This tin could have taken half the mixture quantity again.  A 250g tin was too small.\n===Recipe source===\n* Translated and lightly adapted from a recipe at [http://blog.giallozafferano.it/uovazuccheroefarina/mattonella-di-biscotti-e-cioccolato-con-fichi-e-rum-scuro/ Uova Zucchero e Farina]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Sweets and desserts]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Fruit recipes]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#figs #cream #groundcinnamon #whippingcream #chocolatefigandrummattonella #butter #icingsugar #darkchocolate #dessert #foil #rum </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Ciabatta bread recipe",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Ciabatta bread recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#dough #ciabattabreadrecipe #strongwhiteflour #yeast #driedyeast #warmplace #oliveoil #ciabatta #honey #starter #rest \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A recipe for making ciabatta bread from scratch.  Takes about 15 hours in all, but worth the wait.\n|og:image=https://www.cookipedia.co.uk/wiki/images/0/04/Ciabatta_bread_recipe_recipe.jpg\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1854\n|PortionCalories = 231\n|DatePublished=4th July 2016\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 8\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  15 hours, 20 minutes\n|PrepTime =  15 hours\n|CookTime =  20 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Ciabatta bread recipe recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Surprisingly good</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">I didn't think these would come out as well as they did.  They are like the real thing!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Ciabatta bread recipe loaves proving.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Loaves proving]]\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n\n[[Ciabatta]] (''carpet slipper'') because of its shape, is an [[Italian]] [[White bread|white bread]] made with [[Wheat flour|wheat flour]] and [[Yeast|yeast]]. The [[Dough|dough]] for this loaf is quite wet, hence the 'collapsed' shape.\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n}}\n====for the starter====\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| &#189; teaspoon [[Dried yeast|dried yeast]]\n| 150 ml tepid water\n| 3 tablespoons tepid [[Milk|milk]]\n| &#189; teaspoon [[Honey|honey]]\n| 150g [[Strong white flour|strong white flour]]\n}}\n====for the dough====\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| &#189; teaspoon [[Dried yeast|dried yeast]]\n| 350g [[Strong white flour|strong white flour]] \n| &#189; teaspoon [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 200 ml water\n| 1.5 teaspoons fine [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Make the [[Starter|starter]] first, bear in mind it will need to [[Rest|rest]] overnight in a [[Warm place|warm place]].\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n}}\n====Starter====\n{{RecipeMethod\n| In a very large bowl, sprinkle the [[Yeast|yeast]] into 150 ml of water mixed with 3 tablespoons of [[Milk|milk]].\n| Leave for 10 minutes then stir in the [[Honey|honey]]\n| Mix in 150 g of [[Strong white flour|strong white flour]] to make a fairly loose [[Batter|batter]]\n| Cover with a damp [[Tea-towel|tea-towel]] and leave in a [[Warm place|warm place]] for 12 hours\n}}\n====Dough====\n{{RecipeMethod\n| In a small bowl sprinkle &#189; teaspoon of [[Dried yeast|dried yeast]] into 240 ml of tepid water,  together with &#189; teaspoon of [[Olive oil|olive oil]]. Give it a quick stir then leave for 10 minutes to dissolve\n| Add this mixture to the large bowl together with 350 g of [[Strong white flour|strong white flour]] and 1.5 teaspoons of fine [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| Using a wooden spoon, beat this mixture for at least 5 minutes until fully combined\n| Use a silicone [[Spatula|spatula]] to collect the [[Dough|dough]] residue from the edge of the bowl, cover with a damp cloth and leave for 3 hours in a [[Warm place|warm place]] until doubled or trebled in size\n}}\n====Proving====\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Be very gentle at this stage as we don't to ''knock the [[Dough|dough]] down\n| Generously [[Flour|flour]] 2 [[Baking|baking]] sheets and have a small bowl with extra flour for your hands\n| Using a [[Dough|dough]] scraper divide the dough in two.  My dough was slightly too wet so it was easier to pour the dough onto the floured sheet.\n| Using well floured hands, shape the loaf by tucking the sides under themselves until you have the classic flat elongated shape.\n| Repeat with the second loaf\n| Preheat your [[Oven|oven]] to 220\u00b0 C (425\u00b0 F - gas 7), [fan oven 200\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n| Leave the loaves to [[Prove|prove]] for 30 minutes, during which time they will spread out more\n| [[Bake]] to 30 minutes in the middle of the pre-heated [[Oven|oven]].\n| Allow to cool on a wire rack.\n}}\n\n===Variations===\nIf using fresh [[Yeast|yeast]], use 2.5 g of fresh yeast for the [[Starter|starter]] and 2.5 g of fresh yeast for the [[Dough|dough]]\n==See also==\n\n* [[Ciabatta]]\n* [[Ciabatta with biga]]\n* [[Ciabatta_bread_(breadmaker_recipe)]]\n* [[Parmesan ciabatta]]\n==Chef's notes==\n'''Using a breadmaker:'''\nKneading this mixture with a wooden spoon was hard work to say the least.  The second time I made these, I transferred the dough mixture to our [[Panasonic SD-ZB2502 automatic breadmaker]] for the kneading process.  I set it to pitta bread (22) and let it run for 10 minutes, then switched it off and left for 3 hours to rise.  It was easy to ''pour'' the dough onto the baking sheets, using a knife to cut the dough.\n\n{{Template:Ciabatta bread recipes}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#dough #ciabattabreadrecipe #strongwhiteflour #yeast #driedyeast #warmplace #oliveoil #ciabatta #honey #starter #rest </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Oven baked ciabatta loaves with breadmaker dough\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#dough #bread #flour #breadmaker #bake #baking #driedyeast #warmplace #bakingtray #plainflour #oliveoil \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Raise the dough in the breadmaker (24 hours) and then bake in the oven to make two large loaves\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1098\n|PortionCalories = 549\n|DatePublished=4th October 2017\n|Author = Chef\n|Servings = 2 loaves\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 1 day, 2 hours\n |PrepTime = 1 day\n |CookTime = 20 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Ciabatta loaves with breadmaker dough and oven bake.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Just like the real thing</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.6</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Light and airy to0</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Sue_spins|Susie]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Ciabatta loaves with breadmaker dough and oven bake rising.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Waiting for the loaves to double in size]].\n\nThis [[Italian]] [[Bread|bread]] is made using two doughs.  The mixing and first rising are done in a Panasonic [[Breadmaker|breadmaker]].  The second rising and [[Baking|baking]] are not.  Start the day before you want to eat the bread.\n\nThis recipe is basically the same recipe as [[parmesan ciabatta]], but without the cheese! \n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n}}\n====1st [[Dough|dough]]====\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 1/8 teaspoon easy-[[Bake|bake]] [[Dried yeast|dried yeast]] [0.5 g]\n| 125g strong white [[Bread|bread]] [[Flour|flour]]\n| 105ml water [105g]\n}}\n====2nd [[Dough|dough]]====\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 1/2 a teaspoon of easy-[[Bake|bake]] [[Dried yeast|dried yeast]] [2 g]\n| 125g strong white [[Bread|bread]] [[Flour|flour]]\n| 115g [[Plain flour|plain flour]]\n| 1/2 a teaspoon  of [[Salt|salt]] \n| 1 tablespoon [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 30ml [[Milk|milk]] [30g]\n| 150ml water [150g]\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\nAn hour before you are ready to bake the loaves, preheat your oven to 220\u00b0 C (425\u00b0 F - gas 7), [fan oven 200\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour] and leave it at this temperature fr an hour before baking.\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n}}\n====Starter dough====\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add the ingredients for the first [[Dough|dough]] to the [[Breadmaker|breadmaker]] pan in the order in which they are given.\n| For Panasonic SD253 and most breadmakers, set to 'Basic [[Dough]]'. \n| For the [[Panasonic SD-ZB2502 automatic breadmaker]] set to menu option 16, basic dough.\n| When when the cycle has finished, switch off the machine and leave to rest at room temperature for about 18 hours.\n| ''I make this recipe alot and sometimes the breadmaker does not mix the starter dough properly.  This is because of the small amount of dough in the starter. If this happens I just use a spoon to stir in any unmixed flour and re-run the dough procedure a second time.  I've always had perfect results doing this.'' \n}}\n====Main dough (second rise)====\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add the ingredients for the second [[Dough|dough]] to first dough in the [[Breadmaker|breadmaker]] pan in the order in which they are given.\n| Set to 'French Dough' [[Panasonic SD-ZB2502 automatic breadmaker|Panasonic SD-ZB2502]]: option 21 - 3 hours 35 mins.\n| The [[dough]] should be quite sticky when finished.\n| Turn out onto a lightly floured [[Pastry mat|pastry mat]] or board and cut the [[Dough|dough]] into two.\n| Shape each piece into oblongs of about 25cm each on [[baking tray]]s or stones, which have been dusted with [[Flour|flour]] or [[Semolina|semolina]].\n| Cover with a damp [[Tea-towel|tea-towel]] and leave to rise in a [[warm place]] until the [[Dough|dough]] has doubled in size. ''My loaves puffed up to about twice the volume but the footprint stayed roughly the same size.'' \n}}\n====Baking====\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 220\u00b0 C (425\u00b0 F - gas 7) and keep it hot for one hour before [[Baking|baking]].\n| Shake the risen loaves onto a pre-heated [[oven tray]] or [[pizza stone]] and[[Bake]] the [[Bread|bread]] for about 20 minutes until golden brown.\n}}\n\n{{Template:Ciabatta bread recipes}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Parmesan ciabatta]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking|Parmesan ciabatta]]\n[[Category:Breadmaker recipes|Parmesan ciabatta]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes|Parmesan ciabatta]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes|Parmesan ciabatta]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Parmesan ciabatta]][[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#dough #bread #flour #breadmaker #bake #baking #driedyeast #warmplace #bakingtray #plainflour #oliveoil </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Ciabatta with biga",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Ciabatta with biga, Italian recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#dough #yeast #flour #biga #oliveoil #clingfilm #ciabattawithbiga #ciabatta #knead #bertinet #shiptonmill \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This ciabatta is based on a recipe by Richard Bertinet in his book Dough. Ciabatta flour can be obtained online from Shipton Mill\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2993\n|PortionCalories = 748\n|DatePublished=8th March 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = 4 ciabattas\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 1 day, 13 hours, 20 minutes\n |PrepTime = 1 day, 13 hours\n |CookTime = 20 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Ciabatta.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Lots of work</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Like most artisan breads, this takes lots of work.  Lovely to get the big airy holes is the rolls though.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Bags of ciabatta flour.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Shipton Mill ciabatta flour]]\nThis [[Ciabatta|ciabatta]] is based on a recipe by [[Bertinet|Richard Bertinet]] in his book '''Dough''' (ISBN 1856267628).  Ciabatta [[flour]] can be obtained online from [[Shipton Mill]].\n\n'''For the [[biga]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| &frac12; level teaspoon fresh [[Yeast|yeast]]\n| 180g sparkling mineral water\n| 350g ciabatta [[flour]]\n}}\n'''For the [[dough]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 10g fresh [[yeast]]\n| 340g sparkling mineral water\n| 50g [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 450g ciabatta [[Flour|flour]]\n| 15g [[Salt|salt]]\n| Extra [[Olive oil|olive oil]] for oiling\n| 20 g [[Semolina]] for dusting - optional\n}}\n===Method===\n\n\n'''The [[biga]]'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Dissolve the [[yeast]] in the water\n| Mix all the ingredients in a bowl by hand or in a mixer for 5 minutes until you have a stiff [[dough]].\n| Cover with [[clingfilm]] and leave it in a draught-free area for 24 hours.\n}}\n'''The [[dough]]'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Dissolve the [[Yeast|yeast]] in the water and then add [[Olive oil|olive oil]].\n| [[Sieve]] the [[Flour|flour]] and [[Salt|salt]] into a bowl and mix in the water, [[Yeast|yeast]] and [[Oil|oil]].\n| Then, add the [[Biga|biga]] and mix thoroughly.  (This is a very wet mixture so I would recommend using a mixer with a dough hook).\n| [[Knead]] using your chosen method.  (You can also do this using your food mixer on the second highest speed for 4-5 minutes).\n| [[Oil]] another large bowl and pour the [[Dough|dough]] into it.\n| Allow to rise in a [[warm place]] until it has a bubbly and light texture (about 1&frac12; hours), covering the bowl with [[clingfilm]].\n| Gently deflate the [[dough]] with floured fingers and repeat the previous step or leave in the fridge overnight.\n| If the dough has been in the fridge bring it to room temperature before continuing with the next step.\n| Generously flour your work surface and using your dough scraper turn out the [[dough]] in one piece.\n| Flour the top of the [[dough]] and using your fingers, gently dimple it.\n| Divide the [[dough]] into 4.\n| For each piece of [[dough]], fold one side of it into the middle and press down and seal with the heal of your hand.\n| Fold the other side unto the middle, pressing and sealing in the same manner.\n| Finally, fold in half lengthways and seal the edges so that you end up with a long shape.\n| Place the pieces of [[dough]] onto a couche cloth or piece of linen which has been floured with rye flour.\n| Make ruches in the cloth between each piece of [[dough]], to prevent them from spreading too much, but do allow a little spreading room.\n| Cover with tea towels and allow to prove for about 45 minutes.\n| Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to its highest temperature with a tray half-filled with boiling water placed on the bottom. If using a baking stone, put it in the oven before you turn the heat on.\n| Flour a baking tray or peel, pick up one ciabatta at a time, turn it over, stretching it lengthways a little at the same time and lay on the peel or tray.\n| Transfer to the oven, reduce the heat to 220\u00b0 C (425\u00b0 F - gas 7) and bake for about 20 minutes until light golden brown.\n| Allow to cool on wire racks.\n}}\n===Variations===\nSee also our recipes for [[Ciabatta bread|breadmaker ciabatta]] and [[Parmesan ciabatta]].\n===Chef's notes===\n[[Ciabatta]] [[Freeze|freeze]]s well.  Just reduce the initial [[Baking|baking]] time to 15 minutes, cool, freeze and [[Bake|bake]] for 15-20 minutes straight from [[Frozen|frozen]].\n{{Template:Ciabatta bread recipes}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]][[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#dough #yeast #flour #biga #oliveoil #clingfilm #ciabattawithbiga #ciabatta #knead #bertinet #shiptonmill </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }

title": "Coda alla vaccinara",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Coda alla vaccinara a beef recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#codaallavaccinara #oxtail #garlic #simmer #raisins #onion #parsley #wine #fat #celery #bouquetgarni \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Coda alla vaccinara is a speciality of Roman cuisine. It is a stew made with \"oxtail\" (in fact, usually tail of a calf) and various vegetables\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 8025\n|PortionCalories = 2006\n|DatePublished=19th January 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = Plated!\n |Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 3 hours 15 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 3 hours\n |Image = [[Image:Coda alla vaccinara - plated.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">A Winter Warmer</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.7</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">If you want a hearty meal for a miserable winter's evening, this is it!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nCoda alla vaccinara is a speciality of Roman cuisine. It is a [[Stew|stew]] made with \"[[Oxtail|oxtail]]\" (in fact, usually tail of a calf) and various [[Vegetables|vegetables]]. Its introduction [[Dates|dates]] back to times when it was customary to pay a vaccinaro ([[Cattle|cattle]] butcher) in kind with the entrails, hide, and tail of the animal. Butchers developed a way of turning their fee into a delicacy, thus coda alla vaccinara was formed. Today, almost every Roman household has its unique recipe to cook coda.\n\nTail of the [[Veal|veal]] is [[Parboiled|parboiled]] and then [[Simmered|simmered]] with large amounts of [[Celery|celery]], [[Carrots|carrots]], and aromatic [[Herbs|herbs]]. Following this, [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] and [[Wine|wine]] are added, then the mixture is cooked further with a soffritto of [[Onions|onions]], [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Prosciutto|prosciutto]], [[Pancetta|pancetta]] and some other ingredients. During the final phase of cooking, a [[Bouquet garni|bouquet garni]] of [[Bay leaves|bay leaves]], celery stalks, and [[Cloves|cloves]] are put in the pot for flavouring. Tail should be cooked such a long time that [[Meat|meat]] should be easily separated from the vertebrae. The meal is seasoned with [[Cinnamon|cinnamon]], [[Nutmeg|nutmeg]], and [[Black pepper|black pepper]] and garnished with [[Pine nuts|pine nuts]].\n\nAn important point is to obtain a sweet-and-sour taste. The most common way is to add [[Raisins|raisins]] although many people may prefer to use candied [[Fruits|fruits]] or sweetbitter [[Chocolate|chocolate]]. Coda should be cooked one or two days before it is served and be reheated. The leftover meal is never wasted since it may also be well employed as a delicious [[pasta]] sauce.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 kg (2.25 lb) [[Oxtail|oxtail]], sliced into pieces\n| 2 [[Carrots|carrots]], scrubbed, 1 quartered, the other sliced\n| 2 [[Onions|onions]], peeled, 1 chopped, 1 quartered\n| 1 [[Bouquet garni for beef|bouquet garni for beef]], take your pick!\n| 4 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 50 g [[Pork|pork]] [[Fat|fat]], smashed with a rolling pin\n| 1 clove of [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled and smashed under a knife\n| 175 ml (6 fl oz) [[Dry white wine|dry white wine]] or [[Sherry|sherry]]\n| 750 ml (1.25 [[Pints|pints]]) [[Passata di pomodoro|passata di pomodoro]] or canned plum [[tomatoes]], chopped.\n| 4 [[Celery hearts|celery hearts]], cut into moons\n| 200 ml [[Beef stock|beef stock]]\n| 75 g [[Raisins|raisins]]\n| A little nice vinegar (cider,sherry etc)\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| Chopped [[parsley]] to garnish\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| To a large pan of [[Boiling|boiling]] [[Salted|salted]] water, add the [[Oxtail|oxtail]], 1 quartered [[Carrot|carrot]], 1 quartered [[Onion|onion]], the [[Bouquet garni|bouquet garni]] and a grind of [[Pepper|pepper]]\n| Bring this back to the [[Boil|boil]] and then reduce the heat and [[Simmer|simmer]] for 1 hour\n| In large heavy [[frying pan]] or [[wok]], heat the [[Olive oil|olive oil]], [[Pork|pork]] [[Fat|fat]] and another grind of [[Pepper|pepper]]. Add the chopped [[Onion|onion]] and the smashed [[Garlic|garlic]].  Heat until the garlic starts to turns [[Brown|brown]], then once it has flavoured the [[Oil|oil]], remove and discard it, leaving the [[onion]] in the pan\n| Drain the [[Oxtail|oxtail]] and reserve the [[stock]] for use with another recipe, add to the [[Oil|oil]] and [[Brown|brown]] it on all sides\n| Pour in the [[Wine|wine]] or [[Sherry|sherry]], [[Deglaze|deglaze]] the pan, scraping any goodness from the bottom. Heat until the wine  evaporates\n| Add the [[Passata|passata]] and season to taste with [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]]\n| Transfer everything from the frying pan to a large, lidded pan, cover and [[Simmer]] gently for 1 hour\n| Add the chopped [[Carrot|carrot]], [[Celery|celery]] and [[Raisins|raisins]] and [[Simmer|simmer]] for another 45 minutes\n| Check the liquid levels at this stage as it can easily dry out. Add a little more water if needed.  Check for seasoning.  I found a little [[sherry vinegar]] added at this stage rounded the flavours nicely here.\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Coda alla vaccinara - leeks.jpg|thumb|300px|right|In with the leeks and carrots\nImage:Coda alla vaccinara - big cook.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Just before the 'big cook' at step 7\n</gallery>\n\n===Serving suggestion===\nOriginal recipe suggestion: Serve in soup bowls with crusty bread, garnished with chopped [[parsley]]\nMy serving suggestion: Serve with [[spaghetti]].  Delicious!\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Beef recipes|Oxtail]]\n[[Category:Stews and casseroles]]\n[[Category:Fruit recipes]]\n[[Category:Stewed, braised or pot roasted]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#codaallavaccinara #oxtail #garlic #simmer #raisins #onion #parsley #wine #fat #celery #bouquetgarni </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }

I wouldn't bother making this with instant coffee\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 193\n|PortionCalories = 16\n|DatePublished=12th April 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = Ice cream maker with built-in freezer\n |Servings = Servings: 12 - Makes about a litre of [[Coffee|coffee]] [[Granita|granita]]\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 2 hours 10 minutes\n |PrepTime = 2 hours 5 minutes\n |CookTime = 5 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Freezing Ice cream maker.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Mmmm</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Like a luxury ice-pole</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Granita]] is the classic Sicilian sorbet-type ice. If you have no other option than instant, then make it double strength.\n\nThis is basically a coffee and rum Slush Puppy!\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| &frac34; cup [[Granulated sugar|granulated sugar]]\n| 1.5 cups of water\n| 2.5 cups of strong [[Coffee|coffee]]\n| Splash of [[Rum|rum]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Mix the [[Sugar|sugar]] and water in a heavy pan, heat until the sugar dissolves.\n| [[Boil]] carefully for 5 minutes.\n| Remove from the heat, add the [[Coffee|coffee]] and mix well.\n| Allow to cool then [[Refrigerate|refrigerate]] until very cold.\n| Add a splash of [[rum]] at this stage.\n| Add to your [[Ice-cream maker|ice-cream maker]] and process as directed. About 1 hour should be fine for most machines.\n| [[Freeze]] in a Lock&Lock type box.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nTo serve, scrape the surface with an [[Ice-cream scoop]], scraping up the ice crystals.  Serve in small, chilled dishes.\n===Variations===\n[[Freeze]] in small amounts, like ice-trays and process to slush in a [[Food processor|food processor]] with a blade.  Serve immediately.\n\n{{Soft ice cream}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Ice-cream recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Frozen]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#coffee #rum #coffeegranita #granita #freeze #frozen #boil #refrigerate #foodprocessor #granulatedsugar </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Cook for 5 minutes, stirring often.\n| If you want to soften them a little more, add a few splashes of water and cook for a little longer.\n| Mix the [[Toasted|toasted]] [[Almonds|almonds]] and fresh [[Oregano|oregano]] back in, cook for a few minutes and serve\n}}\n{{Template:PeelingGinger}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Stir fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#courgetteswithalmondsandginger #almonds #grated #lemonjuice #oregano #oliveoil #courgettes #driedoregano #ginger #toasted #stirfried </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

It tastes like pasta and is gluten free!\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 263\n|PortionCalories = 131\n|DatePublished=18th August 2015\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  18 minutes\n|PrepTime =  8 minutes\n|CookTime =  10 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Courgette and garlic pasta recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Spiral pasta, that isn't!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Very healthy for you though.</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nAnother great way to use your home-grown [[Courgettes|courgettes]]. You could use a [[Food processor|food processor]] but the result would not be so aesthetically pleasing.\n\nI've included this in our pasta category, even though it contains no pasta.  It could possible be a gluten free pasta?\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 2 or 3 [[Courgettes|courgettes]], depending upon the size\n| 3 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| A good pinch of [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| 1 [[chile de arbol]]\n| 1 medium sized [[Red onion|red onion]], peeled and very finely chopped\n| 3 [[Cloves of Garlic, peeled and crushed|cloves of garlic, peeled and crushed]]\n| 30 g of [[Parmesan cheese|parmesan cheese]], [[Grated|grated]]\n| 80 g strong [[Cheese|cheese]] of your choice cut into shaving with a [[Speed peeler|speed peeler]]. garnish\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Using a [[Speed peeler|speed peeler]] or [[Mandoline|mandoline]], shave the [[Courgettes|courgettes]] into ribbons\n| Add a good pinch of [[Black pepper|black pepper]] and the (whole) chili to the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and heat in a large [[Frying pan|frying pan]] or [[Wok|wok]].\n| Add the chopped [[Red onion|red onion]] and [[Saute|saute]] for 3 or 4 minutes\n| Stir in the [[Crushed garlic|crushed garlic]] and before it gets a chance to colour, add the [[Courgette|courgette]] ribbons\n| [[Stir fry]] the [[Courgettes|courgettes]], turning often, until they are done to your liking\n| Discard the whole chili and add the shaving of strong [[Cheese|cheese]] to the pan stir well and serve immediately before the cheese melts too much\n| Place the warm [[Tomato sauce|tomato sauce]] on the plates and spoon the [[Courgette|courgette]] mixture over the top\n| Dress with [[Fresh herbs|fresh herbs]] and a good sprinkle of [[Parmesan cheese|parmesan cheese]]\n}}\n===Chef's notes===\nIf you don't have any decent tomato sauce to hand, take a little from a bottle of shop-bought bolognese sauce or similar and freeze the remainder in small portions for future use with similar recipes. \n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main                     {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Ricotta stuffed courgette tempura (zucchini) recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#plainflour #cornflour #blackpepper #deepfried #batter #lime #courgette #tempura #ricottacheese #lager #beer \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Courgette (zucchini) flowers filled with cream cheese in a crispy batter, probably not something you would have everyday, but nice for special occasions\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1481\n|PortionCalories = 370\n|DatePublished=24th December 2014\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  40 minutes\n|PrepTime =  20 minutes\n|CookTime =  20 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Courgette blossoms tempura recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Finding the flowers is hard!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Even here in the country, I find it almost impossible to but the flowers - I need to grow them myself I guess.</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Stuffed zucchini flowers.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Wooden cocktail sticks can be helpful to keep the flowers closed during frying]]\n[[Courgette]] ([[Zucchini|zucchini]]) flowers filled with [[Cream cheese|cream cheese]] and [[deep fried]] in a crispy [[tempura]] [[Batter|batter]] is probably not something you would have everyday, but very nice for special occasions.\n\n'''flowers and filling'''\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 8 [[Courgette|courgette]] flowers with baby [[Courgettes|courgettes]] still connected\n| 225g (8oz) [[Ricotta cheese|ricotta cheese]]\n| [[Zest|zest]] and [[Juice|juice]] of 1 [[Lime|lime]]\n| [[Sea salt]] and freshly ground [[black pepper]]\n| [[Plain flour|plain flour]] for dredging\n| [[Vegetable oil]] for [[Deep frying|deep frying]]\n}}\n'''for the [[Tempura|tempura]] [[Batter|batter]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 75g [[Plain flour|plain flour]]\n| 75g [[Cornflour|cornflour]]\n| \u00bd teaspoon [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| 188 ml [6.5 fl oz] [[Sparkling water|sparkling water]], [[Beer|beer]] or [[Lager|lager]]. Must be ice cold.\n| 1 [[Free range egg|free range egg]] - lightly beaten\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in either a [[Deep fat fryer|deep fat fryer]] or a large saucepan. If you are using a saucepan make sure the oil comes below halfway down the edge of the pan. If you have a [[Thermometer|thermometer]] it needs to reach 190C, but you can test that it\u0092s ready by dropping some [[Bread|bread]] into the oil and it should [[Brown|brown]] in 20 seconds.\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Mix the [[ricotta cheese]], [[lime]] juice and zest in a bowl and season with [[salt]] and [[black pepper]]\n| Spoon enough filling into each flower, leaving enough room to close the flowers.  A wooden [[cocktail stick]] is helpful to hold the flowers closed while frying. \n| Set the flowers aside and prepare the batter\n| Ensure the water is ice cold.\n| Sift the [[flour]], [[cornflour]] and [[salt]] together into a bowl. \n| Make a well in the centre of the flour and pour your chosen liquid together with the previously beaten egg into it.\n| Using a [[balloon whisk]], very gently combine ingredients into a rough batter.\n| It is very important that it is not overmixed at this stage as that will make the batter stodgy.\n| Once your batter is 'runny' enough to coat your chosen filling, stop mixing, even if this leaves the odd lump in the batter.\n| When you are ready to cook, dredge each flower in plain flour, dip into the batter and deep fry for 3.5 minutes\n| Leave on [[kitchen paper]] to drain excess oil \n| Cooked tempura can be kept warm in an oven at 150\u00b0 C (300\u00b0 F), with the door left ajar to keep it crispy.\n}}\n===Chef's notes===\nLumpy batter is good,  It ensures that you do not overwork the batter and turn it into stodge.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes]]\n[[Category:Squash recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Deep fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#plainflour #cornflour #blackpepper #deepfried #batter #lime #courgette #tempura #ricottacheese #lager #beer </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Courgette pasta with almond pesto and rocket",
                "revisions": [
                    {

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Courgette pasta with almond pesto and rocket Italian recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#courgettes #lemon #basil #courgettepastawithalmondpestoandrocket #almonds #chilli #juice #zest #pasta #pesto #oliveoil \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A delicious side or starter, ideal for vegetarians, vegans or anyone who wants to make an interesting meal using courgettes as pasta\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 200\n|PortionCalories = 50\n|DatePublished=8th June 2014\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  20 minutes\n|PrepTime =  20 minutes\n|CookTime = None\n|Image = [[Image:Courgette pasta with almond pesto and rocket recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Vegalicious \ud83e\udd17</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">No wonder it's only 50 calories a serving!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nA delicious side or [[Starter|starter]], ideal for vegetarians, vegans or anyone who wants to make an interesting meal using [[Courgettes|courgettes]] as [[Pasta|pasta]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 2 [[Courgettes|courgettes]] - select the straightest ones you can find\n| 1 [[Lemon|lemon]], [[Juice|juice]] and [[Zest|zest]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground pepper|freshly ground pepper]]\n| 20 g [[Almonds|almonds]]\n| 2 large handfuls of fresh [[Basil|basil]]\n| A pinch of red or yellow [[Chilli|chilli]], finely chopped (more or less, to taste)\n| A good few glugs of [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 2 large handfuls of fresh [[Rocket|rocket]]\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Trim the woody tops off the [[Courgettes|courgettes]]. Using a large, sharp knife, cut the [[Courgette|courgette]] lengthwise into long, thin panels. Cut each panel into thin [[Pasta|pasta]]-like ribbons.\n| Toss in a bowl with a pinch of [[Salt|salt]], the [[Zest|zest]] from the [[Lemon|lemon]] and a good squeeze of [[Juice|juice]].\n| Place the [[Almonds|almonds]], [[Basil|basil]], [[Chilli|chilli]] and a good pinch of [[Salt|salt]] in a [[Food processor|food processor]] (or you can pound in a [[Pestle and mortar|pestle and mortar]]). Pulse or pound until it starts to come together. Add a good squeeze of [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]] and then trickle in enough [[Oil|oil]] until to bring everything together nicely. Taste. Adjust seasoning or balance of [[Basil|basil]], [[Nuts|nuts]], [[Lemon|lemon]] and [[Oil|oil]].\n| Dollop a good spoonful or two of the [[Pesto|pesto]] in with your [[Courgettes|courgettes]]. Gently mix it with your hands, until the [[Courgettes|courgettes]] have a nice [[Pesto|pesto]] coating. Toss the [[Rocket leaves|rocket leaves]] in. Gently mix through. Finish with a drizzle of [[Olive oil|olive oil]], a squeeze of [[Lemon|lemon]], a few fresh [[Basil leaves|basil leaves]] and some chopped [[Almonds|almonds]]. Eat straight away or tote along to a picnic.\n}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Abel and Cole veg box recipes]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n{{Template:Abel and Cole veg box recipes attribution}}\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#courgettes #lemon #basil #courgettepastawithalmondpestoandrocket #almonds #chilli #juice #zest #pasta #pesto #oliveoil </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Crabmeat pasta with fennel and chillies recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#crabmeat #pasta #sweetcorn #parsley #crab #crabmeatpastawithfennelandchillies #driedpasta #lemon #fennel #dill #freshpasta \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This was one of the nicest pasta dishes that I've ever made. I'm sure it would be even better made with fresh crab\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 747\n|PortionCalories = 373\n|DatePublished=13th December 2014\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  40 minutes\n|PrepTime =  30 minutes\n|CookTime =  10 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Crabmeat pasta with fennel and chillies recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Fennel chilli kick!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.7</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">I thought these flavours would override the crabmeat but they were really rather good.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis is my version of Jamie Oliver's [[Crab]] Linguine, adapted for two people using [[Home made pasta|home made pasta]] cut into rustic strips rather that linguine. I've dressed it with fresh [[Parsley|parsley]] and [[Grilled|grilled]] [[Sweetcorn|sweetcorn]] as I can't wait for another chance to play with my Rothenberger MAPP blowtorch!\n\nI've used 2 packets of premium claw [[Crabmeat|crabmeat]] from Morrisons, about \u00a33.75 per carton ''Dec 2014''.\n\nThis was one of the nicest [[pasta]] dishes that I've ever made.  I'm sure it would be even better made with fresh [[crab]].  The [[sweet corn]] was absolutely essential for the balance of this dish, it's sweetness of setting the lemony tang.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 1 portion of [[Home made pasta|home made pasta]], cut into rustic strips, or 180 g [[Dried pasta|dried pasta]] of your choosing.\n| 2 x 114 g packs of Premium Claw [[Crabmeat]]\n| 1 fresh [[Lemons|lemons]]\n| Half a bulb of [[Fennel|fennel]]\n| 1 small [[Red chilli|red chilli]]\n| 1 [[Indian]] [[Green chilli|green chilli]]\n| 1 teaspoon of freshly chopped [[parsley]]\n| 4 tablespoons of [[Extra virgin Olive oil|extra virgin olive oil]]\n}}\n'''to garnish'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 1 fresh [[Sweet corn|sweet corn]] cob\n| Freshly chopped [[dill]]\n| A few nice [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* If you're using [[Fresh pasta|fresh pasta]], don't forget that you are best leaving it in the [[Fridge|fridge]] for an hour or so before you roll it out.  For this recipe I'm assuming that you have your [[Pasta|pasta]] already sorted!\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Add the [[Crabmeat|crabmeat]] to a bowl and add a pinch of [[Black pepper|black pepper]], a good pinch of chopped [[Parsley|parsley]] and any of the green [[Fennel tops|fennel tops]] if there are any.\n| Cut the base of the [[Fennel|fennel]] and trim any grotty bits.\n| Grate the [[Fennel bulb|fennel bulb]] into the [[Crab|crab]].  I've used my new [[Jamie Oliver acid etched coarse grater]].  If you have one, mind your fingers.  It does a blinding job but it is dreadfully sharp!\n| Using a small microplane [[Grater|grater]], add the [[Zest|zest]] of the [[Lemon|lemon]] to the [[Crab meat|crab meat]].\n| Deseed the both of the [[Chillies|chillies]] and chop finely. Add half to the [[Crab meat|crab meat]] and keep the remainder for dressing the dish.\n| Stir up the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] with the [[Juice|juice]] of the zested [[Lemon|lemon]] and mix this together with the chopped [[parsley]], into the [[Crab meat|crab meat]].\n| Gently heat the [[Crab meat|crab meat]] in a separate pan and cook your [[Pasta|pasta]] in a large pan of [[Boiling|boiling]] water. 3 minutes for [[Fresh pasta|fresh pasta]], 7 minutes + for [[Dried pasta|dried pasta]].\n| While the [[Pasta|pasta]] is cooking, [[Microwave|microwave]] the [[Sweet corn|sweet corn]] for a few minutes and toast it with your blowtorch if you have one. See here for more.\n| Drain the [[Pasta|pasta]], keeping back a ladle of the cooking [[Liquor|liquor]].\n| Mix the [[Pasta|pasta]] into the [[Crabmeat|crabmeat]], adding an eggcup full of the pasta water to thin the [[Sauce|sauce]] if needed.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe, scattered with the blackened [[Sweetcorn|sweetcorn]], chopped [[dill]] and the chopped [[Chillies|chillies]].\n\n{{Template:YoutubePastaDough}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Pasta recipes]]\n[[Category:Sea fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Shellfish recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#crabmeat #pasta #sweetcorn #parsley #crab #crabmeatpastawithfennelandchillies #driedpasta #lemon #fennel #dill #freshpasta </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

I LOVE THIS!!!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Crab]] [[Ravioli|ravioli]] and [[lobster bisque]] is a deliciously fishy way to get your [[Pasta|pasta]] hit.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 1 portion of [[Fresh pasta|fresh pasta]]\n| 200 g of white and [[Brown|brown]] [[Crabmeat|crabmeat]] (2 small pots)\n| [[Juice]] and [[Zest|zest]] of half a [[Lemon|lemon]]\n| 2 tablespoons of chopped [[Parsley|parsley]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| 1 can [[Lobster bisque|lobster bisque]] ([[Soup|soup]])\n| A few tablespoons of [[single cream]] to garnish (optional)\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Make the [[Fresh pasta|fresh pasta]], cover with [[Cling Film|cling film]] and leave in a cool place for an hour.\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Mix the [[Crabmeat|crabmeat]], [[Lemon zest|lemon zest]] and [[Juice|juice]], chopped [[Parsley|parsley]], [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and freshly [[Ground|ground]] black together in a bowl\n| Dust a cutting board with light [[Yellow cornmeal|yellow cornmeal]] or [[Plain flour|plain flour]]\n| Using a [[Pasta|pasta]] making machine, roll the pasta into a couple of sheets and lay out on the cutting board\n| Add a teaspoon of [[Crabmeat|crabmeat]] mix at regular intervals along one edge of the [[Pasta|pasta]] sheet\n| [[Brush]] the edges where they will join with a littl eof the [[Egg|egg]]-white reserved from making the [[Pasta|pasta]], or a tiny amount of water\n| Bring the empty edge over to cover the [[Crab|crab]] filling and press firmly down where they will join.\n| Cut the joins with a [[Pizza cutter|pizza cutter]] or a [[Ravioli cutter|ravioli cutter]]\n| Separate the [[Ravioli|ravioli]] and reinforce the joins by pressing down on the edges with the tines of a fork\n| [[Refrigerate]] the [[Ravioli|ravioli]] for an hour so the [[Pasta|pasta]] can firm up and the flavours of the [[Crabmeat|crabmeat]] mingle\n}}\n'''to cook'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| After making this many times, I prefer to cook the [[ravioli]] first in boiling salted water and then finish by heating in the [[lobster bisque]].  This ensures the ravioli is nicely cooked, otherwise it can be too al dente for my liking.  It does also mean that you can cook the ravioli a little ahead of time and just reheat in the soup.\n| Slide the ravioli into a pan of fast boiling salted water, bring it back to the boil and cook for 5 minutes.  A [[wok]] is ideal as it allows you to maneuver the pasta to ensure it's evenly cooked, without breaking it up.\n| Add the [[Lobster bisque|lobster bisque]] to another pan and gently bring to a [[Simmer|simmer]]\n| Carefully slide the [[Ravioli|ravioli]] into the [[Simmering|simmering]] [[Soup|soup]] and heat for 4 minutes\n| it is important that you jiggle the pan every now and then to prevent the [[Ravioli|ravioli]] from sticking to the base of the pan\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Home_made_crab_ravioli.jpg|300px|thumb|right|Rustic home made crab ravioli\nImage:Cutting ravioli.jpg|300px|thumb|right|A [[pizza cutter]] and a fork does better job than a specialised [[ravioli cutter]]\n</gallery>\n===Serving suggestions===\nFor  hint of luxury, drizzle a few tablespoons of [[single cream]] just before serving and serve with a [[Green leaf salad|green leaf salad]] of [[Rocket|rocket]] and [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n\n{{Template:YoutubePastaDough}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Soup and stock recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Pasta recipes]]\n[[Category:Sea fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Shellfish recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#ravioli #pasta #crabravioli #lobsterbisque #crabmeat #singlecream #raviolicutter #crab #pizzacutter #juice #freshpasta </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Crispy duck and hoisin pizza recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#pizza #duck #pizzastone #crispyduckandhoisinpizza #grill #oliveoil #pizzas #pizzadough #shredded #bake #provolone \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Another excuse to play with my homemade sous vide cooker and combine the results in a pizza. I used half of a boneless aromatic crispy duck for the main topping\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2432\n|PortionCalories = 1216\n|DatePublished=2nd May 2015\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  1 hour, 30 minutes\n|PrepTime =  1 hour, 15 minutes\n|CookTime =  15 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Crispy duck and hoisin pizza recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Fab idea!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.6</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Don't think I've ever seen this before but it was really good.</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nAnother excuse to play with my [[homemade sous vide cooker]] and combine the results in a [[Pizza|pizza]].\n\nI used half of a boneless aromatic [[Crispy duck|crispy duck]], bought from [[See Woo]], our brilliant local [[Chinese wholesalers]].  A couple of cooked [[Duck|duck]] breasts would work just as well on this [[Pizza|pizza]].\n\nI [[Vacuum packed|vacuum packed]] the half [[Duck|duck]] in 2 tablespoons of [[Peking duck|peking duck]] [[Sauce]] ([[Hoisin sauce]] is very similar) and cooked [[Sous vide|sous vide]] for 8 hours at 60\u00b0C and [[Shredded|shredded]] it ready for the [[Pizza topping|pizza topping]].  The duck would be perfectly cooked after 3 hours at 57\u00b0C, but I wanted to achieve the 'overcooked and falling apart' finish that you can't get with cooking for shorter times.  As it is vacuum sealed, it stays nice and moist and the quick heat from the grill give the duck a nice crispy finish.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 1 portion [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]] - Makes 2 [[Pizzas|pizzas]]\n| 150g of selected [[Cheeses|cheeses]], [[Grated|grated]].\n| 4 tablespoons of [[Tomato sauce for pizza]]\n| 4 medium [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], sliced\n| 300 g  peking crispy [[Duck|duck]], [[Shredded|shredded]]\n| A large bunch of fresh [[Chives|chives]], chopped\n| [[Olive oil]]\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Preheat the [[Grill|grill]] (if using a [[Pizza stone|pizza stone]])\n* If using the [[Oven|oven]], preheat it to 220\u00b0 C (425\u00b0 F - gas 7)\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Dust your work surface with [[Fine yellow cornmeal|fine yellow cornmeal]]\n| Divide the [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]] into two and roll out into two thin 25.5 cm (10 inch) [[Pizzas|pizzas]]\n| You can leave them in a [[Warm place|warm place]] for an hour or so to rise. I quite like them cooked immediately they are rolled out for a more crispy finish.\n| Prick the [[Pizza|pizza]] all over with a fork. This prevents it puffing up too much and burning while it is cooking\n| With a deft move, slide the [[Pizza|pizza]] from the [[Pizza peel|pizza peel]], on to the preheated [[Pizza stone|pizza stone]].\n| Cook on one side only for about 2 minutes or until lightly [[Browned|browned]].\n| Remove from the [[Oven|oven]] and spread the [[Pizza|pizza]] with 2 tablespoons of [[Tomato sauce for pizza|tomato sauce for pizza]].\n| Sprinkle the cheese over the tomato sauce and top with the shredded duck.  Don't put the cheese on top of the duck if you want it to be crispy.\n| Season with [[Salt|salt]], [[Pepper|pepper]] and finish with a drizzle of [[Olive oil|olive oil]].\n| Return to the [[Oven|oven]] and [[Bake|bake]] until the [[Cheese|cheese]] is nicely melted. This should take about 4 minutes under a [[Grill|grill]] on a [[Pizza stone|pizza stone]], if oven [[Baking|baking]], about 15 minutes in the middle of the oven.\n| Repeat for the second [[Pizza|pizza]].\n| Keep the first [[Pizza|pizza]] warm at the bottom of the [[Oven|oven]] whilst you make the second.\n| Sprinkle with chopped chives and serve\n}}\n===See also===\n*[[Sous vide duck pizza]]\n*[[Sous vide hoisin duck pizza]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Chinese recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Pizza recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Grilled, griddled or barbecued]]\n[[Category:Sous vide cooking]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#pizza #duck #pizzastone #crispyduckandhoisinpizza #grill #oliveoil #pizzas #pizzadough #shredded #bake #provolone </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }

This one uses a spicy pizza topping with home smoked bacon, topped with an egg.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 portion [[spicy tomato pizza topping]] (use a jar of shop-bought pizza sauce if you're stuck for time)\n| 1 portion [[pizza dough]] - makes 2 pizzas\n| 200 g (7 oz) [[mozzarella cheese]] (drained)\n| 100 g good quality sliced [[meat]] (eg: [[prosciutto]], [[salami]], [[speck]]). The recipe freezes well so the ingredients can be increased for later use or to increase [[Servings|servings]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 tablespoon [[Oil|oil]]\n| 1 small [[Red onion|red onion]]\n| &#189; [[Leek|leek]]\n| 1 [[Garlic|garlic]] clove\n| &#188; [[Red pepper|red pepper]]\n| 1 [[Carrot|carrot]]\n| 1 small [[Courgette|courgette]]\n| 1 tin chopped [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n| 150ml [[Vegetable Stock|vegetable stock]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Tomato puree]]\n| &#189; tablespoon [[Sun dried tomato]] [[Puree|puree]] (optional)\n| &#189; teaspoon [[Sugar|sugar]]\n| [[Basil]]\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Five Vegetable Pasta Sauce cooking.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Cooking the veg.\nImage:Five Vegetable Pasta Sauce ingredients.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Five Vegetable Pasta Sauce, the ingredients\n</gallery>\n\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Chop all of the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] fairly small, &#189; inch cubes or smaller.  It will save effort with the [[Hand|hand]] [[Blender|blender]] later and they will cook down quicker.\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a large pan\n| [[Fry]] the [[Carrot|carrot]] first as ths will take longest\n| Add the remaining veg, [[Onion|onion]], [[Leek|leek]], [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Red pepper|red pepper]] and [[Courgette|courgette]] and cook until soft.  about 10 minutes.\n| Add the tin [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Sugar|sugar]], [[Stock|stock]] and purees and give another few minutes to bring back up to heat.\n| [[Dried]] or fresh [[Basil|basil]] can be used, add at the last minute before blending.  No need to chop first if using fresh.\n| Using a [[Hand|hand]] [[Blender|blender]] straight in the pot is easiest although you can do this gradually in a worktop blender, blend until you reach a consistency you prefer.\n| Freezes well and can be gradually [[defrosted]] from [[Frozen|frozen]] on a low heat on the [[Hob|hob]] or in the [[Microwave|microwave]].\n}}\n===Chef's notse===\nThank you [[User:Kitchenminion|Kitchenminion]], for a wonderful recipe idea.  With the addition of a cheese topping, the ingredients shown served 2 people, for 2 days.
