#driedyeast #rosemary \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A version of Focaccia made in a Thermomix\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 145\n|PortionCalories = 15\n|DatePublished=16th February 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = 10\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  30 minutes\n|PrepTime =  10 minutes\n|CookTime =  20 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Focaccia TM recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Looks fab</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.7</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Wish my Thermy still worked \ud83e\udd14</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Carla_Cancio-Bello,_J.D.,_on_behalf_of_Cuban_Cuisine_UK|Carla]] </span></span>\n}}\nA version of [[Focaccia]] made in a [[Thermomix]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredientsTM\n\n| 500g [[Strong white bread flour|strong white bread flour]] (I used Sainsbury's Extra Strong Canadian [[Flour|flour]])\n| 1 x 7g sachet fast-action [[Dried yeast|dried yeast]] or 15g fresh [[Yeast|yeast]]\n| 30g [[Olive oil|olive oil]] plus extra for drizzling\n| 350g water (I used sparkling [[Mineral water|mineral water]])\n| 1 teaspoon fine [[Salt|salt]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Coarse salt|coarse salt]] for sprinkling (I used [[Salt#Himalayan Pink Rock Salt|pink Himalayan rock salt]]\n| 2 tablespoons fresh [[Rosemary leaves|rosemary leaves]], chopped\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Mix the [[Flour|flour]], [[Yeast|yeast]], [[Oil|oil]], water and fine [[Salt|salt]] '''20 seconds / Speed 6''', then '''2 minutes / [[Knead]]'''.\n| Leave to [[Rest|rest]] until [[Dough|dough]] is pushing up the MC.\n| '''10 seconds / [[Knead]]'''\n| Leave to [[Rest|rest]] again until [[Dough|dough]] is pushing up the MC.\n| Tip out the [[Dough|dough]] into an oiled [[Baking tray|baking tray]] 22cm x 33cm approx. and spread out using your hands.\n| Cover and allow to prove until almost doubled in size.\n| Make dimples in the risen [[Dough|dough]] with your fingers.\n| Sprinkle the [[Dough|dough]] with the extra [[Olive oil|olive oil]], the [[Coarse salt|coarse salt]] and the [[Rosemary|rosemary]].\n| Sprinkle a little water over the top.\n| [[Bake]] for 20-25 minutes 220\u00b0 C (425\u00b0 F - gas 7), [fan [[Oven|oven]] 200\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour].\n| Remove from the [[Oven|oven]] and allow to cool on a rack.\n}}\n===Recipe source===\n\n* Lightly adapted from a recipe in '''Fast and Easy Cooking''' which is the book supplied with Thermomixes in the UK.\n===Servings===\nServings: 10 - 1 large loaf\n\n===Chef's notes===\nTo remove any [[Dough|dough]] that may become stuck under the blades spin '''5 seconds / Speed 6'''.\n\nAga:  [[Bake]] on the floor rack of the [[Roasting]] [[Oven]] for 18-20 minutes.\n\nAlthough I used [[groundnut oil]] to grease the tin, the bread still stuck, probably due to the drizzled [[olive oil]] which soaks through the [[bread]].  I would recommend lining the tin with something such as [[Bake-O-Glide]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#dough #oliveoil #yeast #rest #coarsesalt #knead #flour #bake #rosemaryleaves #driedyeast #rosemary </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Focaccia Stromboli",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Focaccia Stromboli a cheese recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#dough #focacciastromboli #oliveoil #focaccia #breadmaker #mozzarellacheese #pizzastone #focacciabread #garlic #warmplace #rosemary \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A rolled focaccia bread that is filled with mozzarella cheese that erupts from the surface when hot. Best served whilst warm, directly from the oven\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2399\n|PortionCalories = 199\n|DatePublished=8th March 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment =\n |Servings = Servings: 12 - Makes 1 large cheese [[Focaccia]] bread\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 3 hours 30 minutes\n |PrepTime = 2 hours 30 minutes\n |CookTime = 1 hour\n |Image = [[Image:Focaccia Stromboli recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">A pizza, by another name</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Fabulous.  It's basically a rather good pizza!  Well done!!!</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Chef|Jerry, aka Chef]] ac([[User talk:Chef|talk]])</span></span>\n}}\nA rolled [[Focaccia bread|focaccia bread]] that is filled with [[mozzarella cheese]] that erupts from the surface when hot.\n\nBest served whilst warm, directly from the [[Oven|oven]].\n\nThe [[Dough|dough]] stage can be completed in a [[Breadmaker|breadmaker]] but the final [[Baking|baking]] needs to be done in the [[Oven|oven]].\n\n'''for the [[Focaccia bread|focaccia bread]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 2 teaspoons of [[Dried active yeast|dried active yeast]]\n| 350 ml water\n| 500g (1 lb) [[Strong white flour|strong white flour]]\n| 1.5 teaspoon fine [[Salt|salt]]\n| 3 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n}}\n''' for the topping and filling'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 200g (7 oz) [[mozzarella cheese]] cut into small chunks\n| 2 [[Garlic]] cloves, 1 peeled and crushed, 1 thinly sliced\n| A big handful of fresh [[Basil leaves|basil leaves]], roughly chopped\n| 3 tablespoons of [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| 1 tablespoon of finely chopped fresh [[rosemary]] leaves\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 200\u00b0 C (400\u00b0 F - gas 6)\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Focaccia Stromboli rolled.jpg|thumb|300px|right|[[Focaccia]] Stromboli - rolled, ready for the oven on a hot [[pizza stone]]\nImage:Focaccia Stromboli pre-roll.jpg|thumb|300px|right|[[Focaccia]] Stromboli - before rolling\n</gallery>\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| If using a [[Breadmaker|breadmaker]] make the [[Dough|dough]] using the longest dough setting you have, then follow the recipe from step 7\n| For the Panasonic SD 253 [[breadmaker]], use the French dough setting, for the [[Panasonic SD-ZB2502 automatic breadmaker]], use menu option 21, French dough.\n| Using a small bowl, add 250 ml of the (tepid / warm) water to a bowl and sprinkle the [[Yeast|yeast]] over it.  Leave in a [[warm place]] for 5 minutes to dissolve.\n| In a large mixing bowl, add the sifted [[Flour|flour]] and [[Salt|salt]]. Make a well in the centre and pour in the yeasted liquid.\n| Mix with your hands, adding as much of the remaining warm water as needed to make a sort pliable [[Dough|dough]].\n| Tip the [[Dough|dough]] out onto a floured worktop and [[Kneading bread|knead]] with your hands for 10 minutes so it becomes silky and elastic.\n| Clean the large bowl,  lightly [[Oil|oil]] it (an oil [[Spray|spray]] is good for this), add the [[Dough|dough]], cover with a damp cloth and leave to rise in a [[warm place]] for 2 hours.\n| [[Knock down]] and leave to rest for 10 minutes.\n| Shape the [[Dough|dough]] into a rectangle (35 cm x 20 cm (14\" x 8\")\n| Cover with a cloth and leave to rest for a further 15 minutes.\n| Sprinkle the [[Cheese|cheese]], [[Basil|basil]], [[Garlic|garlic]] and a little of the [[rosemary]] over the [[Dough|dough]] then, starting from one of the shorter side, roll up like a [[Swiss]] roll.\n| Place on an oiled [[Baking|baking]] sheet and [[Punch|punch]] holes in the surface.  This is where the [[Mozzarella cheese|mozzarella cheese]] will erupt from while it bakes.\n| Drizzle with half of the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] the sprinkle with chopped [[Rosemary leaves|rosemary leaves]], [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]].\n| [[Bake]] for 1 hour.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nDrizzle with the remaining [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and serve warm.\n===Chef's note===\nIf using a [[pizza stone]] follow the preheating directions and allow to heat in the [[oven]] and slide the [[focaccia]] onto the stone from a [[cornmeal]]-dusted [[pizza peel]] or similar.\n==See also==\n* [[Stromboli]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Breadmaker recipes]][[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#dough #focacciastromboli #oliveoil #focaccia #breadmaker #mozzarellacheese #pizzastone #focacciabread #garlic #warmplace #rosemary </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }

title": "Folded breakfast pizza",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Folded breakfast pizza\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#pizza #bakedbeans #pizza #bakedbeanpizza #breakfastpizza #baconandbeans #pizzas #pizzastone #russelsofupwell\n|hashtagrev=12032020\n|description=An egg, sausage, bacon and baked beans calzone pizza. Perfect Heinz beans folded pizza\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n\n{{recipesummary\n|DatePublished=6th March 2023\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  1 hour, 45 minutes\n|PrepTime =  1 hour, 15 minutes\n|CookTime =  30 minutes\n|TotalCalories = 2129\n|PortionCalories = 1064\n|Image = [[Image:Folded breakfast pizza recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">A fabulous pizza</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">I couldn't eat one for breakfast though \ud83d\ude32</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Sue_spins|Susie]] </span></span>\n}}\nAn [[Egg|egg]], [[Sausage|sausage]], [[Bacon|bacon]] and [[baked beans]] folded [[Calzone pizza|calzone pizza]].\n\nThis recipe makes 2 nice big [[Pizzas|pizzas]], perfect for two hungry people! I don't think I could eat this for [[Breakfast|breakfast]] though, but it makes a wonderful evening meal!\n\nIt's worth draining the excess sauce from the [[Beans|baked beans]] and removing the extra water from the [[Mozzarella|mozzarella]] or your [[Pizza|pizza]] might be a bit soggy.\n\nYou can make your own [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]] or buy ready made [[Pizza|pizza]] [[Dough|dough]], the rest is easy.  There's a page [[Calzone folding|here on how to crimp the folded pizza]] if you're unsure how to do it.\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 1 portion [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]]\n| 2 slices of [[Treacle Cured Bacon from Russell's of Upwell]]\n| 2 [[Pork sausages|pork sausages]]\n| 2 large [[Eggs|eggs]]\n| 1 can of Heinz [[Beans|beans]] (415 g)\n| 1 ball [[Mozzarella cheese|mozzarella cheese]]\n| 100 g [[Grated|grated]] [[Cheddar cheese|cheddar cheese]]\n| 50 g [[Grated|grated]] [[Gruyere cheese|gruyere cheese]] (optional) \n| [[Cornmeal]] for dusting; use [[Plain flour|plain flour]] at a push\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Tip the [[Beans|beans]] out into a [[Sieve|sieve]] or [[Colander|colander]] and leave it for an hour to allow most of the [[Sauce|sauce]] to drain. Discard the drained sauce.\n* Squeeze as much of the water as you can from the [[Mozzarella|mozzarella]] and tear into small pieces.\n* Leave it in a [[Sieve|sieve]] to drain while the [[Beans|beans]] do the same.\n* Preheat your [[Oven|oven]] to 210\u00b0 C (410\u00b0 F - gas 6)\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Slice the [[Sausages|sausages]] lengthwise - this helps them cook properly\n| Chop the [[Bacon|bacon]] into small bite-size pieces\n| Grate the [[Cheddar]] or mixture of hard [[Cheese|cheeses]]\n| We find it easier to divide the fillings onto separate dishes prior to 'building' the two [[Pizzas|pizzas]] - up to you!\n| Divide the [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]] into two portions and roll out on a worksurface liberally  dusted with [[Cornmeal|cornmeal]] to stop it sticking\n| If you're using a [[Pizza stone|pizza stone]], build the [[Pizzas|pizzas]] on a really well dusted [[Baking tray|baking tray]] or you'll never get them off your work surface\n| When filling the [[Pizza|pizza]] try to keep the filling to one half of the [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]]\n| Also make sure you leave a decent 'edge' unfilled or you will have a job crimping it\n| Sprinkle the [[Mozzarella|mozzarella]] and [[Cheddar|cheddar]], etc. over one half the base of each [[Pizza|pizza]]\n| Pour the [[Baked beans|baked beans]] over the [[Cheese|cheese]]\n| Cover with the chopped [[Bacon|bacon]] and place the slices [[Sausages|sausages]] over the [[Beans|beans]] and [[Cheese|cheese]]\n| Top with a raw [[Egg|egg]]\n| Fold the [[Pizza|pizza]] over and [[Calzone folding|crimp the edges]] to make sure none of the lovely filling escapes while cooking\n| Make a couple of holes in the top of each [[Pizza|pizza]]\n| [[Bake]] for 30 minutes at  210\u00b0 C (410\u00b0)\n| Remove it from the [[Oven|oven]] and leave to [[Rest for|rest for]] 10 minutes if you can wait! This way you can make sure the [[Sausage|sausage]] is properly cooked\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Folded breakfast calzone pizza on a pizza stone.jpg|Two baked bean breakfast pizzas baked on the pizza stone after 30 minutes\nImage:Baked bean calzone pizza ready to bake on a pizza stone.jpg|Ready to bake for 30 minutes at 210\u00b0 C - 410\u00b0 F\nImage:Baked bean sausage bacon egg pizza ready to fold.jpg|Ready to fold and crimp - cross your fingers!\nImage:The ingredients for a baked bean and breafast pizza.jpg|All of the ingredients for a breakfast calzone pizza\n</gallery>\n===Recipe source===\n* I got the idea from this from a daytime tv [[Air-fryer|air-fryer]] advert and thought that using a [[Pizza stone|pizza stone]] I can do a better job of this than they did in an air-fryer\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Pizza recipes]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:12032020'>#pizza #bakedbeans #pizza #bakedbeanpizza #breakfastpizza #baconandbeans #pizzas #pizzastone #russelsofupwell</code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Really easy to make and as good with frozen peas as it is\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1445\n|PortionCalories = 361\n|DatePublished=20th January 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime = 10 minutes\n|PrepTime = 5 minutes\n|CookTime = 5 minutes (microwave)\n|Image = [[Image:Formaggio piselli recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">The Fast Show food?</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Jesse's favourite, probably.</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\n\nOk it's really [[Cheesy peas|cheesy peas]], but is sounds so posh that it's staying as Formaggio piselli!\n\nReally easy to make and as good with [[Frozen|frozen]] [[Peas|peas]] as it is with fresh peas, which means you can make this with stuff from the [[fridge]] and freezer.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 2.5 cups of [[Frozen]] [[Peas|peas]]\n| &#190; cup of [[Parmesan]] [[Cheese|cheese]] (once [[Grated|grated]])\n| 1 tablespoon [[Butter|butter]]\n| 1 juice and [[Zest|zest]] from half a [[Lemon|lemon]]\n| Sea [[Salt|salt]] and freshly ground [[Black pepper|black pepper]]\n| pinch of [[Sugar|sugar]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Cook the [[Peas|peas]] to your liking:\n|# Fresh [[Peas|peas]] - 4 minutes in [[Boiling|boiling]] water\n|# [[Frozen]] [[Peas|peas]] - From frozen - in a bowl with 1 tablespoon of water, cover with a saucer and microwave on full power for 4 minutes\n| Drain and reserve a little of the cooking water.\n| Add the [[Peas|peas]] to a small pan with the [[Butter|butter]], a few tablespoons of the cooking water (or [[Chicken|chicken]] [[Stock|stock]] if you have some to hand), season to taste with [[Salt|salt]], [[Pepper|pepper]] and [[Sugar|sugar]].\n| Tip the [[Parmesan]] [[Cheese|cheese]] in and stir well to coat the [[Peas|peas]], adding a little extra liquid if required.\n| The end result should be glossy, well coated [[Peas|peas]].\n| Remove from the heat, drizzle with the [[Lemon|lemon]] juice and sprinkle with the lemon [[Zest|zest]].\n}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Peas]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Peas]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes|Peas]]\n[[Category:Starters|Peas]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes|Peas]]\n[[Category:Microwaved]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#peas #formaggiopiselli #frozen #parmesan #butter #zest #lemon #cheese #boiling #stock #fridge </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

cup of [[Parmesan]] [[Cheese|cheese]] (once [[Grated|grated]])\n| 1 tablespoon [[Butter|butter]]\n| 1 juice and [[Zest|zest]] from half a [[Lemon|lemon]]\n| Sea [[Salt|salt]] and freshly ground [[Black pepper|black pepper]]\n| Pinch of [[Sugar|sugar]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Cook the [[Peas|peas]] to your liking:\n|# Fresh [[Peas|peas]] - 4 minutes in [[Boiling|boiling]] water\n|# [[Frozen]] [[Peas|peas]] - From frozen - in a bowl with 1 tablespoon of water, cover with a saucer and microwave on full power for 4 minutes\n| Drain and reserve a little of the cooking water.\n| Add the [[Peas|peas]] to a small pan with the [[Butter|butter]], a few tablespoons of the cooking water (or [[vegetable stock]] if you have some to hand), season to taste with [[Salt|salt]], [[Pepper|pepper]] and [[Sugar|sugar]].\n| Tip the [[Parmesan cheese]] in and stir well to coat the [[Peas|peas]], adding a little extra liquid if required.\n| The end result should be glossy, well coated [[Peas|peas]].\n| Remove from the heat, drizzle with the [[Lemon|lemon]] juice and sprinkle with the lemon [[Zest|zest]].\n}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Peas]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Peas]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes|Peas]]\n[[Category:Starters|Peas]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes|Peas]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Peas]]\n[[Category:Microwaved]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#peas #frozen #butter #lemon #zest #cheesypeas #boiledorsimmered #vegetablestock #grated #blackpepper #parmesan </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Fresh pasta",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Fresh homemade pasta, an Italian recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#flour #freshpasta #egg #eggs #pastacookingtimes #chickens #dough #kneadingbread #yolk #foodprocessor #spinach \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Having the benefit of free range chickens, this recipe is often used and is far superior to even the very best shop bought fresh pasta\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 133\n|PortionCalories = 67\n|DatePublished=22nd July 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = Blended until 'rice-like'\n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime = 20 minutes plus 30 minutes drying time\n|PrepTime = 15 minutes\n|CookTime = 5 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:RecipeFresh pasta.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Can't go wrong</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Makes great pasta - I can't be bothered with a machine, I just roll it and cut it into strips.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Artisan pasta.jpg|thumb|right|300px|'Artisan pasta' - roll out and slash into strips with a knife.  Thank you Jamie.]]\nHaving the benefit of [[Chickens|free range chickens]], this recipe is often used and is far superior to even the very best shop bought fresh pasta.\n\nIt's easier with a pasta machine, but by no means impossible without.  Use Jamie Oliver's trick, with a [[rolling pin]], roll the pasta into a few sheets at the thickness you require, then slice into rustic strips with a knife. Simple.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 100 g [[Italian grade 'OO' flour]] or [[plain flour]]\n| 1 whole [[:Category:Egg recipes|free range egg]]\n| 1 [[:Category:Egg recipes|free range egg yolk]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add all of the [[flour]] into a [[food processor]] and give it a whizz\n| Add the whole [[egg]] and the [[yolk]] and blitz it until it resembles rice grains, about 2 minutes or so\n| If it turns floury add a tiny drop of water\n| Likewise, if it stays as wet [[dough]], add a little more [[flour]]\n| Once it's rice-like, knock out onto a lightly dusted worktop and [[Kneading bread|knead]] into a ball, place in a bowl and cover with a dampened tea-towel for an hour or so\n| Divide into 3 or 4 balls, placing unused balls back in the covered bowl\n| With a rolling pin, roughly roll out each ball so it fits into your pasta machine, and  repeatedly run through the machine, from the thickest setting, to the final thickness\n| It's useful if you can hang the pasta over a skewer until it's ready to use or it tends to stick together\n| In the biggest pan you have (10 pints water / 1 lb pasta) bring water with a pinch of [[salt]], to the boil - no oil required\n| Once on a rolling boil, add the pasta, a quick stir with a chop-stick or long spoon to prevent sticking\n| The texture you should be aiming for is [[al-dente]] - a little resistance when you bite; rabbit like! This only takes a few minutes with fresh pasta\n| Once [[al-dente]], remove, drain and serve\n}}\n===By weight: ratio of [[flour]] to [[eggs]]===\nTo calculate the exact amount of [[eggs]] to [[flour]], by weight, use 3 parts [[flour]] to 2 parts [[egg]].  To make a rich ''Royal pasta dough'', use only the egg yolks, reserving a little of the white should you need to moisten the dough a little.\n\nIf using this method, weigh the eggs first and then multiply that by 1.5 to calculate the amount of flour you will need.\n===Variations===\n\nA handful of [[spinach]] leaves will produce green pasta, [[tomato puree]] - red; experiment with colours. You may need to add slightly more [[flour]] if your additions already contain water (as with spinach)\n\nTo make whole wheat pasta use three quarters of durum wheat flour and one quarter of chickpea flour with a little bit of water and olive oil, no eggs. \n\nWhole wheat flour and spelt flour can be used as well, always with a little bit of water and oil. Once you have done the dough, leave it in the fridge for half an hour: it will be easier to roll it out. Follow instruction above. Whole wheat pasta has a slightly harder texture and it's ideal for [[Pasta e fagioli|pasta e fagioli]].\n===Drying hand-made pasta===\nSince this recipe was written, I've found a far easier way to dry hand rolled pasta, especially if you're just going to rustically hand cut it.  Shake a generous amount of [[fine yellow cornmeal]] onto a work surface and lay the pasta sheets on the cornmeal once it has been rolled out to your desired thickness. Leave it an hour or more to dry out and then you can then cut it to any shape you want.  The cornmeal prevents it from sticking to the work surface and unlike flour, most of the cornmeal falls off as you handle the pasta.  What doesn't fall off, separates during the boiling process.\n\n===Dried pasta===\nDried pasta is fresh pasta that has been air dried to remove all moisture.  Most dried pasta is not made with egg so will keep for years.  If pasta has been made with egg it will only keep for a few days and should be refrigerated whilst it is being stored.\n===Cooked rice and food safety===\nCooked pasta and cooked rice is a primary source of [[bacillus cereus food poisoning]]. Once pasta or rice is cooked it should be promptly consumed or kept hot (over 60\u00b0C [140\u00b0F]) or refrigerated (below 4\u00b0C [40\u00b0F]).  It must not be left at room temperature.\n== How much does one cup of pasta weigh? ==\n\n''Estimated [[Generic_conversion_table#Volume|US cup]] to weight equivalents:''\n\n<table border=\"0\" cellpadding=\"2\" width=\"500\">\n\n  <tr>\n\n    <td colspan=\"2\"><strong>Ingredient</strong></td>\n\n    <td><strong>US Cups </strong></td>\n\n    <td><strong>Grams</strong></td>\n\n    <td><strong>Ounces</strong></td>\n\n  </tr>\n\n    \n\n  <tr>\n\n    <td>Pasta</td>\n\n    <td>short cut - dry</td>\n\n    <td><div align=\"center\">1</div></td>\n\n    <td>100 grams</td>\n\n    <td>4 ounces</td>\n\n  </tr>\n\n    \n\n  <tr>\n\n    <td>Pasta</td>\n\n    <td>short cut - cooked</td>\n\n    <td><div align=\"center\">1</div></td>\n\n    <td>200 grams</td>\n\n    <td>7 ounces</td>\n\n  </tr>\n</table>\n\n'''Conversion notes:'''<br />\n\nEvery [[ingredient]] has a cups to ounces or grams conversion table. Search for the ingredient, cup to weight conversions are at the end of each ingredient page.\n\nWe also have a [[generic conversion table]] and a [[portions per person lookup]].\n\n<YouTube>https://youtu.be/RLiP_6YNQ3I</YouTube>\n==See also==\n* '''[[Gallery of pasta types]]'''\n* '''[[Pasta cooking times]]'''\n* '''A varied selection of [[:Category:Pasta recipes|Pasta recipes]]'''\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Pasta]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes|Pasta]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Pasta]]\n[[Category:Pasta recipes|Pasta]]\n[[Category:Store cupboard items|Pasta]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#flour #freshpasta #egg #eggs #pastacookingtimes #chickens #dough #kneadingbread #yolk #foodprocessor #spinach </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }

Thanks.</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nLiterally meaning 'drowned [[Omelette|omelette]]' this recipe comes from the Arezzo area of Tuscany.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 5 [[free range eggs]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Plain flour|plain flour]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Dried|dried]] [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]]\n| Seasoning\n| [[Olive oil]]\n| 1 [[Onion|onion]], finely chopped\n| 1 stick of [[Celery|celery]], finely chopped\n| 1 [[Carrot|carrot]], finely chopped\n| [[Garlic]] to taste, finely chopped\n| 6 ripe [[Plum tomatoes|plum tomatoes]], skinned, seeded and chopped (use canned if fresh are not available)\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Beat the [[Eggs|eggs]] in a bowl with the [[Flour|flour]], [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]] and seasoning.\n| Heat some [[Oil|oil]] in a large [[Frying pan|frying pan]] until hot, the add the [[Egg|egg]] mixture.\n| When the underside is cooked, slide it onto a plate and the back into the pan on the other side and cook until golden.\n| Leave until it is totally cold.\n| Meanwhile, [[Fry|fry]] the [[Onion|onion]], [[Celery|celery]] and [[Carrot|carrot]] until the onion is soft, then add the [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]].\n| Season, mix well and [[Simmer|simmer]] until you have a smooth, rich [[Sauce|sauce]] - about 20 minutes.\n| Cut the [[Omelette|omelette]] into strips, add to the [[Sauce|sauce]] and heat through for 5 minutes.\n| Serve, sprinkled with the [[Parmesan]] [[cheese]].\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nGrate some [[Parmesan cheese]] over the top and serve with a [[Crunchy salad|crunchy salad]] and some [[Bread|bread]].\n===Chef's notes===\nIf you do not have the confidence to slide the [[Omelette|omelette]] in and out of the pan, you can [[Cheat|cheat]].  When the underside is done, cook the top under a hot [[Grill|grill]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n{{OmeletteRecipes}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#frittataaffogata #omelette #garlic #carrot #sauce #breadcrumbs #celery #onion #plumtomatoes #simmer #tomatoes </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Gluten free sausage and spinach pasta bake",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Gluten free sausage and spinach pasta bake recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#pasta #grated #glutenfree #spinach #sausage #tomato #boil #butter #whitesauce #glutenfreesausageandspinachpastabake #nutmeg \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This gluten free sausage, spinach and pasta bake comes to Cookipedia courtesy of debbie&andrews sausages\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 3467\n|PortionCalories = 577\n|DatePublished=23rd October 2015\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 6\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime =  1 hour, 10 minutes\n|PrepTime =  15 minutes\n|CookTime =  55 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Gluten free sausage and spinach pasta bake recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Different!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">I do like the idea of spinach in this.  Healthy too.</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Perfect-pork.png|300px|thumb|right|[[Debbie and Andrew's Perfect Pork sausages]]]]\nThis [[Gluten free|gluten free]] [[Sausage|sausage]], [[Spinach|spinach]] and [[Pasta|pasta]] [[Bake|bake]] comes to [[Cookipedia]] courtesy of [[debbie&andrew's sausages]]. This makes a great easy meal for six people.\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 1 pack [[Debbie and Andrew's Perfect Pork sausages]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 1 [[Onion|onion]], [[Diced|diced]]\n| 1 [[Carrot|carrot]], [[Grated|grated]]\n| 150ml [[Red wine|red wine]]\n| 300ml [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]]\n| 3 tablespoons [[Tomato|tomato]] pur\u00e9e\n}}\n====for the pasta layer:====\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 50g [[Butter|butter]]\n| 50g [[Plain flour|plain flour]] (for a [[Gluten free|gluten free]] alternative, try Udi's [[All purpose flour|all purpose flour]] Mix)\n| 600ml [[Milk|milk]]\n| 1tsp freshly [[Grated|grated]] [[Nutmeg|nutmeg]]\n| 500g penne [[Pasta|pasta]] (or a [[Gluten free|gluten free]] alternative)\n| 200g fresh [[Spinach|spinach]]\n| 140g [[Cheddar cheese|cheddar cheese]], [[Grated|grated]]\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Preheat your [[Oven|oven]] to 190\u00b0 C (375\u00b0 F - gas 5), [fan oven 170\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Slit the [[Sausages|sausages]] and remove the [[Meat|meat]] from the skins. Chop or [[Dice|dice]] the [[Sausage meat|sausage meat]] into small bite-size pieces.\n| Now heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a non stick pan, add the [[Onion|onion]] and [[Fry|fry]] for 5 minutes until soft and golden. Stir in the [[Sausage meat|sausage meat]] and fry for another 5 minutes. Finally add the [[Carrot|carrot]], [[Wine|wine]], [[Stock|stock]] and [[Tomato|tomato]] pur\u00e9e and season well with [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]]. Bring to the [[Boil|boil]] then [[Simmer|simmer]] for 10 minutes and set aside.\n| Melt the [[Butter|butter]] in another pan. Add the [[Flour|flour]] and stir to make a [[Roux|roux]]. Slowly add the [[Milk|milk]], whisking all the time, until the [[White sauce|white sauce]] is thick and smooth. Add the [[Nutmeg|nutmeg]] and more seasoning then stir and put to one side.\n| Bring a large pan of [[Salted|salted]] water to the [[Boil|boil]]. Add the [[Pasta|pasta]], stir well, bring back to the boil then cook for 10 minutes until [[Al dente|al dente]]. Remove from the heat, stir in the [[Spinach|spinach]] and leave for 2 minutes until the spinach wilts. Drain the pasta and spinach well and put to one side.\n| In a shallow ovenproof dish, layer the three mixtures - [[Pasta|pasta]] first, then [[Sausage|sausage]] mix, then [[White sauce|white sauce]]. Make sure your top layer is white [[Sauce|sauce]] and sprinkle with [[Cheese|cheese]].\n| [[Bake]] in the preheated [[Oven|oven]] for 20 minutes until golden [[Brown|brown]] and bubbling on top. Serve immediately.\n}}\n===See also===\n* [[Udis Gluten Free Products|Udi's Gluten Free Products for gluten free baking products]]\n* [http://www.healthysupplies.co.uk/gluten-free-pasta.html?gclid=COSSior32MgCFaYSwwodvOsFHA Gluten free pasta from www.healthysupplies.co.uk]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Gluten free recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pasta recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Stews and casseroles]]\n[[Category:Debbie&andrew's sausage recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n{{Template:DebbieAndAndrew attribution}}\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#pasta #grated #glutenfree #spinach #sausage #tomato #boil #butter #whitesauce #glutenfreesausageandspinachpastabake #nutmeg </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

We have our own hens so that's a help!\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 portion of [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]] - Makes 2 pizzas\n| 5 or 6 spears of giant [[Asparagus|asparagus]]\n| 1 [[Green bell pepper|green bell pepper]], [[Roasted sweet peppers|roasted]] de-seeded and roughly chopped\n| 220 g of [[Goat|goat]]'s [[Cheese|cheese]]\n| 4 tablespoons of [[Tomato sauce|tomato sauce]] - see Chef's notes below\n| 2 [[Hard boiled eggs|hard boiled eggs]], peeled but left whole\n| A handful of [[Fresh herbs|fresh herbs]], chopped\n| [[Extra virgin olive oil]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Chop the [[Asparagus|asparagus]] diagonally in 2cm slices, discarding the woodier parts from lower down.\n** Normal [[Asparagus|asparagus]] can be left whole and [[Blanched|blanched]] for about 3 to 4 minutes.\n* [[Boil]] the [[Asparagus|asparagus]] for 10 to 12 minutes\n* [[Roast]] the [[Sweet Pepper|pepper]] - [[Roasted sweet peppers|see here]]\n* Make the [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]]\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 220\u00b0 C (425\u00b0 F - gas 7), [fan oven 200\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Make 1 pizza per person\n| Roll the [[Dough|dough]] out into two circles\n| Divide the fillings into two portions, one for each pizza\n| Spread the [[Tomato sauce|tomato sauce]] on to one half of the circle, leaving the edge free from [[Sauce|sauce]]\n| [[Crumble]] the [[Cheese|cheese]] over the [[Sauce|sauce]]\n| Sprinkle the chopped [[Herbs|herbs]], [[Asparagus|asparagus]] and [[Green peppers|green peppers]] over the [[Sauce|sauce]]\n| Pop the [[Egg|egg]] in the middle, season with [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]] and give a final drizzle of [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| [[Brush]] the clean edge with water or [[Milk|milk]] so it helps to make a good seal\n| Fold the [[Pizza|pizza]] [[Calzone folding]]\n| [[Bake]] for about 20 minutes\n}}\n===Variations===\n* These pizzas are so versatile that you can put almost anything in them. They will get hot enough to melt the cheese but anything that might need pre-cooking needs to be done outside of the pizza.  They get ''just'' hot enough to cook a raw egg if that's any help.\n===Chef's notes===\nAs we make [[Pizzas|pizzas]] so often, I divide up homemade [[Tomato sauce|tomato sauce]] into single-[[Pizza|pizza]]-portions and [[Freeze|freeze]] them in small bags.  If I've no homemade [[Sauce|sauce]], I [[Cheat|cheat]] and use a few tablespoons from a bottle of ready made [[Pasta sauce|pasta sauce]]  and freeze the remainder as above.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes]]\n[[Category:Pizza recipes]][[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#asparagus #sauce #tomatosauce #goatscheeseandasparaguscalzonepizza #cheese #pizzadough #pizza #roastedsweetpeppers #egg #sweetpepper #blanched </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

I came up with this recipe as I thought the flavours and textures went well together.  They do! another nice fish dish.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nAs a general rule, when you cook fish you want keep things simple and you don't want to ruin the delicate flavour of the fish with sauces (such as [[maionese]]): use just a little bit of lemon, olive oil, garlic and herbs such as thyme and oregano.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 whole [[grey mullet]] (the common name in Italian is \"cefalo\" or \"muggine\")\n| 1 [[lemon]]\n| 1 [[Garlic|garlic]] clove\n| thyme (better fresh)\n| [[salt]] and [[black pepper]]\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat your [[Grill|grill]] or the [[Oven|oven]] to the highest temperature.\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Mix the lemon juice and some of the rind grated, thyme and garlic finely chopped and salt\n| Cut the fish two or three times on each side\n| Place in a baking dish and pour the mix over, leave to marinate for half an hour turning it a few times\n| Grill the fish for about 6-10 minutes each side (depending on the size)\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Grey mullet with thyme.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Grey Mullet with thyme, garlic and lemon\nImage:Grey mullet.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Grey Mullet\n</gallery>\n===Serving suggestions===\nYou can serve with a green vegetable of your choice and/or boiled or [[Roast_potatoes|roast potatoes]].\n===Variations===\nInstead of thyme you can use [[oregano]] or [[rosemary]].\n\nInstead of grilling you can cook it in the oven at 200 \u00b0C for 15-30 minutes depending on the size of the fish. To check it is cooked try to remove a small piece: it should come away easily, if not put back in the oven for another 5 minutes and check again.\n==See also==\n* http://www.jamieoliver.com/recipes/fish-recipes/barbequed-red-mullet-with-a-hot-salsa\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Sea fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Grilled, griddled or barbecued]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#grilledgreymullet #miseenplace #barbecued #maionese #blackpepper #grilled #rosemary #greymullet #roast_potatoes #grill #lemon </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Grilled White Fish with Balsamic Vinegar an Italian recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#fish #grilledwhitefishwithbalsamicvinegar #spinach #oliveoil #boil #rice #balsamicvinegar #belazu #grill #basa #balsamic \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Try this fresh and healthy fish recipe with basa fillets for a change\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1088\n|PortionCalories = 272\n|DatePublished=20th January 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = Served with new potatoes and green peppers and a salad\n |Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 30 minutes\n |PrepTime = 10 minutes\n |CookTime = 20 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Grilled White Fish with Balsamic Vinegar recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Fine flavours</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.6</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Really nice tastes. Any balsamic vinegar works well in this recipe. You don't need the expensive stuff!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis recipe works well with any firm-bodied [[white fish]], try it with [[Basa|basa]] fillets for a change.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 4 fillets of white [[Fish|fish]], such as [[Basa|basa]], [[Cod|cod]], [[Haddock|haddock]] or [[Sea bass|sea bass]] \n| 300g [[Basmati rice|basmati rice]] \n| 1 tablespoon [[Belazu]] [[Olive oil|olive oil]] \n| 4tbsp [[Belazu]] [[Balsamic vinegar|balsamic vinegar]] \n| 350g young [[Spinach|spinach]]\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat your [[Grill|grill]] or the [[Oven|oven]] (400F/200C/gas mark 6) depending upon your cooking preference.\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Place the [[Fish|fish]] on a plate and season lightly with [[Salt|salt]]. Leave for 10 minutes. \n| Meanwhile, rinse the [[Rice|rice]] and place in a pan with 450ml cold water. Bring to the [[Boil|boil]], then immediately reduce the heat to very low and cover the pan. Cook for 10 minutes. Turn off the heat and leave, covered, for 10 minutes.\n| [[Boil]] the kettle. Preheat the [[Grill|grill]] to its highest setting. Rinse the [[Fish|fish]] and pat dry with kitchen paper.\n| Smear the [[Fish|fish]] fillets with [[Olive oil|olive oil]], place on 15cm [[Foil|foil]] squares and fold up the edges to make little boat.\n| Splash each fillets with 1 tablespoon [[Balsamic|balsamic]]. Place on the [[Grill pan|grill pan]] and cook, placed about 6cm from the heat, for 5-8 minutes, depending on the thickness of the fillet, until just cooked through. If more convenient, cook the [[Fish|fish]] in hot [[Oven|oven]] (400F/200C/gas mark 6).\n| Cook the [[Spinach|spinach]] for 1 minute in [[Boiling|boiling]] [[Salted|salted]] water. Drain in a [[Colander|colander]], pressing out excess water.\n}}\n\n(''Lindsey Bareham in The Times'')\n\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Grilled White Fish with Balsamic Vinegar grilling.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Grilling\nImage:Grilled White Fish with Balsamic Vinegar marinading.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Marinading\n</gallery>\n\n===Serving suggestions===\nSlip [[Fish|fish]] and juices on to a plate and serve with the [[Rice|rice]] and [[Spinach|spinach]].\n===Variations===\nInstead of grilling in tin-foil 'boats', I just marinaded the fish for 2 hours in [[balsamic vinegar]] and [[olive oil]] and then grilled for about 4 minutes a side, turning once - lightly oil the grill tray first to prevent sticking.\n\nThis was very nice served with [[new potatoes]] ([[Potatoes#Pictures of varieties of potatoes|Pink Fir Apple]]) and a small salad.\n\n{{Template:Belazu attribution}}\n===Belazu products used in this recipe===\n* [http://www.mybelazu.com/details/balsamic-vinegar.html Belazu Balsamic Vinegar]\n* [http://www.mybelazu.com/details/early-harvest.html Belazu Early Harvest Extra Virgin Olive Oil Unfiltered]\n* [http://www.mybelazu.com/products/extra virgin-olive-oils.html Belazu Extra virgin olive oil]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Belazu recipes]]\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Sea fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Grilled, griddled or barbecued]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#fish #grilledwhitefishwithbalsamicvinegar #spinach #oliveoil #boil #rice #balsamicvinegar #belazu #grill #basa #balsamic </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

#herbs #garlic #ham #fry #spaghetti #onions \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A quick and easy recipe that is idea for students or anyone who is short on time and cooking equipment\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1613\n|PortionCalories = 403\n|DatePublished=6th May 2014\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime =  20 minutes\n|PrepTime =  5 minutes\n|CookTime =  15 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Ham, tomato and pasta scramble recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Lovely</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">..and I'm retired, not a student!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:NonLoggedInUser|NonLoggedInUser]] </span></span>\n}}\nA quick and easy recipe that is idea for students or anyone who is short on time and cooking [[Equipment|equipment]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 2 [[Cloves of Garlic, peeled and crushed|cloves of garlic, peeled and crushed]]\n| 1 [[Onion|onion]], peeled and finely chopped\n| 2 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 125 g pack of cooked sliced [[Ham|ham]], chopped finely\n| 1 tablespoon [[Tomato puree|tomato puree]]\n| &#188; teaspoon [[Caster Sugar|caster sugar]], or [[Cheat|cheat]]: crush normal [[Sugar|sugar]] between 2 tablespoons\n| &#189; teaspoon [[Dried oregano|dried oregano]]\n| 1 400g can of chopped [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n| 225 g (8 oz) [[Spaghetti|spaghetti]]\n| [[Sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]] to taste\n| 1 ball of [[Mozzarella cheese|mozzarella cheese]], [[Grated|grated]] or finely sliced and chopped\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| [[Boil]] a [[Kettle|kettle]] full of water for your [[Pasta|pasta]]\n| Add the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] to a [[Frying pan|frying pan]] and give it a good twist of [[Black pepper|black pepper]]\n| Gently [[Fry|fry]] the [[Onions|onions]] for 4 minutes, stirring now and then\n| Add the [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Fry|fry]] for another few minutes, don't let it burn\n| Add the [[Ham|ham]] and '[[Stir-fry|stir-fry]]' it for a minute so it can absorb the flavour of the [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Onions|onions]]\n| Meanwhile, cook the [[Spaghetti|spaghetti]] for 8 to 10 minutes in lightly [[Salted|salted]] [[Boiling|boiling]] water\n| Drain and return to the [[Pasta|pasta]] saucepan\n| Pour the [[Sauce|sauce]] over the cooked [[Pasta|pasta]] and mix really well\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with the [[Grated|grated]] [[Mozzarella|mozzarella]] sprinkled on top.\n\nA few fresh [[tomatoes]] dotted about look and taste nice and could be part of your [[5 a day]].\n===Variations===\nUse any [[Herbs|herbs]] of your choice, as a general rule you can usually use double the amount of [[Fresh herbs|fresh herbs]] compared to  [[Dried|dried]] [[Herbs|herbs]].\n\nSpoil yourself, add a little [[Grated|grated]] [[Parmesan cheese|parmesan cheese]] as well\n===Chef's notes===\n[[Cheat]] on the chopped [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], use normal canned [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]  and while they are still in the can, use a sharp knife to chop them up.\n\n{{Template:YoutubePastaDough}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat title": "Ham leek and cheese gratin",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Ham leek and cheese gratin recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#leeks #cheesesauce #microwave #ham #boil #cheddarcheese #hamleekandcheesegratin #butter #cheese #breadcrumbs #blackpepper \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This recipe is a simple way of combining leeks, cheese and ham into a gorgeous meal\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1634\n|PortionCalories = 817\n|DatePublished=30th September 2015\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime =  15 minutes\n|PrepTime =  15 minutes\n|CookTime = None\n|Image = [[Image:Ham leek and cheese gratin recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">A bit burnt, hey?</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">You need to watch this a bit closer!</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Chef|Jerry, aka Chef]])</span></span>\n}}\nI always seem to let our [[Leeks|leeks]] run to [[Seed|seed]], by which time they are unusable.  This year I'm making an effort to use them profusely.  I've even deliberately run out of [[Onions|onions]] and just put a sign in the [[Onion|onion]] bowl: \"USE LEEKS!\"\n\nThis recipe is a simple way of combining [[Leeks|leeks]], [[Cheese|cheese]] and [[Ham|ham]] into a gorgeous meal.\n\nThis was very tasty but one problem was the whole leeks.  Although it looks nice, once soft they are very difficult to cut - in future I will slice them thinly and probably not par-boil first. 20 seconds in the [[microwave]] would be enough.\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 4 medium to small [[Leeks|leeks]], liberally trimmed, peeled and cleaned\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| Pinch of fresh [[Thyme leaves|thyme leaves]]\n| 150g cooked [[Ham|ham]] - the thinner the better, thick ham does not roll well!\n| 100g [[Cheddar cheese]] for the [[Cheese sauce|cheese sauce]]\n| &#190; pint of [[Milk|milk]] [354 ml]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Butter|butter]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Plain flour|plain flour]]\n| 4 tablespoons [[Panko|panko]] [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]]\n| 25g [[Cheddar cheese]] to top\n| 25g crumbled [[Blue cheese|blue cheese]] (optional)\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 4), [fan oven 160\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Leeks and ham sauce added.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Adding the final topping\nImage:Leeks and ham ready for cheese sauce.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Leeks rolled in ham, ready for the sauce\n</gallery>\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Ensure the [[Leeks|leeks]] are properly cleaned\n| I've used small gratin dishes so had to halve them but you can leave them whole\n| [[Boil]] the [[Leeks|leeks]] in lightly [[Salted|salted]] water for about 8 minutes or until softened - they can also be microwaved, see below.\n| Drain well.\n| Meanwhile, to make the [[Cheese sauce|cheese sauce]], melt the [[Butter|butter]] with a pinch of [[Black pepper|black pepper]] and stir in the [[Flour|flour]] once melted.\n| Whisk the [[Milk|milk]] in and bring to a [[Simmer|simmer]], don't [[Boil|boil]]. Once [[Simmering|simmering]], whisk well, add 100 g of the [[Cheddar]] and once melted, remove from the heat.\n| Roll the [[Leeks|leeks]] in the cooked [[Ham|ham]] and lay in a lightly oiled gratin dish or shallow [[Casserole|casserole]].\n| Pour the [[Cheese sauce|cheese sauce]] over the [[Leeks|leeks]].\n| If you have the time, chilling the mixture in the gratin dishes (as pictured), solidifies the cheese sauce making it easier to add the topping, which has a tendency to sink into the hot sauce.\n| Mix the [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]] and any [[Cheese|cheese]] you are using for the topping in a bowl and [[Crumble|crumble]] well, maybe add a pinch of [[Black pepper|black pepper]].\n| Pour this mixture over the top and [[Bake|bake]] uncovered at the top of the [[Oven|oven]] at 180\u00b0 C\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nA few [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] is all this dish needs to finish it off.\n===Variations===\nYou could include a little [[Pasta|pasta]] to stretch this dish even further.\n===Chef's notes===\nThe [[Leeks|leeks]] can be softened in the [[Microwave|microwave]], the advantage of this over [[Boiling|boiling]] is that they keep their color.\n\nLay them on a plate and [[Microwave|microwave]] on full power for 2 minutes.full power.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#leeks #cheesesauce #microwave #ham #boil #cheddarcheese #hamleekandcheesegratin #butter #cheese #breadcrumbs #blackpepper </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Insalata di ruote a cheese recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#insalatadiruote #pasta #anchovies #bread #garlic #prosciutto #salad #lemonjuice #greenpepper #tomatoes #diced \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Ruote is a wagon wheel shaped pasta and this is a salad made with prosciutto, anchovies and Parmesan cheese\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1125\n|PortionCalories = 281\n|DatePublished=25th October 2012\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = Pasta Ruote and Pasta Spighe\n |Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 35 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 20 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Pasta Ruote and Pasta Spighe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Fancy-pants pasta rules</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Much nicer than plain-old macaroni!</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[:Image:Pasta 2006 3.jpg|Ruote]] is a wagon wheel shaped [[Pasta|pasta]] and this is a [[Salad|salad]] made with [[Prosciutto|prosciutto]], [[Anchovies|anchovies]] and [[Parmesan cheese]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 100 g ruote - see '''Variations''' and '''Chef's Notes''' below\n| 2 thick slices [[Bread|bread]], crust removed and cubed\n| 90 ml [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| [[Garlic]] cloves, to taste, cut in half\n| 1 bunch [[Spring onions|spring onions]], coarsely chopped\n| &frac12; small [[Iceberg lettuce|iceberg lettuce]], [[Shredded|shredded]]\n| 50 g small [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]], wiped and sliced\n| 100g [[Prosciutto|prosciutto]], [[Diced|diced]]\n| 1 [[Green pepper|green pepper]], [[Diced|diced]]\n| 50 g [[Anchovies|anchovies]], chopped\n| 15 ml [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]]\n| 30 ml Worcester [[Sauce|sauce]]\n| Seasoning\n| 6 baby [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], halved\n| 25 g [[Parmesan]], shaved\n| Small handful of [[Black olives|black olives]], pitted\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| [[Boil]] the [[Pasta|pasta]] in a large saucepan of water until [[Al dente|al dente]] - see instructions on packet.\n| Drain, rinse and cold water and drain again, throughly.\n| [[Fry]] the [[Bread|bread]] cubes in 30 ml of the [[Oil|oil]] until golden and drain on [[Kitchen towel|kitchen towel]].\n| Rub a [[Salad|salad]] bowl with the [[Garlic|garlic]] cloves and discard.\n| Add the [[Pasta|pasta]] to the bowl, together with the [[Lettuce|lettuce]], [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]], [[Prosciutto|prosciutto]] and [[Green pepper|green pepper]]. Mix gently.\n| Make a dressing with the remaining [[Oil|oil]], [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]], Worcester [[Sauce|sauce]], seasoning and [[Anchovies|anchovies]].\n| Pour over the [[Salad|salad]], add the [[Bread|bread]] and toss thoroughly.\n| Garnish with the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Parmesan]] and [[Olives|olives]].\n| Serve immediately\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nGoes well with plainly cooked [[Steak|steak]] or on its own.\n===Variations===\nAs an alternative to ruote, try spighe or any other open [[pasta shape]].\n===Chef's notes===\n[[:Image:Pasta 2006 3.jpg|Ruote]] and [[:Image:Pasta 2006 3.jpg|spighe]] are not very easy to find.  I have come across these types of [[Pasta|pasta]] in Lidl's and some independent delicatessens.  Ruote can be obtained online from [[Fratelli Camisa]].\n\nPersonally, I never bother rubbing [[Garlic|garlic]] on the inside of bowls as you can hardly taste it.  I would prefer just to crush some up and mix it with the dressing.\n===Chef's notes===\n{{Template:ThinkPig}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Insalata di ruote]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Insalata di ruote]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes|Insalata di ruote]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes|Insalata di ruote]]\n[[Category:Freshwater fish recipes|Insalata di ruote]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes|Insalata di ruote]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes|Insalata di ruote]]\n[[Category:Pasta recipes|Insalata di ruote]]\n[[Category:Pasta salad recipes|Insalata di ruote]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes|Insalata di ruote]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes|Insalata di ruote]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Insalata di ruote]]\n[[Category:Starters|Insalata di ruote]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes|Insalata di ruote]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#insalatadiruote #pasta #anchovies #bread #garlic #prosciutto #salad #lemonjuice #greenpepper #tomatoes #diced </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

If you are using softer vegetables that are likely to turn to mush after prolonged cooking, add them during the last few hours of cooking.\n\nProbably not authentically Italian, but I used the remaining meat, padded out by the kidney beans, to make two 'pies' with [[dumpling crusts]] - very good they were too. It's ideal for [[Freezing|freezing]], make double the quantity and [[Freeze|freeze]] in small batches for extra quick meals.\n\nThis has to be a cheat because it's so simple to make.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 500g (18 oz) lean [[Minced beef|minced beef]]\n| 1 tablespoon freshly chopped [[Oregano|oregano]] - ''see variations''\n| 1 small [[Onion|onion]], finely chopped\n| 2 Cloves of [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled and crushed\n| [[Zest|zest]] of 1 [[Lemon|lemon]], finely chopped\n| 15 g (1/2 oz) fresh [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| Pinch of [[Grated|grated]] [[Nutmeg|nutmeg]]\n| 1 [[Egg|egg]], beaten\n}}\n''' for [[Frying|frying]]'''\n* [[Olive oil]]\n''' to serve'''\n* 520 g Buttered [[Spaghetti|spaghetti]] or buttered [[Egg noodles|egg noodles]]\n* 30 g [[Parmesan cheese]] - shaved with a [[Speed peeler|speed peeler]] or freshly [[Grated|grated]]\n\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| In a large bowl, mix all of the ingredients with clean hands until nicely combined.\n| Cover and [[Refrigerate|refrigerate]] for 3 or 4 hours if possible for the flavours to mix.\n| Divide the mixture into about 20 balls, roughly the size of a golf ball.\n| Gently shallow [[Fry|fry]] in a little [[Olive oil|olive oil]] until [[Browned|browned]] on the outside and cooked to your liking. About 5 to 7 minutes, turning regularly - scrape from the pan with a spatula to prevent them breaking up.\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Italian meatballs, twenty.jpg|20 Italian meatballs\nImage:Italian meatballs, mixed.jpg|Mixed, ready to chill\nImage:Italian meatballs ingredients.jpg|Meatball ingredients\n</gallery>\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe on a pile of buttered pasta or egg noodles and [[Tomato_sauce#Tomato_sauce_recipes|one of these tomato sauces]]\n\nGarnish with shavings of [[Parmesan cheese]].\n===Variations===\nUse [[pork]] instead of [[beef]].\n\nTry an [[Alfredo sauce]] instead of a tomato based sauce.\n\nUse fresh [[Basil|basil]] as an alternative, or a mixture of [[basil]] and [[Oregano|oregano]] (or [[Marjoram|marjoram]]), if using [[Dried oregano|dried oregano]], use 1 teaspoon.  Don't bother with [[Dried|dried]] [[Basil|basil]].\n===Chef's notes===\nI forgot to buy the lemon for this recipe, so used slightly less than a quarter of the rind (flesh discarded) from one of my [[preserved lemons]], finely chopped.\n\n{{Template:YoutubePastaDough}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Beef recipes]]\n[[Category:Cookery cheats]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pasta recipes]]\n[[Category:Student recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#basil #italianmeatballswithpasta #parmesancheese #oliveoil #grated #oregano #freezing #dried #meatballrecipe #panfried #driedoregano </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Don't add more stock until the previous liquid has been absorbed into the [[rice]]\n| This will about 20 minutes\n| Once the rice is cooked, stir in the [[cream]] and season with [[salt]] and freshly grated [[black pepper]]\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\n\nServe immediately with freshly grated [[Parmesan cheese]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Rice recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#butter #leeks #parmesancheese #rice #leekandcreamrisotto #vegetable #boiledorsimmered #simmer #vegetarian #blackpepper #risottorice </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Lentil lasagne - A Thermomix recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#butter #cheese #lentils #lasagne #puylentils #nutmeg #onion #sauce #garlic #vegetablestock #groundcoriander \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Lentils often sound boring, but used this way they are delicious especially if made with earthy Puy lentils (Lentilles vertes du Puy)\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1777\n|PortionCalories = 444\n|DatePublished=26th September 2014\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime =  2 hours, 5 minutes\n|PrepTime =  20 minutes\n|CookTime =  1 hour, 45 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Lentil lasagne TM recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Prawn and crab is nicer</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">3.4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">\ud83d\ude03</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Lentil lasagne2.jpg|thumb|300px|right|The interior]]\nLentils often sound boring, but used this way they are delicious especially if made with earthy [[Puy lentils]] (Lentilles vertes du Puy)\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 350g [[Puy lentils]]\n| 125g [[Parmigiano-Reggiano|Parmesan]] or [[Grana Padano]] cheese (for a vegetarian alternative, use Bookham's [[Twineham Grange cheese]])\n| 30g [[Butter|butter]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 1 large [[Onion|onion]], thickly sliced\n| [[Garlic]] to taste, thickly sliced\n| 2 teaspoons [[Ground coriander|ground coriander]]\n| 600g [[Vegetable Stock|vegetable stock]]\n| Seasoning\n| 40g [[Plain flour|plain flour]]\n| 40g [[Butter|butter]]\n| [[Freshly ground white pepper]]\n| Freshly [[Ground|ground]] [[Nutmeg|nutmeg]] - use plenty\n| 600g [[Milk|milk]]\n| [[Lasagne]] sheets (use the ones that don't require cooking first)\n| Extra [[Butter|butter]] for dotting (optional)\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Wash the [[Lentils|lentils]] and put them in a jug covered with [[Boiling|boiling]] water.\n| Meanwhile cut the [[Cheese|cheese]] into chunks, add to the bowl '''6 seconds / Speed 10''''''Bold text'''\n| Remove from the bowl and reserve\n| Add the [[Butter|butter]], [[Oil|oil]], [[Onion|onion]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] to the TM bowl '''25 minutes / Speed 1 / Temp Varoma / Reverse blade / MC off''', but increase to '''Speed 2 for the last 10 minutes'''\n| Drain the [[Lentils|lentils]] and add to the bowl '''2 minutes / Speed 2 / 100\u00b0 C / Reverse blade / MC off'''\n| Add the [[Coriander|coriander]] and [[Vegetable Stock|vegetable stock]] '''25 minutes / Speed 2 / 100\u00b0 C  / Reverse blade / MC off''' - much of the liquid should have been absorbed.  If not, increase the cooking time, but watch it because you don't want the mixture to be totally absorbed\n| Season to taste, but bear in mind that the [[Cheese|cheese]] will be salty\n| Remove from the bowl and reserve\n| Rinse the bowl so that any traces of the [[Lentils|lentils]] mixture have disappeared (no need for a thorough wash)\n| Add the [[Butter|butter]], [[Flour|flour]], [[Pepper|pepper]], [[Nutmeg|nutmeg]] and [[Milk|milk]] to the rinsed out bowl '''7 minutes / Speed 4 / 90\u00b0 C / MC on'''\n| In the meantime, preheat the [[Oven|oven]] 200\u00b0 C (400\u00b0 F - gas 6), [fan oven 180\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n}}\n'''To prepare for the [[Oven|oven]] '''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Take a [[Lasagne|lasagne]] or [[Baking|baking]] dish and pour half of the [[Lentil|lentil]] mixture into the bottom - spread it out fairly evenly\n| Cover with [[Lasagne|lasagne]] sheets\n| Pour half of the [[Sauce|sauce]] over the sheets, then top with half of the [[Grated|grated]] [[Cheese|cheese]]\n| Add the remaining [[Lentils|lentils]], [[Lasagne|lasagne]] sheets, [[Sauce|sauce]] and [[Cheese|cheese]] as just described\n| Dot the top layer of [[Cheese|cheese]] with [[Butter|butter]] if desired.\n| [[Bake]] for about 45 minutes\n}}\n===Recipe source===\n\n* Adapted and converted for [[Thermomix]] from a recipe by Rose Elliot\n===Chef's notes===\nThe timing for cooking the [[Lentils|lentils]] is approximate and you may find that you will need a little less [[Stock|stock]] or a shorter cooking time.  [[Puy lentils]] are cooked in 20-25 minutes if [[Boiled|boiled]], so try not to overcook them, especially as they have had a short soaking beforehand.  Just don't let the mixture get too dry and bear in mind that the liquid will continue to evaporate whilst making the [[Basic white sauce|b\u00e9chamel sauce]].\n{{LasagneRecipes}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Pasta recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#butter #cheese #lentils #lasagne #puylentils #nutmeg #onion #sauce #garlic #vegetablestock #groundcoriander </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "\n<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Liver in garlic butter recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#liver #breadcrumbs #garlic #flour #butter #thymeleaves #eggwash #liveringarlicbutter #sieve #panfried #salad \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Another nice way to cook liver with as much garlic as you like!\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|DatePublished=15th May 2019\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  2 hours, 10 minutes\n|PrepTime =  2 hours\n|CookTime =  10 minutes\n|TotalCalories = 1365\n|PortionCalories = 682\n|Image = [[Image:Liver in garlic butter recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Wow!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Just Wow.  What a mix of flavours\ud83e\udd17</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Chef|Jerry, aka Chef]])</span></span>\n}}\nAnother nice way to cook [[Liver|liver]] with as much [[Garlic|garlic]] as you like!\n\nAs a habit, I like to soak [[Liver|liver]] in [[Milk|milk]] before cooking.  You can omit that step if you wish, other than imparting more [[Garlic|garlic]] flavour, it probably doesn't make too much difference.\n[[Image:Liver coated, ready to fry.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Breadcrumbed liver, ready to fry]]\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 3 tablespoons [[Butter|butter]]\n| Pinch of [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| 6 [[Cloves of Garlic, peeled and crushed|cloves of garlic, peeled and crushed]]\n| 200 ml [[Milk|milk]]\n| 200g [[Lambs|lambs]] [[Liver|liver]], deveined and thinly sliced\n| 1 tablespoon picked [[Thyme leaves|thyme leaves]]\n| 2 [[Eggs|eggs]], beaten\n| 2 tablespoons of [[Plain flour|plain flour]]\n| 25g [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]]\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Add the [[Milk|milk]], half of the [[Crushed garlic|crushed garlic]] and the sliced [[Liver|liver]] to a [[Lock and Lock box]], cover, shake well and leave for an hour or two, shaking now and then.\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Drain the [[Milk|milk]] from the [[Liver|liver]] using a [[Sieve|sieve]] so you retain the [[Garlic|garlic]]!\n| Beat the [[Thyme leaves|thyme leaves]] into the [[Egg|egg]]\n| Arrange the [[Flour|flour]], [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]], [[Egg wash|egg wash]] on plates, and a spare plate for the coated [[Liver|liver]]\n| Coat the [[Liver|liver]] in [[Flour|flour]], [[Dip|dip]] in the [[Egg wash|egg wash]] and roll in the [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]]\n| Heat the [[Butter|butter]] in a [[Frying pan|frying pan]] and add the [[Black pepper|black pepper]]\n| Add the remaining [[Garlic|garlic]] to the pan and [[Fry|fry]] for one minutes\n| Add all of the [[Liver|liver]] to the pan and cook for 5 minutes, turning once\n| Remove from the pan and [[Rest for|rest for]] 5 minutes\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with a light [[Salad|salad]] and [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]].  We had some leftover roasties too.  Yum!\n===Variations===\nWe make [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]] from the [[Bread|bread]] we [[Bake|bake]] everyday which makes this look rather 'gnarly'.  Normal breadcrumbs are fine.\n===Chef's notes===\nAdd the [[Flour|flour]] to a [[Lock and Lock box]] with the drained [[Liver|liver]], cover and shake well.  This is quick, easy and the best way to evenly flour the liver.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Lamb recipes]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#liver #breadcrumbs #garlic #flour #butter #thymeleaves #eggwash #liveringarlicbutter #sieve #panfried #salad </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Lobster ravioli with a light tomato and curry leaf sauce",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Lobster ravioli with a light tomato and curry leaf sauce recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#pasta #lobster #semolina #sauce #ravioli #groundnutoil #salad #coriander #springonions #creamcheese #parsley \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This is a delightfully sophisticated lobster recipe.\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|DatePublished=26th September 2016\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = 2 \n|Difficulty = 3\n|TotalTime =  3 hours, 10 minutes\n|PrepTime =  2 hours\n|CookTime =  1 hour, 10 minutes\n|TotalCalories = 1157\n|PortionCalories = 578\n|Image = [[Image:Lobster ravioli with a light tomato and curry leaf sauce recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Thanks Nik!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Seems a long time since we've made this together!</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis [[unusual recipe]] comes courtesy of [[Nik & Edwina's cookbook]].\n\nA delightfully sophisticated dish this, the elegant sweet/[[Salt|salt]] flavour of the [[Lobster|lobster]] goes incredibly well with the warm, comforting, creamy taste and texture of the [[Pasta|pasta]], and the deliciously light, bright, sweet/savoury summery [[Sauce|sauce]].\n\nThere will be some [[Pasta|pasta]] left over - it is difficult to make any less than this - but it freezes very well indeed.\n{{RecipeIngredients\n}}\n====the pasta ====\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 100g 00 [[Pasta|pasta]] [[Flour|flour]] \n| 1 whole [[Egg|egg]] \n| fine [[Semolina|semolina]] for dusting \n}}\n====the sauce====\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| [[Groundnut oil]] \n| 6 [[Curry leaves|curry leaves]] (preferably fresh) \n| 6 ripe [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], halved \n| 150ml [[Fish stock|fish stock]] \n| 100ml water \n| 10g [[Coriander|coriander]] [[Roots|roots]], washed and finely chopped \n}}\n====the ravioli filling:-====\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 1 raw [[Lobster|lobster]] tail, shelled and cut in half \n| 1 [[Red chilli|red chilli]], finely chopped \n| 2 [[Spring onions|spring onions]], very finely chopped \n| 3 teaspoon chopped [[Parsley|parsley]] \n| 1 tablespoon mild [[Cream cheese|cream cheese]] \n| 1 teaspoon [[Milk|milk]] \n| [[Salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]]\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| To make the [[Pasta|pasta]] put the '00' pasta [[Flour|flour]] and [[Egg|egg]] in a bowl and mix together well until you have a soft smooth [[Dough|dough]]. It takes about 5 minutes. Turn the dough out onto a [[Semolina|semolina]] dusted work surface and let stand for 5 minutes. Then [[Knead|knead]] for 5 minutes until the dough is very smooth, and similar in texture to plasticene. Cover the ball of dough with [[Cling Film|cling film]] and allow to [[Rest for|rest for]] a least 2 hours in the [[Fridge|fridge]] \n| To make the [[Sauce|sauce]], put a tablespoon of [[Groundnut oil|groundnut oil]] into a large [[Saucepan|saucepan]]. Gently [[Fry|fry]] the [[Onions|onions]] for a minute or so then add the [[Curry leaves|curry leaves]] and [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]. Cook until tomatoes have softened, then add the water, [[Coriander|coriander]] [[Roots|roots]] and [[Fish stock|fish stock]]. [[Simmer]] for 20 minutes, then strain and check seasoning and set aside \n| To make the [[Ravioli|ravioli]] filling, [[Steam|steam]] the [[Lobster|lobster]] for four minutes. Remove from heat, and allow to cool a little, then chop finely. Place two thirds of the lobster in a [[Food processor|food processor]] along with the [[Chilli|chilli]], [[Spring onions|spring onions]], [[Milk|milk]], [[Cream cheese|cream cheese]] and [[Parsley|parsley]], and whizz until very smooth. Then stir the remaining lobster into the mix, and set aside \n| To make the [[Ravioli|ravioli]], roll the [[Pasta|pasta]] out thinly and pass through a [[Pasta machine|pasta machine]] until almost translucent. Place on a floured surface and cut out 12 x 8cm circles. Put a heaped teaspoon of the [[Lobster|lobster]] mixture in the centre of 6 of the circles, then smear a little water around the edge. Pop another disc of pasta on top, smoothing the edges together ensuring that there aren't any air bubbles inside, and seal the edges well. Place on a plate sprinkled with fine [[Semolina|semolina]], to stop the ravioli sticking together. Repeat with the other half of the pasta to create a total of 6 pieces. This can be done 3-4 hours in advance, if needs be \n| Finally get a large pan of [[Boiling|boiling]] [[Salted|salted]] water going. Once at a rolling [[Boil|boil]], gently add the [[Pasta|pasta]] and cook for 4-5 minutes. Meanwhile reheat the [[Sauce|sauce]] and divide between two [[Soup|soup]] plates. Add three [[Ravioli|ravioli]] each, garnish with some [[Salad|salad]] leaves and serve\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with your favourite [[Salad|salad]] leaves\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Pasta recipes]]\n[[Category:Sea fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Shellfish recipes]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n[[Category:Nik and Edwina's Cookbook recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#pasta #lobster #semolina #sauce #ravioli #groundnutoil #salad #coriander #springonions #creamcheese #parsley </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }
