title": "Meatballs from sausages",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Meatballs from sausages, a recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#sausages #oliveoil #onion #sausagemeat #meatballs #yellowcornmeal #fry #meatballsfromsausages #pizza #herbs #basil \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Make up to 35 lovely meatballs from just six sausages - fabulous for pizzas or meatballs and spaghetti\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|DatePublished=11th February 2017\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = 35 meatballs from 6 sausages!\n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime =  25 minutes\n|PrepTime =  15 minutes\n|CookTime =  10 minutes\n|TotalCalories = 2421\n|PortionCalories = 605\n|Image = [[Image:Meatballs from sausages recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">40 meatballs!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">I did even better than you: 40 meatballs from 6 sausages.</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nWe bought some lovely Italian-style [[Sausages|sausages]] from [[Gourmet sausage maker - Bexley]] ([[Hall Place Farmers' Market, Bexley, Kent]]), but this time, instead of using them as sausages we would extract the [[Sausagemeat|sausagemeat]] from the sausages and make [[Meatballs|meatballs]].\n\nWe'll use half of them to make a [[Pizza|pizza]] each and the remainder can be [[Frozen|frozen]] to be used later in a nice [[Tomato sauce|tomato sauce]] with some [[Spaghetti|spaghetti]].\n\nI've added fresh [[Basil|basil]] as it will works very well with the [[Italian sausages]].  Use whatever fresh or dried [[Herbs|herbs]] you feel would suit your particular [[Sausages|sausages]].\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 6 meaty [[Italian]]-style [[Sausages|sausages]]\n| Pinch of [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| 4 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 1 small white [[Onion|onion]], very finely chopped\n| Bunch of fresh [[Basil leaves|basil leaves]], finely chopped\n| 2 tablespoons of [[Yellow cornmeal|yellow cornmeal]]\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| With a sharp knife, carefully cut the [[Sausages|sausages]] lengthwise and [[Scoop|scoop]] the [[Sausagemeat|sausagemeat]] from the skins, which you can discard.\n| Peel and very finely chop the white [[Onion|onion]].\n| Finely chop the fresh [[Basil|basil]].\n| Mix the chopped [[Onion|onion]], [[Herbs|herbs]] and [[Sausagemeat|sausagemeat]] together in a bowl and scrunch it together in your hands, squeezing it  through your fingers to mix really well.\n| Using a teaspoon as a rough measure, roll the mixture into quite small balls - I managed 35 small [[Meatballs|meatballs]] from 6 [[Sausages|sausages]]!\n| Toss the [[Meatballs|meatballs]] in [[Yellow cornmeal|yellow cornmeal]].\n| Add a pinch of [[Black pepper|black pepper]] to the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and gently [[Fry|fry]] for about 5 minutes, turning once.\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Six fat Italian-style sausages meatball ingredients.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Ingredients for the meatballs\nImage:Six fat Italian-style sausages.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Six fat Italian-style sausages\n</gallery>\n===Serving suggestions===\nIdeal for adding to [[Pizzas|pizzas]] or to serve in a [[Tomato sauce|tomato sauce]] with [[Pasta|pasta]].\n===Chef's notes===\nI'm deliberately using more [[Olive oil|olive oil]] than I really needed to [[Fry|fry]] the [[Sausages|sausages]] in because I want any remaining [[Oil|oil]] from the [[Frying|frying]] to drizzle over the [[Pizza|pizza]] before [[Baking|baking]] it.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Pizza recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#sausages #oliveoil #onion #sausagemeat #meatballs #yellowcornmeal #fry #meatballsfromsausages #pizza #herbs #basil </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Meatball pizza",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Meatball pizza a cheese recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#pizza #meatballpizza #meatballs #sauce #pizzastone #grill #pizzas #oliveoil #mozzarellacheese #chili #redwine \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=To my mind this is about the pizza and the sauce, not the actual meatballs, hence using shop-made meatballs\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1893\n|PortionCalories = 473\n|DatePublished=22nd October 2012\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 4 - Makes two large [[Pizzas|pizzas]]\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  1 hour 25 minutes<br />Includes making the dough\n|PrepTime = 1 hour 15 minutes  \n|CookTime =  10 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Meatball pizza recipe baked.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Pizza perfection</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">A complete meal that tastes even better than it looks</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nTo my mind this is about the [[Pizza|pizza]] and the [[Sauce|sauce]], not the actual [[Meatballs|meatballs]], hence using shop-made meatballs.  By all means '''[[Meatballs|make your own]]''' if you feel so inclined.\n\nUse a [[Pizza stone|pizza stone]]!  It makes such a difference.  Your [[Pizzas|pizzas]] will go from those soggy-based shop bought shockers, to [[Pizza]] Express perfection in one simple step!\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 portion [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]]\n| 300 g pack of cooked [[Meatballs|meatballs]] of your choice\n| 150 g pack of [[Mozzarella cheese|mozzarella cheese]]\n| large can [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], chopped.\n| A good glug of [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 1 [[Onion|onion]], peeled and sliced\n| 2 [[Cloves garlic, crushed|cloves garlic, crushed]]\n| 1 [[Dried|dried]] [[Chile de Arbole|chile de arbole]], [[Ground|ground]] to powder in a [[Coffee grinder|coffee grinder]] or [[Pestle and mortar|pestle and mortar]] (or &frac12; teaspoon [[Chili powder|chili powder]])\n| 125 ml [[Red wine|red wine]]\n| A pinch of [[Sugar|sugar]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| [[Fine yellow cornmeal]] for dusting\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Make the [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]] as instructed\n* If using a [[pizza stone]], preheat the [[pizza stone]] under a very hot [[grill]] for about 20 minutes.  Place it about 8cm (3\") from the heat source.\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Meatball pizza ready for the oven.jpg|Ready for the oven\nImage:Meatball pizza stone baked.jpg|One done, one waiting\nImage:Meatball pizza tomato sauce.jpg|Tomato sauce reduced\n</gallery>\n===Method===\n'''Meatball [[Sauce|sauce]]'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| [[Fry]] the [[Onions|onions]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] in a few glugs of [[Olive oil|olive oil]] seasoned with [[Black pepper|black pepper]] until soft, about 10 minutes.\n| Add the [[Meatballs|meatballs]], [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Red wine|red wine]], [[Chili|chili]] and [[Simmer|simmer]] until reduced and very thick - you don't want a wet [[Pizza|pizza]].\n| As I have plenty of time on [[Pizza|pizza]] day (Friday!) I make the [[Sauce|sauce]] early in the afternoon and put it on the heat for 5 minute batches every hour or so, leaving it uncovered to 'dry-out' in between. You can of course just [[Simmer|simmer]] to reduce, but you need to watch it and keep stirring all the time.\n| Season to taste\n}}\n'''Putting it together'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Preheat the [[Grill|grill]] to high as you can get it\n| Set the [[Pizza stone|pizza stone]] about 8 cm (3\") below the heat source or the [[Pizza|pizza]] may burn\n| Dust the work surface with [[yellow cornmeal]] and then stretch or roll the [[Dough|dough]] into two thin rounds\n| Prick the pizza all over with a fork. This prevents it puffing up too much and burning while it is cooking\n| [[Grill]] the [[Pizza|pizza]] for about 2 minutes on one side only or until browned.\n| Remove from the oven, flip over and ad the topping.\n| Divide the [[Meatballs|meatballs]] and [[Sauce|sauce]] between the two [[Pizzas|pizzas]], cut the meatballs in half and spread over the [[Pizza|pizza]]\n| Cover with sliced [[Mozzarella cheese|mozzarella cheese]], drizzle with a little [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and [[Bake|bake]] for for 3 to 5 minutes (depending on how hot your [[Oven|oven]] is) or until the [[Cheese|cheese]] browns a little.  Watch it carefully as it's easy to burn at such a high heat.\n| Serve!\n}}\n===Chef's notes===\nLots of supermarkets do chopped tomatoes, flavoured with [[Chili|chili]]/[[Basil|basil]]/[[Oregano|oregano]] etc, and though it's as easy to do this yourself, they are quite handy for [[Pizza|pizza]] toppings.\n\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Pizza recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]][[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#pizza #meatballpizza #meatballs #sauce #pizzastone #grill #pizzas #oliveoil #mozzarellacheese #chili #redwine </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Add more [[Bread crumbs|bread crumbs]] as needed.\n| Place coated bites to the side and repeat for remaining bites.\n| After all bites have been coated, repeat the [[Egg|egg]]-[[Dip|dip]] and [[Crumb|crumb]]-coat for each once more.\n| Place all bites in fryer basket and submerge in 175\u00b0C [[Oil|oil]].\n| Let sit for 30 seconds, gently rocking basket occasionally.\n| Lift basket and let cool for a few seconds. If [[Cheese|cheese]] is not beginning to ooze out from half the sticks, re-submerge in [[Oil|oil]] for another 10-15 seconds, gently shaking the basket. Repeat until the [[Cheese|cheese]] is just starting to ooze out.\n| Dump onto [[Paper towel|paper towel]] and pat off excess [[Oil|oil]] gently.\n}}\n===Recipe source===\n\n* [http://en.wikibooks.org/wiki/Cookbook:Mozzarella_Sticks Wiki cookbook]\n===Variations===\nTry [[Mozzarella sticks]], identical recipe but the result is breaded cheese sticks rather than bites.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Deep fried]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#egg #breadcrumbs #mozzarellabites #cheese #starter #miseenplace #deepfried #deepfatfryer #snack #mozzarella #mozzarellacheese </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Mozzarella sticks a cheese recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#egg #breadcrumbs #mozzarellasticks #cheese #mozzarella #deepfried #dip #snack #crumb #mozzarellacheese #starter \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Recipe for deep fried mozzarella sticks, a great starter or just a tasty snack\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 706\n|PortionCalories = 353\n|DatePublished=8th March 2014\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  20 minutes\n|PrepTime =  15 minutes\n|CookTime =  5 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Mozzarella Sticks recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Oh, love these</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Crunchy, cheesy and gooey. Mmm!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n\nRecipe for [[Deep fried|deep fried]] [[Mozzarella|mozzarella]] sticks, a great [[Starter|starter]] or just a tasty [[Snack|snack]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 113g (\u00bc pound) [[Mozzarella cheese|mozzarella cheese]], drained\n| 118 ml (\u00bd cup) seasoned [[Bread crumbs|bread crumbs]]\n| 1 large [[Egg|egg]]\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Preheat [[Deep fat fryer|deep fat fryer]] to 175\u00b0C (350\u00b0F)\n\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Preheat deep fryer to 350\u00b0F (175\u00b0C).\n| Slice [[Mozzarella|mozzarella]] into sticks 1-3 cm in diameter.\n| In a small bowl, whisk [[Egg|egg]].\n| Fill another small bowl with [[Bread crumbs|bread crumbs]].\n| Dip 3-4 sticks at a time into the [[Egg|egg]].\n| Shake excess [[Egg|egg]] off sticks and place them in the [[Bread crumbs|bread crumbs]].\n| Shake bowl of [[Bread crumbs|bread crumbs]], evenly coating all sticks. Add more [[Bread crumbs|bread crumbs]] as needed.\n| Place coated sticks to the side and repeat for remaining sticks.\n| After all sticks have been coated, repeat the [[Egg|egg]]-[[Dip|dip]] and [[Crumb|crumb]]-coat for each once more.\n| Place all sticks in fryer basket and submerge in 175\u00b0C [[Oil|oil]].\n| Let sit for 30 seconds, gently rocking basket occasionally.\n| Lift basket and let cool for a few seconds. If [[Cheese|cheese]] is not beginning to ooze out from half the sticks, re-submerge in [[Oil|oil]] for another 10-15 seconds, gently shaking the basket. Repeat until the [[Cheese|cheese]] is just starting to ooze out.\n| Dump onto [[Paper towel|paper towel]] and pat off excess [[Oil|oil]] gently.\n}}\n===Recipe source===\n\n* [http://en.wikibooks.org/wiki/Cookbook:Mozzarella_Sticks Wiki cookbook]\n===Variations===\nTry [[Mozzarella bites]], identical recipe but the result is bite-sized nibbles, rather than sticks.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Deep fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#egg #breadcrumbs #mozzarellasticks #cheese #mozzarella #deepfried #dip #snack #crumb #mozzarellacheese #starter </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

/seo -->\n\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1355\n|PortionCalories = 338\n|DatePublished=16th December 2012\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = 4 to 6 people\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 45 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 30 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Mushroom risotto recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Not a risotto fan</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span rice]]\n| 150 ml (1/4 pint) [[Dry white wine|dry white wine]]\n| 1.2 [[Litres|litres]] (2 [[Pints|pints]]) hot [[Vegetable stock|vegetable stock]]\n| 2 tablespoons fresh [[Parsley|parsley]], garnish\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Soak the [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]] in ''just [[Boiled|boiled]]'' water for 10 minutes - reserve the liquor to add to the [[Stock|stock]]\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a large pan and saut\u00e9 the [[Onions|onions]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] for 4 minutes until softened. Add the [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]] and saut\u00e9 for another 4 minutes until coloured\n| Stir in the [[Rice|rice]] and coat well with the [[Oil|oil]]\n| Pour in the [[Wine|wine]] and [[Simmer|simmer]] until it has been absorbed into the [[Rice|rice]]\n| Add a ladle of the [[Stock|stock]], stir gently and [[Simmer|simmer]] until the stock has been absorbed.  Repeat until all the stock has been absorbed and the [[Rice|rice]] is plump and tender.\n| Roughly chop the soaked [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]], stir into the [[Risotto|risotto]] with the [[Butter|butter]].  Season to taste and serve immediately\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe hot with [[Grated|grated]] [[Parmesan cheese]]\n===Chef's notes===\nWhen adding the [[Stock|stock]] a ladle at a time, don't be tempted to hurry this stage. Always wait until the last ladle has been absorbed before adding the next - it's going to take about 20 minutes to complete.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Rice recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#mushrooms #stock #rice #parmesancheese #mushroomrisotto #butter #simmer #grated #vegetablestock #oliveoil #drywhitewine </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

teaspoon made-up [[English mustard]]\n| 150 ml [[Vegetable Stock|vegetable stock]], a [[Stock cube|stock cube]] is fine for this\n| 100g [[Wild rice|wild rice]], rinsed under running water and drained\n| 150 ml [[Creme fraiche|creme fraiche]]\n| 1 teaspoon of [[Dry sherry|dry sherry]]\n| Half a [[Lemon|lemon]] cut into [[Wedges|wedges]]\n| A handful of [[Green beans|green beans]], trimmed and halved\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Cook the [[Wild rice|wild rice]] as instructed on the packet. Note that [[Wild rice|wild rice]] can take as long as 50 minutes to cook properly so you may need to adjust the stroganoff cooking time appropriately\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a [[Wok|wok]] or saucepan and give a good grind of [[Black pepper|black pepper]], add the [[Onions|onions]] and gently [[Fry|fry]] for about 5 minutes or until translucent.\n| Add the [[Crushed garlic|crushed garlic]] and [[Fry|fry]] for another 2 minutes.\n| Add the sliced [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]] and [[Saute|saute]] for 6 minutes, turning now and then.\n| Add the [[Mustard|mustard]] and [[Paprika powder|paprika powder]] and mix well, then pour over the [[Stock|stock]]. Ensure the [[Stock|stock]] is well mixed and [[Simmer|simmer]] for about 5 minutes.\n| Meanwhile cook the [[Beans|beans]] for about 6 minutes in [[Boiling|boiling]] water.\n| Add the [[Creme fraiche|creme fraiche]] together with the [[Juice|juice]] from &#188; of the [[Lemon|lemon]] and stir well.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with the [[Wild rice|wild rice]] and [[Green beans|green beans]]\n===Recipe source===\n\n* Based on a recipe seen on bbc.co.uk/food\n===Variations===\nUse [[Sour cream|sour cream]] instead of [[Creme fraiche|creme fraiche]]\n===Chef's notes===\nDon't add any extra salt without tasting first as [[Vegetable Stock|vegetable stock]] from a cube tends to be rather salty.\n\nIf you want to thicken the sauce, mix a little of the [[Stock|stock]] with a level teaspoon of [[Cornflour|cornflour]] and stir back in at stage 5 and mix well.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Rice recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#wildrice #cremefraiche #mushroomstroganoffwithgreenbeansandwildrice #stock #fry #paprikapowder #lemon #mushrooms #vegetablestock #greenbeans #vegetarian </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Ikea meatballs are great but balls of sausage-meat work are a favourite for these pizzas here at home.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nHaving just got my [[Pizza stone|pizza stone]], I am rushing around trying to find [[Pizzas|pizzas]] that are really well suited to 'the stone'.\n\nThis one uses the [[Grill|grill]], a pizza stone and the oven so it's as close to a proper pizza oven as you can get.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 portion [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]] - Makes 2 pizzas\n| 150 g ball of [[Mozzarella cheese|mozzarella cheese]], torn into pieces\n| 1 spicy pepperoni-style [[sausage]]\n| 300g cooked [[Meatballs|meatballs]] - (I used turkey and chicken meatballs from Waitrose - delicious)\n| [[Extra virgin olive oil]] for drizzling\n| 3 [[Cloves garlic, crushed|cloves garlic, crushed]]\n| 1 cup [[Spicy tomato sauce|spicy tomato sauce]]\n| Handful of [[Basil leaves|basil leaves]], torn\n| 1 tablespoon [[Pickled|pickled]] [[Capers|capers]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Fine yellow cornmeal|fine yellow cornmeal]]\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Make the [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]] as instructed\n* If using a [[pizza stone]], preheat the [[pizza stone]] under a very hot [[grill]] for about 20 minutes.  Place it about 8cm (3\") from the heat source.\n\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Make 1 pizza per person\n| Dust the work surface with [[Fine yellow cornmeal|fine yellow cornmeal]]\n| Stretch or roll the [[Dough|dough]] into two thin rounds\n| Sprinkle the stone with [[Fine yellow cornmeal|fine yellow cornmeal]]\n| Prick the pizza all over with a fork. This prevents it puffing up too much and burning while it is cooking\n| Pre-cook the empty pizza base on one side only for about 3 minutes or until it is lightly browned\n| Remove from the oven, flip and add the topping.\n| Lightly [[Oil|oil]] one side of the [[Pizza|pizza]] and [[Grill|grill]], oiled side down, flip an repeat, about 2 minutes per side\n| Drizzle the [[Pizza|pizza]] with [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and spread the pizza with &frac12; of the [[Tomato sauce|tomato sauce]]\n| Top with torn [[Mozzarella|mozzarella]], Crushed [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Sausage|sausage]] and [[Meatballs|meatballs]]\n| [[Bake]] for 3 or 4  minutes or until the [[Cheese|cheese]] browns a little - watch it carefully as it can burn easily.\n| Remove and sprinkle with torn [[Basil|basil]] and [[Capers|capers]]\n| Keep the fist pizza warm at the bottom of the oven whilst you make the second.\n| Serve hot\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:New York-style stone baked pizza ready.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Ready to go back in the oven\nImage:New York-style stone baked pizza base.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Stone baked base resting while the other base is cooking\n</gallery>\n===Chef's note===\nIf you don't have a [[pizza peel]] use an upturned plate, dusted with [[Fine yellow cornmeal|fine yellow cornmeal]] and some deft handwork to slide the dough onto the stone.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pizza recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#newyorkstylestonebakedpizza #fineyellowcornmeal #pizzastone #grill #meatballs #pizzas #pizza #pizzadough #sausage #capers #pizzapeel </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "New York style calzone pizza",

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=New York style calzone pizza a cheese recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#provolonecheese #pizzas #parmesancheese #meats #pizzadough #pizzastone #newyorkstylecalzonepizza #unusualrecipes #bake #dip #homesmokedbacon \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=You can fill this spicy calzone with just about anything\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1866\n|PortionCalories = 933\n|DatePublished=1st November 2012\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 2 plus some breakfast pizza!\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  1 hour 25 minutes<br />Includes making the dough\n|PrepTime = 1 hour 15 minutes  \n|CookTime =  10 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Goat's cheese and asparagus calzone pizza recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n}}\n\nYou can fill this spicy calzone with just about anything. For this version, I have used a packet of sliced speciality cold [[Meats|meats]], pepperoni, [[Salami|salami]], [[Prosciutto|prosciutto]] and [[Home smoked bacon|Home smoked bacon]].  Use what you have available but don't try to over-fill the [[Pizzas|pizzas]]!\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 portion [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]]\n| 1 portion [[Spicy tomato pizza topping|spicy tomato pizza topping]] (use a jar of shop-bought [[Pizza|pizza]] [[Sauce|sauce]] if you're pushed for time)\n| 150 g selection of quality sliced meats from the [[deli counter]]\n| 250g [[Provolone cheese|provolone cheese]], sliced\n| 20 g (&frac14; cup) [[Parmesan cheese]], freshly [[Grated|grated]]\n| [[Basil leaves]] to garnish\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the oven to 230\u00b0 C (450\u00b0 F - gas 8) using a [[Pizza stone|pizza stone]] if possible\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Divide your [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]] into two balls and roll out into two 20 cm (8\") rounds\n| Spread one half of the base with the [[Spicy tomato sauce|spicy tomato sauce]]\n| Layer the [[Provolone cheese|provolone cheese]] and the sliced [[Meats|meats]], sprinkling with [[Parmesan cheese]]\n| Fold the pizza over so it creates a semi-circle and seal the edge by crimping rolling over, starting from one corner. A short [[Calzone folding|how-to guide is here]].\n| [[Brush]] the seal and the surface with [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| Cut 3 small slits in the top to allow [[Steam|steam]] to escape\n| Dust the [[Pizza stone|pizza stone]] with [[Fine yellow cornmeal|fine yellow cornmeal]]\n| [[Bake]] for 10 minutes\n| Remove and let the [[Pizzas|pizzas]] rest for 5 miutes\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with a [[Salad|salad]].  If there is any [[Tomato sauce|tomato sauce]] left over after making the [[Pizzas|pizzas]], warm it up and serve with the pizzas as a [[Dip|dip]]\n===Variations===\nUse [[Mozzarella cheese|mozzarella cheese]] if you can't get [[Provolone cheese|provolone cheese]]\n\nI love en egg inside a [[calzone]] pizza, but often find that it often does not cook properly, so a neat cheat is to [[Poached eggs|poach the egg]] in water beforehand.  I'm sure no self-respecting pizza chef would do that but it works for me!\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Like a Cornish pastie..</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">..but much, much nicer!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Pizza recipes]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#provolonecheese #pizzas #parmesancheese #meats #pizzadough #pizzastone #newyorkstylecalzonepizza #unusualrecipes #bake #dip #homesmokedbacon </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "New York style deli pizza",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=New York style deli pizza a cheese recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#pizzastone #pizzadough #newyorkstyledelipizza #basilleaves #pizzas #mozzarellacheese #parmesancheese #dip #meats #cheese #sauce \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=As with any pizza, you can make it with almost any ingredients. Try and keep the quantities about the same though\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1177\n|PortionCalories = 294\n|DatePublished=6th November 2012\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 4 - Makes two large [[Pizzas|pizzas]]\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  1 hour 25 minutes<br />Includes making the dough\n|PrepTime = 1 hour 15 minutes  \n|CookTime =  10 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Pizza stone-used.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Almost as good!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.7</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Not quite New York, but almost!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nAs with any pizza, you can make it with almost any ingredients. Try and keep the quantities about the same though.  You can end up with a damp soggy pizza if you overdo the [[cheese]].\n[[Image:New York style deli pizza ready to cook.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Ready to cook]]\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 portion [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]] - makes 2 pizzas\n| 1/2 portion [[Spicy tomato pizza topping|spicy tomato pizza topping]] (use a jar of shop-bought [[Pizza|pizza]] [[Sauce|sauce]] if you're pushed for time)\n| 150g [[Mozzarella cheese]], torn into pieces\n| 100g from a selection of good quality sliced meats from the [[deli counter]]\n| 25g of [[Parmesan cheese]], freshly [[Grated|grated]]\n| Olive oil\n| [[Basil leaves]] to garnish\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Make the [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]] as instructed\n* If using a [[pizza stone]], preheat the [[pizza stone]] under a very hot [[grill]] for about 20 minutes.  Place it about 8cm (3\") from the heat source.\n\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Make 1 pizza per person\n| Preheat the oven to 230\u00b0 C (450\u00b0 F - gas 8) or about 9 cm (3\") from a very hot grill if using a [[Pizza stone|pizza stone]]\n| Dust the work surface with [[Fine yellow cornmeal|fine yellow cornmeal]] and divide your [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]] into two balls and roll out into two 20 cm (8\") rounds\n| Prick the pizza all over with a fork. This prevents it puffing up too much and burning while it is cooking.\n| Pre-cook the pizza base for about 3 minutes on one side only if using a [[pizza stone]], then remove from the oven, flip and add the topping\n| Spread the [[Spicy tomato sauce|spicy tomato sauce]] on the surface of the pizza\n| Layer the sliced [[Meats|meats]] and [[Mozzarella cheese]] onto the pizza and sprinkle with [[Parmesan cheese]]\n| Drizzle with [[olive oil]]\n| [[Bake]] for about 9 to 10 minutes or until the base is crispy and the cheese has melted\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nGarnish with the [[basil leaves]] and serve with a [[Salad|salad]].  If there is any [[Tomato sauce|tomato sauce]] left over after making the [[Pizzas|pizzas]], warm it up and serve with the pizzas as a [[Dip|dip]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Pizza recipes]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#pizzastone #pizzadough #newyorkstyledelipizza #basilleaves #pizzas #mozzarellacheese #parmesancheese #dip #meats #cheese #sauce </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }

Add a glug of [[Balsamic vinegar|balsamic vinegar]]. [[Bubble]] again. Fold in [[Fresh herbs|fresh herbs]]\n==See also==\n\n* [https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Vd3yG_HGl60 Abel & Cole 'how to' video for this recipe]\n{{LasagneRecipes}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Pasta recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Cookery cheats]]\n[[Category:Gluten free recipes]]\n[[Category:Abel and Cole veg box recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n{{Template:Abel and Cole veg box recipes attribution}}\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#courgettes #nopastalasagne #bubble #basil #parmesan #pinenuts #mozzarella #oliveoil #tomatosauce #pastasauce #images </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Olive bread",
                "revisions": [
                    {

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Olive bread, Italian recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#dough #olive #olivebread #oliveoil #bread #flour #strongwholemealflour #yeast #whitebread #kneadingbread #celsius \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Start this delicious bread 2 or 3 days before you want it. It takes a while to make, but is worth it\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1254\n|PortionCalories = 125\n|DatePublished=27th October 2012\n|Author = JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Servings: 10 - Makes 1 large loaf\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 2 days, 1 hour, 50 minutes\n |PrepTime = 2 days, 1 hour 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 35 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Olive bread recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Delightful flavour</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.3</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Lots of effert and time, but worth it!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n\nStart this delicious bread 2 or 3 days before you want it.  It takes a while to make, but is worth it.  \n\nThe recipe is adapted from one by Andrew Whitley's book '''Bread Matters''' (ISBN 0007298498).\n\n'''For the sponge:'''\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 3g fresh [[Yeast|yeast]]\n| 150ml water at about 20 [[Degrees|degrees]] [[Celsius|celsius]]\n| 75g strong, [[White bread|white bread]] [[Flour|flour]]\n| 75g [[Strong wholemeal flour|strong wholemeal flour]]\n| For the [[Dough|dough]]:\n| 225g sponge, taken from the above\n| 150g strong, [[White bread|white bread]] [[Flour|flour]]\n| 75g [[Strong wholemeal flour|strong wholemeal flour]]\n| 4g finely [[Ground|ground]] [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| 15ml [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 105ml water\n}}\n'''For the [[Bread|bread]]:'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 30g [[Pumpkin seeds|pumpkin seeds]]\n| 20ml [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| The [[Dough|dough]] from above\n| 90g black [[Olive|olive]] paste\n}}\n===Method===\n\n\n'''The sponge:'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Dissolve the [[Yeast|yeast]] in the water and pour into a large bowl.\n| Mix in the [[Flours|flours]]. cover with a lid or plastic bag and leave at room temperature for 16-48 hours.\n}}\n'''The [[Dough|dough]]:'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Mix together all of the ingredients and [[Kneading bread|knead]] until the [[Dough|dough]] is stretchy and silky.\n| Return to the bowl, cover and leave to rise until double its size.\n}}\n'''The [[Bread|bread]]:'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| [[Knock back]] the [[Dough|dough]] and incorporate the [[Seeds|seeds]] and the [[Olive oil|olive oil]].\n| On a lightly dusted worksurface or [[Pastry mat|pastry mat]], roll out the [[Dough|dough]] until is measures about 20 x 30cm.\n| Spread the [[Olive|olive]] paste over the [[Dough|dough]] and roll up like a [[Swiss]] roll.\n| Tuck each end under the middle until they meet underneath.\n| Place in a 1kg greased loaf tin and allow to rise until it has almost doubled in size.  \n| [[Bake]] at 190\u00b0 C (375\u00b0 F - gas 5) for about 35 minutes.\n}}\n===Chef's notes===\nBlack [[Olive|olive]] paste can be bought in Sainsbury's.  The [[Dough|dough]] will feel very oily, but that is fine.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#dough #olive #olivebread #oliveoil #bread #flour #strongwholemealflour #yeast #whitebread #kneadingbread #celsius </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Olive oil bread",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Olive oil bread, Italian recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#dough #flour #yeast #oliveoil #oliveoilbread #dried #breadmaker #knead #semolina #oregano #driedyeast \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This is a focaccia type recipe but the dimples are irregular there are not so many of them\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1405\n|PortionCalories = 140\n|DatePublished=27th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Servings: 10 - Makes 1 loaf\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 14 hours 30 minutes\n |PrepTime = 14 hours\n |CookTime = 30 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Olive oil bread recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Nice snacking bread</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Lovely recipe Julia.</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]]</span></span>\n}}\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n\nThis is a [[Focaccia|focaccia]] type recipe but the dimples are irregular there are not so many of them.  I have started by making an overnight sponge, to encourage [[Yeast|yeast]] acitivity, but you can omit that stage if you like amd mix in all the ingredients at the same time.\n\nSee 'Variations' below for instructions on partially or fully making this [[Bread|bread]] in a [[Breadmaker|breadmaker]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 15g fresh [[Yeast|yeast]] or 1x7g sachet of fast-action [[Dried yeast|dried yeast]]\n| 320g [[Sparkling mineral water|sparkling mineral water]]\n| 500g [[Strong white bread flour|strong white bread flour]]\n| 20g [[Semolina|semolina]]\n| 10g [[Salt|salt]]\n| 50g [[Olive oil|olive oil]] + 4 tbsps, plus a little extra for [[Brushing|brushing]]\n| Coarse [[Rock|rock]] or [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| [[Dried]] or fresh [[oregano]], to taste\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Make an overnight sponge by dissolving the [[Yeast|yeast]] in the water and mixing into half the [[Flour|flour]] and all the [[Semolina|semolina]] - if using [[Dried yeast|dried yeast]], just stir it in with the [[Flour|flour]] before adding the water.\n| The following morning, mix in the remaining [[Flour|flour]], [[Salt|salt]] and 50g [[Olive oil|olive oil]] to form a sticky [[Dough|dough]], adding more water if necessary.\n| [[Knead]], using your chosen method.\n| Shape into a ball and leave to rest in a lightly oiled bowl, until almost double its size.\n| Lightly [[Flour|flour]] the worksurface and empty the [[Dough|dough]] onto it.\n| Gently deflate the [[Dough|dough]] and [[knead]] briefly.\n| Repeat steps 4-6, omitting the kneading.\n| Lightly [[Oil|oil]] a pie dish (see Chef's notes below) and place the [[Dough|dough]] in the pie dish.\n| Drizzle the 4 tablespoons [[Oil|oil]] over the top and push the [[Dough|dough]] gently towards the sides of the dish.\n| Cover with [[Clingfilm|clingfilm]] and leave to prove for 45 minutes.\n| Dimple the [[Dough|dough]] sporadically and prove for a further 30 minutes.\n| Meanwhile, preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 220\u00b0 C (425\u00b0 F - gas 7), [fan oven 200\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour].\n| Sprinkle the [[Dough|dough]] with the [[Oregano|oregano]] and coarse sea or [[Rock salt|rock salt]].\n| [[Bake]] in the [[Oven|oven]] for 25-30 minutes.\n| Slide onto a wire rack and [[Brush|brush]] with a little more [[Olive oil|olive oil]] whilst still hot.\n| Allow to cool before cutting or tearing.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nThis is delicious on its own, no [[Butter|butter]] needed so very healthy!  Good with [[Cheese|cheese]] and [[Salad|salad]].\n===Variations===\nYou can add other ingredients to it such as [[Herbs|herbs]], Crushed [[Garlic|garlic]] or [[Dried|dried]] [[Chilli flakes|chilli flakes]].  Also experiment with different [[Oils|oils]] such as [[Avocado oil|avocado oil]], but make sure they have a fairly high smoke point.\n\nYou can make the whole thing in a [[Breadmaker|breadmaker]], but you will have a brick shaped loaf.  However, you can use it to do the hard work for stages 2-7.  In either case, select the Italian setting or the setting for which you have a [[Focaccia|focaccia]] recipe in the manufacturer's recipe booklet.  For the [[Panasonic SD-ZB2502 automatic breadmaker]], use menu option 21, French dough rise.\n===Chef's notes===\nThe tin I used to make this bread is made by Falcon,  It is an '''[http://www.amazon.co.uk/Falcon-Enamel-24cm-Oblong-Dish/dp/B000TAVXYI/ref=sr_1_3?ie=UTF8&qid=1310850610&sr=8-3 enamel pie dish]''' measuring 24cm and is just right for this bread.  \n\nThese dishes are easy to clean - if anything sticks, just soak in hot water for a short while.  They are also very inexpensive.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Breadmaker recipes]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]][[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#dough #flour #yeast #oliveoil #oliveoilbread #dried #breadmaker #knead #semolina #oregano #driedyeast </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }

title": "Onion focaccia",
                "revisions": [
                    {

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Onion focaccia, Italian recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#onionfocaccia #oliveoil #bake #yeast #knockback #dough #clingfilm #bread #flour #blackpepper #frenchbread \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A very easy and basic focaccia recipe\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 949\n|PortionCalories = 94\n|DatePublished=8th March 2013\n|Author = JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Servings: 10 - Makes one loaf\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 4 hours 25 minutes\n |PrepTime = 4 hours\n |CookTime = 25 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Onion focaccia recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Lovely loaf Julia</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.8</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Makes a fabulous starter, warmed with real butter.</span> \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Chef|Jerry]] </span></span>\n}}\nA very easy and basic [[Focaccia|focaccia]] recipe.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 350g strong [[Bread|bread]] [[Flour|flour]] (I used Wessex Mill [[French bread]] [[Flour]] - similar to Type 65)\n| &frac12; teaspoons [[Salt|salt]]\n| 1 x 7g sachet Easy-[[Bake]] [[Yeast|yeast]], or 15g fresh yeast\n| 200ml water\n| 1 tablespoon [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| &frac12; [[Red onion|red onion]], finely chopped\n| Maldon [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and freshly ground [[black pepper]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* If using fresh [[Yeast|yeast]], activate in the water.\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Mix the first 5 ingredients and [[Kneading bread|knead]] thoroughly.\n| Place in a bowl, covered with some oiled [[Clingfilm|clingfilm]] and put in a [[warm place]] until risen to double its size.\n| On a floured board, [[Knock back|knock back]], knead, return to the bowl and allow to rise again to double its size.\n| [[Knock back]] and place in a suitable receptacle, eg a shallow, greased 25cm cake tin - I used a rectangular Falcon enamel [[Pie dish|pie dish]].\n| Cover again in [[Clingfilm|clingfilm]] and let it rise until twice the height.\n| Preheat your [[Oven|oven]] to 200\u00b0 C (400\u00b0 F - gas 6), and 10 minutes before you want to [[Bake|bake]] it, push your fingers into the [[Dough|dough]] to make some dimples.\n| Sprinkle the [[Dough|dough]] with the [[Onions|onions]], [[Salt|salt]], [[black pepper]] and [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and leave to prove for 10 minutes.\n| [[Bake]] for 20-25 minutes until golden and leave to cool on a wire rack.\n}}\n===Variations===\nAdd [[Herbs|herbs]], [[Spices|spices]] etc of your choice.\n===Chef's notes===\nIn theory you should use lukewarm water, but I made this with [[Sparkling mineral water|sparkling mineral water]] straight from the [[Fridge|fridge]].  It takes a lot longer to prove, but a longer [[Fermentation|fermentation]] makes a better [[Bread|bread]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Foacaccia]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes|Foacaccia]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Foacaccia]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking|Foacaccia]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes|Foacaccia]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Foacaccia]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#onionfocaccia #oliveoil #bake #yeast #knockback #dough #clingfilm #bread #flour #blackpepper #frenchbread </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]

                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Ossobuco alla Milanese a beef recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#vealshanks #gremolata #butter #celery #garlic #onion #beefstock #onions #carrots #tomato #carrot \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Ossobuco (Italian for 'holed bone'), in English often spelled osso buco or osso bucco, is a Milanese speciality of veal shanks cooked in meat broth\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 4979\n|PortionCalories = 1244\n|DatePublished=28th July 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = Ossobuco, finished\n |Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 3\n |TotalTime = 2 hours 45 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 2 hours 30 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Ossobuco.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Winter warmer</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">3.9</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Superb with rustic bread.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n'''Ossobuco''' (Italian for 'holed bone'), in English often spelled '''osso buco''' or '''osso bucco''', is a Milanese speciality of [[veal shanks]] cooked in meat broth and flavoured with [[white wine]]. Slowly braised, this relatively tough, yet flavourful cut of meat becomes meltingly tender, and the connective tissues and [[Marrowbone|marrow]] dissolve into the sauce, making it rich and creamy.\n[[Image:Ossobuco ready to cook.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Ready to go]]\n\nThe shank is a relatively cheap cut of [[veal]] which is readily available in most good supermarkets and butcher shops. Look for meaty hind-shanks cut from the top of the thigh with a high proportion of meat-to-bone; each piece should be about 5\" across and 1\" to 1&frac12;\" thick.\n\nTraditionally, '''ossobuco''' is made without [[tomatoes]] (these being unknown in Milan until the late 19th century). However, the traditional version, prepared with [[cinnamon]], [[allspice]], [[bay leaf]] and [[gremolata]] called in bianco, has by and large been replaced with the newer version which includes [[tomatoes]] and the 'holy trinity' of Italian cooking: [[carrot]], [[celery]] and [[onion]], flavoured with a [[bouquet garni]] and without [[gremolata]] (although 'hybrid' versions exist which include both [[tomato]] and [[gremolata]]). It should be noted that while the traditional combination with [[risotto alla milanese]] is perfect for the former version (for which is was intended), the modern-day version with [[tomato]], which is both moister and bolder in flavour and does not combine well with [[saffron]], is better served with [[polenta]]. The following recipe is for a 'modern' version.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 4 slices [[veal hind shank]], about 1\" to 1&frac12;\" (2.5cm to 4cm) thick\n| 1 medium [[onion]], chopped finely\n| 3 ribs [[celery]] with leaves, chopped finely\n| 1 medium [[carrot]], chopped finely\n| 2 [[cloves garlic, crushed]]\n| 3 tablespoons [[butter]]\n| 4 tablespoons [[olive oil]]\n| 1 cup (240ml) dry white [[wine]] or white [[vermouth]]\n| 2 cups (about 480ml) [[beef stock]]\n| 3 tablespoons [[tomato puree]]\n| 6 [[anchovy]] fillets, mashed\n| &frac12; teaspoon dried [[thyme]]\n| 2-3 [[bay leaves]]\n| 2 strips [[lemon]] peel\n| [[Sea salt]]\n| Freshly ground [[black pepper]]\n| [[Plain  flour]]\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat oven to 175\u00b0C (350\u00b0F - gas 4).\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| If the butcher has not done so, tie the [[veal shanks]] around the middle with [[kitchen twine]]; this will keep them from falling apart during cooking.\n| Choose a heavy, covered roasting pan or [[Dutch oven]] which will just accommodate the [[veal shanks]] in one layer. Put the [[butter]], 2 tablespoons of the oil, the [[onions]], [[celery]] and [[carrots]] in the pan and [[saut\u00e9]] over medium heat until the vegetables have wilted, about 8 minutes. Add the [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[lemon peel]] and saut\u00e9 until they're fragrant, about 2 minutes more. Remove from the heat.\n| Meanwhile, heat the remaining oil in a skillet until it is near the smoking point. Lightly flour the [[veal shanks]] and slip them into the oil. Richly brown the [[veal shanks]] on both of the cut sides, then place them in the roasting pan on top of the vegetables.\n| Place the wine in the skillet and boil until reduced by one-half, [[deglaze]] the pan, scraping up any brown residue. Pour this over the [[veal shanks]].\n| Heat the [[beef stock]] to a boil in the skillet, whisking in the [[tomato puree]] and [[anchovies]]. Add this to the [[veal shanks]], along with the herbs, several grindings of [[pepper]], and a large pinch of [[salt]]. The liquid should cover &frac34; of the shanks. If not, add extra water.\n| Bring the pot to a simmer, cover, and place in the oven. Cook for approximately 2 hours, turning and basting the shanks every &frac12; hour. If you notice that the cooking liquids have nearly evaporated, add hot water, about &frac12; cup at a time. The veal is done when it is fork tender and falling from the bone.\n| Transfer the shanks to a platter, remove the strings, and cover to keep warm. If the sauce seems watery, as is probable, place the pan on the stove top over high heat and reduce the cooking liquid until the sauce has a thick, creamy consistency. Pour the sauce over the shanks and serve.\n}}\n== Chef's notes ==\n* The recipe calls for [[anchovies]], which enrich the finished sauce without adding a \"fishy\" flavour: don't omit them, even should you not be fond of anchovies.\n* Traditionally, the cooking sauce is finished with a mixture of [[Garlic|garlic]], [[lemon zest]] and [[parsley]] called ''Gremolata.'' It adds a burst of freshness to the finished dish and is highly recommended. [[Gremolata]] consists of the grated zest of one [[lemon]], one finely minced clove of [[Garlic|garlic]], and one tablespoon of finely chopped [[parsley]]. Add this mixture to the sauce at the end of the cooking, as it's being reduced.\n* Osso buco is almost ''always'' served with [[risotto]]&ndash;indeed; it's one of the few examples in Italian cooking where a starch is served with the main course and is a marriage that no man should put asunder. One may, for a change, substitute [[orzo]] or [[acini de pepe]] cooked in [[meat stock]] and finished with [[butter]] and [[Parmesan cheese]].\n===Pictured version===\nThis was a complete success, though a few notes are in order:\n\nAs always, the recipe was made with what we had 'in stock'.\n* 1 very thick steak was easily sufficient for 2\n* 1 big leek instead of the [[onions]]\n* 4 lovely thin [[carrots]] (two sliced, two left as-is)\n* 2 teaspoons of [[Marigold vegetable stock]] in two coffee mugs boiling water\n* 3 tablespoons of [[cornmeal]], I prefer it to [[flour]]\nThis went wonderfully with fresh crusty bread.\n==See also==\n* [[Slow roast recipes]]\n\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Beef recipes]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Stews and casseroles]]\n[[Category:Veal recipes]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Stewed, braised or pot roasted]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#vealshanks #gremolata #butter #celery #garlic #onion #beefstock #onions #carrots #tomato #carrot </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }

This has been adapted for Thermomix...\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|DatePublished=31st December 2016\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = 10\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  25 hours\n|PrepTime =  24 hours\n|CookTime =  1 hour\n|TotalCalories = 780\n|PortionCalories = 78\n|Image = [[Image:The new (2014) Thermomix TM5.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Cheesey bread</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Great for a sausage sandwich</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}{{Template:WorkInProgress}}\nA [[Wheat|wheat]] and [[Rye|rye]] [[Bread|bread]] recipe from [[Italy]], with added [[Parmesan cheese]] and made using the [[Tang zhong|tang zhong]] method.  This has been adapted for [[Thermomix]].\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 30g [[White bread|white bread]] [[Flour|flour]]\n| 150g water\n| 7g sachet [[Dried|dried]] fast action [[Yeast|yeast]]\n| A further 270g of [[White bread|white bread]] [[Flour|flour]]\n| 200g [[Rye flour|rye flour]]\n| 100g [[Parmesan]], [[Grated|grated]] \n| 9g [[Salt|salt]]\n| A further 225g water\n| Extra [[Parmesan]], [[Grated|grated]]\n| [[Polenta]]\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Put the 30g [[Flour|flour]] and 150g water into the bowl '''5 minutes / 65\u00b0C / Speed 4''', reducing to '''Speed 2''' after 2 minutes.\n| Leave to cool to room temperature.\n| Add the [[Yeast|yeast]], [[Flours|flours]], [[Grated|grated]] [[Parmesan]], [[Salt|salt]] and the 225g water to the bowl '''20 secs / Speed 4'''.\n| Then '''4 minutes / [[Knead]]'''.\n| Shape into a ball and place in a lightly oiled bowl.\n| Cover and leave to rise in the [[Fridge|fridge]] - this could be overnight or for several hours.\n| Remove the [[Dough|dough]] from the [[Fridge|fridge]] and bring up to room temperature.\n| Shape and place in either a 1kg loaf tin or [[Banneton|banneton]] which has been greased and lightly coated with [[Polenta|polenta]].\n| Cover the tin or [[Banneton|banneton]] with oiled [[Cling Film|cling film]] and leave to [[Prove|prove]].\n| Pre-heat the [[Oven|oven]] to 190\u00b0 C (375\u00b0 F - gas 5), [fan oven 170\u00b0 C ].\n| If using a [[Banneton|banneton]], carefully invert the [[Dough|dough]] onto a [[Baking tray|baking tray]] or stone, which has been sprinkled with more [[Polenta|polenta]].\n| Sprinkle the [[Dough|dough]] with [[Grated|grated]] [[Parmesan]] and [[Bake|bake]] for xx minutes.\n| Turn out of the tine or remove from the [[Baking tray|baking tray]] and leave to cool thoroughly before slicing\n}}\n===Chef's notes===\nYou can use coarse [[Semolina|semolina]] instead of [[Polenta|polenta]]. Do not exceed 9g [[salt]] because the [[Parmesan]] is salty in itself.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#parmesan #grated #polenta #banneton #dough #flour #yeast #whitebread #fridge #bakingtray #tangzhong </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "\n<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Panforte recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#panforte #cake #icingsugar #honey #rice #groundcinnamon #bake #melon #plainflour #butter #greaseproofpaper \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Panforte is a traditional spiced cake from Siena in Tuscany, which is often consumed at Christmas and other special occasions.\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|DatePublished=23rd November 2016\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = 6\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  40 minutes\n|PrepTime =  10 minutes\n|CookTime =  50 minutes\n|TotalCalories = 3368\n|PortionCalories = 561\n|Image = [[Image:Tes recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Nicer than Christmas Cake!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">\ud83e\udd36\ud83e\udd36\ud83e\udd36</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nPanforte is a traditional spiced [[Cake|cake]] from Siena in Tuscany, which is often consumed at Christmas and other special occasions.  It comes in two varieties:\n\nDark - the top is coated in [[Spices|spices]] and contains candied [[Melon|melon]]\n\nWhite - the top is sprinkled with [[Sugar|sugar]]\n\nThe white sort is often called 'Panforte Margherita' and was so named in honour of the visit to Siena of Queen Margherita of Savoy in 1879.  It is this variety which is most commonly seen today and is the subject of this recipe.\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 50g clear [[Honey|honey]], preferably [[Italian]] wildflower (millefiori)\n| 230g [[Muscovado sugar|muscovado sugar]]\n| 140g [[Plain flour|plain flour]]\n| 230g whole [[Almonds|almonds]], unpeeled\n| 350g [[Candied peel|candied peel]]\n| 3 [[Oranges|oranges]], [[Zest|zest]] only, [[Grated|grated]]\n| \u00bd teaspoon [[Ground cinnamon|ground cinnamon]]\n| \u00bc teaspoon [[Ground|ground]] [[Nutmeg|nutmeg]]\n| \u00bc teaspoon [[Ground cloves|ground cloves]]\n| \u00bc teaspoon [[Ground black pepper|ground black pepper]]\n| 70ml water\n| [[Rice]] paper, for lining the bottom of the [[Cake|cake]] tin\n| [[Icing Sugar|icing sugar]] for dusting\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Pre-heat the [[Oven|oven]] to  170\u00b0 C (gas 3), [fan oven 150\u00b0 C]\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Lin the base of a 20cm / 8in [[Cake|cake]] tin with [[Rice|rice]] paper.\n| Line the sides with [[Greaseproof paper|greaseproof paper]] and grease with [[Butter|butter]] or [[Groundnut oil|groundnut oil]] (Vegans) or use [[Bake-O-Glide]].\n| In a large pan, melt the [[Honey|honey]] and [[Sugar|sugar]] over a medium heat - do not allow to burn.\n| In a bowl, mix all of the remaining ingredients, except the water and [[Icing Sugar|icing sugar]].\n| Once the mixture in the [[Saucepan|saucepan]] is bubbling, stir in the [[Fruit|fruit]] mixture and the water.\n| Carry on cooking until the mixture takes on a slightly sticky texture.\n| Pour into the [[Cake|cake]] tin and [[Bake|bake]] for about 35 minutes.\n| Allow to cool and dust with sifted [[Icing Sugar|icing sugar]].\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nCut into [[Wedges|wedges]] and serve as it is, with [[Tea|tea]] or [[Coffee|coffee]].  It can also be served instead of Christmas [[Cake|cake]] or pudding, in which case, a dollop of Chantilly [[Cream|cream]] would be lovely.\n===Recipe Source===\n[http://eur-lex.europa.eu/LexUriServ/LexUriServ.do?uri=OJ:C:2012:231:0006:0011:EN:PDF European Commission: IGP Panforte di Siena documentation]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes]]\n[[Category:Sweets and desserts]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Fruit recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#panforte #cake #icingsugar #honey #rice #groundcinnamon #bake #melon #plainflour #butter #greaseproofpaper </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

'Rustiche' meaning rustic, refers to the pasta which has ridges down the length of it\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2430\n|PortionCalories = 607\n|DatePublished=25th October 2012\n|Author = JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 50 minutes\n |PrepTime = 30 minutes (roasting peppers included)\n |CookTime = 20 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Pappardelle rustiche all'amatriciana recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">I made this with fresh home-made pasta</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Just rolled out and slashed into pappardelle-type strips</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Pappardelle rustiche.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Pappardelle rustiche]]\nPapperdelle with [[Tomato|tomato]] and [[Bacon|bacon]] [[Sauce|sauce]].  'Rustiche' meaning rustic, refers to the [[Pasta|pasta]] which has ridges down the length of it.  This recipe is usually made with [[Spaghetti|spaghetti]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 120g [[Pancetta|pancetta]] or streaky [[Bacon|bacon]], cut into thin strips\n| [[Olive oil]]\n| 1 [[Onion|onion]], finely sliced\n| [[Garlic]] to taste, chopped\n| 500g ripe [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], finely chopped\n| 2 [[Roasted red peppers|roasted red peppers]], finely chopped\n| [[Salt]]\n| 400g pappardelle rustiche\n| 20g [[Parmesan cheese]], [[Grated|grated]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat a little [[Oil|oil]] in a pan and gently cook the [[Pancetta|pancetta]] or [[Bacon|bacon]].\n| Add the [[Onion|onion]] and the [[Garlic|garlic]] and allow turn golden.\n| Add the tomates, season and cook until the [[Sauce|sauce]] is done.\n| Meanwhile, [[Boil|boil]] the [[Pasta|pasta]] in plenty of [[Salted|salted]] [[Boiling|boiling]] water for 10 minutes, or until [[Al dente|al dente]].\n| Drain, and place in a serving bowl.\n| Add the [[Sauce|sauce]], tossing it lightly and sprinkle with some [[Parmesan]].\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Salad|salad]].\n===Variations===\nAdd some [[Chillies|chillies]] or [[Ginger|ginger]] if you want to [[Spice|spice]] it up a bit.\n===Chef's notes===\n{{Template:ThinkPig}}\n\n{{Template:YoutubePastaDough}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pasta recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]][[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#sauce #bacon #pappardellerusticheallamatriciana #pancetta #garlic #pasta #onion #boiling #spice #salted #panfried </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

The second rising and baking are not\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1313\n|PortionCalories = 656\n|DatePublished=8th March 2013\n|Author = JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = 2 small loaves\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 1 day, 2 hours\n |PrepTime = 1 day\n |CookTime = 2 hours\n |Image = [[Image:Parmesan ciabatta recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">A lot of work..</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.12</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">..but worht the effort.</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis [[Italian]] [[Bread|bread]] is made using two doughs. Start the day before you want to eat the bread\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n|'''1st [[Dough|dough]]'''\n| 1/8 teaspoon easy-[[Bake|bake]] [[Dried yeast|dried yeast]]\n| 125g strong white [[Bread|bread]] [[Flour|flour]]\n| 105ml water\n}}\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n|'''2nd [[Dough|dough]]'''\n| 1/2 a teaspoon easy-[[Bake|bake]] [[Dried yeast|dried yeast]]\n| 125g strong white [[Bread|bread]] [[Flour|flour]]\n| 115g [[Plain flour|plain flour]]\n| 50g [[Parmesan cheese]] ([[Grated|grated]])\n| 1/2 a teaspoon of [[Salt|salt]] \n| 1 tablespoon [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 30ml [[Milk|milk]]\n| 150ml water\n| 1 tablespoon [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] (optional)\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add the ingredients for the first [[Dough|dough]] to the [[Breadmaker|breadmaker]] pan in the order in which they are given.\n| For Panasonic SD253 and most breadmakers, set to 'Basic [[Dough]]'. \n| For the [[Panasonic SD-ZB2502 automatic breadmaker]] set to menu option 16, basic dough.\n| When when the cycle has finished, switch off the machine and leave to rest at room temperature for about 18 hours.\n| Add the ingredients for the second [[Dough|dough]] to first dough in the [[Breadmaker|breadmaker]] pan in the order in which they are given.\n| Set to 'French Dough' [[Panasonic SD-ZB2502 automatic breadmaker|Panasonic SD-ZB2502]]: option 21 - 3 hours 35 mins.\n| The [[dough]] should be quite sticky when finished.\n| Turn out onto a lightly floured [[Pastry mat|pastry mat]] or board and cut the [[Dough|dough]] into two.\n| Shape each piece into oblongs of about 25cm each on [[baking tray]]s or stones, which have been dusted with [[Flour|flour]] or [[Semolina|semolina]].\n| Cover with a damp [[Tea-towel|tea-towel]] and leave to rise in a [[warm place]] until the [[Dough|dough]] has doubled in size.\n| Sprinkle each loaf with [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] if desired.\n| Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 220\u00b0 C (425\u00b0 F - gas 7) and keep it hot for one hour before [[Baking|baking]].\n| [[Bake]] the [[Bread|bread]] for about 20 minutes until golden brown.\n}}\n===Variations===\nUse any strong, hard, [[Italian cheese]], such as [[Pecorino]].  See also our recipes for plain [[Ciabatta bread recipe|ciabatta]] made entirely in a [[Breadmaker|breadmaker]] and handmade [[Ciabatta with biga]].\n{{Template:Ciabatta bread recipes}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Parmesan ciabatta]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking|Parmesan ciabatta]]\n[[Category:Breadmaker recipes|Parmesan ciabatta]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes|Parmesan ciabatta]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes|Parmesan ciabatta]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Parmesan ciabatta]][[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#parmesanciabatta #dough #breadmaker #bread #flour #bake #driedyeast #baking #pastrymat #italian #pecorino </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Parmesan turnip tops",

title": "Pasta e fagioli",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Pasta e fagioli, Italian recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#pastaefagioli #italian #celery #soup #tomatoes #carrots #pasta #elbowmacaroni #driedthyme #vegetable #stock \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Pasta e fagioli, meaning \"pasta and beans\", is a traditional meatless Italian dish\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1404\n|PortionCalories = 351\n|DatePublished=25th October 2012\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  1 hour, 5 minutes\n|PrepTime =  20 minutes\n|CookTime =  45 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Pasta e fagioli recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Pasta soup</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.6</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Quite nice, but it's just pasta soup!</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\nPasta e fagioli, meaning \"pasta and [[Beans|beans]]\", is a traditional meatless [[Italian]] dish. Like many other [[Italian]] favorites including [[Pizza|pizza]] and [[Polenta|polenta]], the dish started as a peasant dish, being composed of inexpensive ingredients. Today it can be widely found, even in restaurants that do not specialize in [[Italian cuisine]]. It is often pronounced ''pasta fazool'' in the United States.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 2 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 1 medium [[Onion|onion]], peeled and sliced\n| 3 [[Garlic cloves, peeled and crushed|garlic cloves, peeled and crushed]]\n| 2 [[Carrots|carrots]], sliced\n| 3 [[Celery|celery]] stalks chopped into moons\n| 1 can [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], chopped\n| 1 can of good quality [[Vegetable|vegetable]] [[Soup|soup]] or 225 ml [[Vegetable Stock|vegetable stock]]\n| &#189; teaspoon [[Oregano|oregano]]\n| Pinch of [[dried thyme]]\n| 1 [[bay leaf]]\n| [[Sea Salt|Sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| 180 g small pasta, such as [[elbow macaroni]]\n| 1 can [[Cannellini beans|cannellini beans]], rinsed and drained\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the oil over a medium heat and add a good grind of [[black pepper]].\n| Add the [[onions]], [[garlic]], [[celery]], [[carrots]] and saut\u00e9 the for about 6 minutes, stirring now and then.\n| Add the [[soup]] or [[stock]], [[tomatoes]] and simmer vigorously for about 15 minutes or more if you want a thicker soup.\n| Add the [[pasta]], cover and simmer for about 10 minutes or until the [[pasta]] is cooked.\n| Season to taste with [[salt]] and [[pepper]].\n| Stir in the beans and cook for a further 15 minutes\n}}\n\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe in bowls, garnished with grated [[Parmesan cheese]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Soup and stock recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Pasta recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]][[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#pastaefagioli #italian #celery #soup #tomatoes #carrots #pasta #elbowmacaroni #driedthyme #vegetable #stock </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }

This could easily be made with any pasta.\n\n[[Cod roe]] is only available fresh during the very limited season (January to March UK) but canned [[Cod|cod]] [[Roe|roe]] is available all year round and the very large cans can be sliced and [[Frozen|frozen]] for later use.\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| 130 g [[Pasta|pasta]] negra\n| 1 x 4cm (1\u00bd\u0094) slice of canned [[Cod roe|cod roe]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Butter|butter]]\n| [[Freshly ground black pepper]]\n| Freshly cut [[Herbs|herbs]] to garnish\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Cook the [[Pasta|pasta]] for 7 to 10 minutes in lightly [[Salted|salted]] [[Boiling|boiling]] water (or as directed on the packet)\n| Meanwhile, melt 1 tablespoon of [[Butter|butter]] in a small pan with a good pinch of [[Black pepper|black pepper]]\n| Add the sliced [[Cod roe|cod roe]] to the hot pan and crush with the back of a spoon\n| Cook for 4 or 5 minutes turning regularly.  The [[Roe|roe]] does not really need to be cooked so it's just to add a little colour and get the [[Butter|butter]] mixed in well.  Season to taste.\n| Arrange the [[Pasta|pasta]] on a plate, add the cooke droe and dress with frsh [[Herbs|herbs]].\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nI found [[Horseradish sauce|horseradish sauce]] to be a good [[Accompaniment|accompaniment]] for this.\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Pasta recipes]]\n[[Category:Sea fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#pasta #codroe #butter #herbs #roe #lunch #boiledorsimmered #pastanegrawithbutteredcodroe #blackpepper #salted #accompaniment </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

We had this with [[Grilled|grilled]] beefsteak [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], drizzled with [[Balsamic vinegar|balsamic vinegar]], [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and fresh [[Black pepper|black pepper]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 200 g [[Taleggio cheese]], crumbled\n| 200 g [[Pasta|pasta]] of choice\n| 2 [[Cloves of garlic, crushed|cloves of garlic, crushed]]\n| 2 [[Bay leaves|bay leaves]]\n}}\n'''to serve'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 2 beefsteak [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n| [[Balsamic vinegar]]\n| [[Olive oil]]\n| [[Freshly ground black pepper]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Slice the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] in half, drizzle with [[Balsamic vinegar|balsamic vinegar]], [[Olive oil|olive oil]], [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]] and [[Grill|grill]] for about 10 minutes\n|  Add the [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Bay leaves|bay leaves]] to a pan of [[Boiling|boiling]] water and cook the [[Pasta|pasta]] for the time directed on the packet ( [[Pasta cooking times|pasta cooking times]] for most types of pasta can be found here)\n| Drain the [[Pasta|pasta]], reserving &#189; a [[Cup|cup]] of the cooking [[Liquor|liquor]]\n| Add the [[Pasta|pasta]] back to the pan with a splash of [[Olive oil|olive oil]], the crumbled [[Taleggio]] and enough of the cooking water to loosen the [[Cheese|cheese]] into a [[Sauce|sauce]].  About 3 tablespoons should do, but if you add too much it's easy to reduce again.\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Pasta with Taleggio cheese ingredients.jpg|300px|thumb|right|The very simple ingredients\nImage:Pasta with Taleggio cheese beefsteak tomatoes.jpg|300px|thumb|right|Beefsteak tomatoes and balsamic vinegar\n</gallery>\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Grilled|grilled]] [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n===Recipe source===\n\n* Antonio Portillo ([[La Sabrosa Continental]])\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Pasta recipes]]\n[[Category:Grilled, griddled or barbecued]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#pasta #pastawithtaleggiocheese #oliveoil #tomatoes #balsamicvinegar #lasabrosacontinental #taleggiocheese #grilled #bayleaves #blackpepper #cheese </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

pint tepid water\n| 1 teaspoon easy [[Yeast|yeast]] or 1 sachet of yeast\n| 1 teaspoon [[Salt|salt]]\n| 1 teaspoon golden [[Caster sugar|caster sugar]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 8 tablespoons [[Pizza|pizza]] [[Sauce|sauce]] or passata\n| 1 [[Red onions|red onions]], sliced into 5mm rings\n| 1 [[Pear|pear]] sliced into 20 mm slices\n| 150g [[Gorgonzola|gorgonzola]] cheese, chopped into pieces\n| 4 tablespoons [[Walnuts|walnuts]], chopped\n| 25g [[Rocket|rocket]] leaves\n| [[Olive oil]] to serve\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Put the [[Yeast|yeast]] in a bowl, with the [[Sugar|sugar]] and cover with the warm water. \n| Leave this to the side for 5 minutes. \n| In a bowl (or even better, a [[Mixer|mixer]] or [[Bread maker|bread maker]]), add the [[Flour|flour]], [[Yeast|yeast]] and [[Sugar|sugar]] solution, [[Salt|salt]] and [[Olive oil|olive oil]].\n| Mix together to form a soft [[Dough|dough]]. \n| If doing by [[Hand|hand]] turn the [[Bread|bread]] out onto a floured surface, then with a firm fist, [[Kneading bread|knead]] the bread, for 10 minutes. \n| Place the [[Dough|dough]] in a large clean mixing bowl, which has had a dribble of [[Oil|oil]] wiped over it. \n| Cover with some oiled [[Cling film|cling film]] and leave in a [[warm place]] such as an airing cupboard or near a warm cooker for 1 hour. \n| When you come back to it, the [[Dough|dough]] will have doubled in size. \n| Remove the [[Cling film|cling film]] and stick your fist into the [[Dough|dough]]. It will knock all the air out of it. \n| Knock the [[Dough|dough]] around for a minute or until it has deflated. It is now ready to shape.\n| Heat an [[Oven|oven]] to 200C. \n| Cut the [[Dough|dough]] into 4 then roll out each piece into a flat thin round [[Pizza|pizza]] base.\n| Prick the pizza all over with a fork. This prevents it puffing up too much and burning while it is cooking.\n| Top each [[Pizza|pizza]] with 2 tablespoons of [[Tomato sauce|tomato sauce]], some [[Onions|onions]] rings, [[Pear|pear]] slices, some [[Gorgonzola]], 1 tablespoon of [[Walnuts|walnuts]]. \n| Lay the [[Pizzas|pizzas]] on [[baking tray]]s and [[Bake|bake]] in the [[Oven|oven]] for 15-20 minutes. You want to base to be golden and crispy and the [[Cheese|cheese]] to be melted and gooey.\n| When they have finished cook top with a handful of [[Rocket|rocket]] and a drizzle of [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and serve.\n}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Fruit recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Pizza recipes]]\n[[Category:British Onions recipes]]\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n{{Template:British Onions attribution}}\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#dough #oliveoil #yeast #pizza #pearredonionandgorgonzolapizza #rocket #pear #gorgonzola #clingfilm #walnuts #pizzas </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
