What a blinding idea!\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2987\n|PortionCalories = 746\n|DatePublished=21st January 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = Topped with [[yogurt]] mixed with [[horseradish cream]] \n|Servings = Serves 4 - Makes 4 1/2 pounder burgers\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  1 hour, 15 minutes\n|PrepTime =  1 hour\n|CookTime =  15 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Pecorino stuffed chorizo burgers recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Horseradish Cream</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Made with yogurt - wow!</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nThe inspiration for this recipe came from an episode of Triple D; [http://www.foodnetwork.com/diners-drive-ins-and-dives/index.html Diners, Drive-ins and Dives], my favourite cooking program.\n[[Image:Pecorino stuffed chorizo burgers_ingredients.jpg|thumb|300px|right|That's all she wrote...]]\n\nIts basically a [[Burger|burger]] made from a mix of [[Beef mince|beef mince]] and [[Minced|minced]] [[Chorizo sausage|chorizo sausage]] stuffed with nice [[Italian cheese]].\n\nThis was a fantastic and will be made again and again!\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 200g [[Chorizo sausage|chorizo sausage]]\n| 500 g [[Beef mince|beef mince]] ([[Ground beef|ground beef]])\n| 100 g [[Pecorino Romano|pecorino romano]], freshly [[Grated|grated]]\n| &#189; teaspoon [[Salt|salt]]\n| &#189; teaspoon [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| &#189; teaspoon [[Mexican oregano]]\n| [[Fresh herbs]]\n| 2 large slices of [[Bread|bread]] or a cup of [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]]\n| 4 tablespoons [[Milk|milk]]\n| 1 large [[Egg|egg]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Blitz the [[Bread|bread]] slices to crumbs in a [[Food processor|food processor]] with a metal blade.\n| Soak the [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]] in the [[Milk|milk]] for about 15 minutes and then squeeze out any excess [[Milk|milk]].\n| Skin the [[Chorizo|chorizo]] and blitz to a [[Mince|mince]] in a [[Food processor|food processor]] with a metal blade.\n| To the [[Chorizo|chorizo]] [[Mince|mince]] in the [[Mixer|mixer]], add the [[Herbs|herbs]] and [[Spices|spices]], [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]], the [[Egg|egg]] and the mince.\n| Blitz until combined but be careful not ro turn it into [[Pate|pate]]!\n| Divide the [[Burgers|burgers]] and the [[Cheese|cheese]] into four.\n| Using you hands, press out into large [[Burgers|burgers]] and fill with the [[Cheese|cheese]] and fold up to seal.  [[Mould]] into flat burgers.\n| Refrigerate for 30 minutes if you have the time, this seems to help firm them up and bind them together.\n| [[Grill]] for 15 minutes on a tray, not a rack, turning once. ''I think it's nice to let them cook in their own chorizo flavoured oil.''\n| [[Rest for]] a 5 minutes before serving to allow the [[Meat|meat]] to relax and the [[Cheese|cheese]] to melt properly.\n}}\n<gallery widths=270px heights=270px perrow=5>\nImage:Pecorino stuffed chorizo burgers ingredients.jpg|A few simple ingredients\nImage:Chorizo, herbs, beef mince.jpg.jpg|Minced chorizo and herbs with ground beef\nImage:Chorizo, herbs, beef mince, breadcrumbs, egg.jpg.jpg|Breadcrumbs and egg agged\nImage:Chorizo burger mince, pecorino cheese.jpg|Chorizo mince with 100g of [[pecorino cheese]]\nImage:Moulding the pattie,stage one.jpg|Filling the burger with cheese\nImage:Moulding the patttie, stage two.jpg|Folding\nImage:Mouilding the pattie, stage three.jpg|Closing the gaps\nImage:Four half-pound burgers.jpg|Four half-pounders\nImage:Pecorino stuffed chorizo burgers recipe.jpg|The best burger I've ever tasted!\n</gallery>\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Chips|chips]], in a bun with [[Salad|salad]] leaves and sliced [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]].\n===Variations===\nI've used [[Oregano|oregano]] as the base flavour but use a little of what you fancy; [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Horseradish|horseradish]], [[Chillies|chillies]], [[Sage|sage]], [[Thyme|thyme]] would all make good alternatives.\n===Chef's notes===\nFollow the [[RSPCA Think Pig Checklist]] to make sure that your [[Pork|pork]] has come from pigs that have been reared to higher welfare standards.\n\n* http://bit.ly/rspcathinkpig\n\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Beef recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Grilled, griddled or barbecued]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#pecorinostuffedchorizoburgers #breadcrumbs #cheese #chorizosausage #foodprocessor #egg #bread #burgers #chorizo #beefmince #mince </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

gas 7)\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Coat the [[Fish|fish]] on both sides and sprinkle on a little [[Salt|salt]].\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a pan and [[Fry|fry]] the [[Fish|fish]] for 3 minutes on each side.\n| Drain on kitchen paper and reserve.\n| Add the [[Onion|onion]], [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Celery|celery]] and [[Bay leaves|bay leaves]] to the [[Oil|oil]] and [[Fry|fry]] gently for about 6 minutes.\n| Add the [[Tomato|tomato]] pur\u00e9e and water or [[Stock|stock]] to the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] and stir.\n| Bring to a [[Simmer|simmer]] and simmer gently for about 10 minutes.\n| Add the [[Fish|fish]] to the [[Sauce|sauce]] then add the [[Wine|wine]] and [[Oregano|oregano]].\n| [[Boil]] for about 2 minutes.\n| Turn the [[Fish|fish]] over, season with [[Pepper|pepper]], then transfer to a [[Baking|baking]] dish.\n| [[Bake]] for about 8 minutes.\n}}\n===Variations===\nThis would also work with [[Tuna|tuna]] or [[Hake|hake]] steaks.\n===Chef's notes===\nI feel that for 6 people, the sauce quantity should be increased.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Sea fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#fish #pescespadainsalsadipomodoro #wine #garlic #celery #tomato #bayleaves #fry #onion #miseenplace #fishstock </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Just dollop some over freshly cooked pasta and you have a meal fit for a king.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 2 cloves of [[Garlic|garlic]], chopped\n| [[Sea salt]] and [[freshly ground black pepper]]\n| 60 g fresh [[basil leaves]],washed and carefully dried, all stalks removed.\n| 3 tablespoons of, very lightly toasted [[pine nuts]]\n| 4 tablespoons freshly grated [[Parmesan cheese]] plus 2 tablespoons of [[Pecorino]].\n| 125 ml [[Extra virgin olive oil]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Blitz the [[basil]], [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[salt]] in the [[food processor]] - don't blend it too smoothly, you want some texture\n| Add the toasted [[pine nuts]] and blitz again\n| Pour in both cheeses and add just enough olive oil, but don't blitz again, because this would make the cheese in the Pesto too glutinous.Just fold in gently, until well incorporated.\n| Season with [[black pepper]]\n}}\n\nCan be kept in the fridge for a week or so,if you keep a layer of oil covering the Pesto,but also freezes well. Make a batch to use over the Winter, when [[basil]] is in short supply.\n\n===Serving suggestions===\n\nServe with [[fresh pasta]]\n===Variations===\n\nAdd a dash of [[lemon juice]] or lime juice.  If [[basil]] is unavailable, flat-leaved [[parsley]] is excellent, although not authentic.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Pasta recipes]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#basil #freshpasta #pestorecipe #garlic #pinenuts #blackpepper #lemonjuice #basilleaves #parsley #parmesancheese #pecorino </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

[[Black pepper]], to taste\n| 75 g [[Philadelphia Light with garlic and herbs]], softened\n}}\n'''garnish'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| A few fresh [[Chives|chives]] to serve\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Heat the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] in a large saucepan.\n| Add the [[Chicken|chicken]] and cook until golden [[Brown|brown]] and the juices run clear. Remove from pan.\n| Melt the [[Butter|butter]] and saut\u00e9 the [[Onions|onions]] for 3-5 minutes.\n| Add the [[Rice|rice]] and stir until well coated in [[Butter|butter]].\n| Ladle in a little hot [[Stock|stock]]; stir until the [[Stock|stock]] is absorbed.\n| Add another ladle and continue until all [[Stock|stock]] is absorbed and [[Rice|rice]] is cooked.\n| Season to taste with [[Pepper|pepper]].\n| Stir through the Philly and cooked [[Chicken|chicken]].\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with fresh [[Chives|chives]].\n===Recipe source===\n\n* [http://www.philadelphia.co.uk/philadelphia3/page?siteid=philadelphia3-prd&locale=uken1&PagecRef=609&rid=40 The Philadelphia recipe website]\n\n==See also==\n{{OtherRecipes Philadelphia light with garlic and herbs}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Rice recipes]]\n[[Category:Philadelphia recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n[[Category:Cookery cheats]]\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#butter #philadelphiachickenandchiverisotto #stock #oliveoil #chives #chicken #rice #recipesfromothersites #chickenstock #risottorice #chickenbreasts </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Pizza dough",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Pizza dough, Italian recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#pizzadough #warmplace #dough #breadmaker #pizzastone #oregano #butter #oliveoil #panasonicbreadmaker #driedyeast #pizzas \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Use this as a base recipe for your pizzas. I'm afraid I always use my breadmaker now for making pizza dough, it's so quick and easy\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1211\n|PortionCalories = 302\n|DatePublished=8th March 2013\n|Author = Chef\n|Servings = Serves 4 - Enough for '''two''' large [[pizzas]]\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime = 1 hour 22 minutes\n|PrepTime = 1 hour 15 minutes\n|CookTime = 7 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:My pizza dough recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">I make this once a week</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">We have home made pizza at least once a week and make this regularly.  I am a bit lazy and I'm afraid I always use the breadmaker now</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>}}\n\nUse this as a base recipe for your pizzas.\n\nI'm afraid I always use my [[breadmaker]] now for making [[pizza]] [[dough]], it's so quick and easy.  For the [[Panasonic SD-ZB2502 automatic breadmaker]], use menu option 22, pizza dough.\n\nThis is the recipe I use, it works well without or without the [[breadmaker]], though without the breadmaker I still cheat and use the [[food processor]] to mix it.\n\nThere is a good [[spicy tomato sauce for pizzas|spicy tomato sauce for pizzas here]] and another recipe that will use up your glut of home grown tomatoes, [[spicy tomato sauce for pizzas|here]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 level teaspoon [[dried yeast]]\n| 300 g (11 oz) [[strong white flour]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[sugar]], ''see [[Talk:Pizza dough|comments]]''\n| 15 g (1/2 oz) [[butter]] or [[olive oil]]\n| 1 teaspoon table [[salt]]\n| 160 ml water - or by weight instead of volume, 160 g water\n| 1 teaspoon dried [[oregano]]\n}}\n\n===Method===\n'''The easy way'''\n* Tip it all in the breadmaker, switch to ''dough'' or ''pizza'' setting, wait for an hour , remove the perfect [[dough]].\n* '''Recipe option code 22''' on the [[Panasonic SD-ZB2502 automatic breadmaker]]\n'''Another easy way'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Sift the flour into a bowl\n| Warm the water to body temperature, not hot, stir in the milk powder and salt\n| Take a few tablespoons of the warm water, add the sugar and yeast and leave in a [[warm place]] for 15 minutes.\n| Tip the flour into a food processor with a dough hook or plastic blade\n| Add the dried [[oregano]], butter, yeast mixture and the rest of the water\n| Knead until elastic and not too sticky, adjust with extra flour / water if required\n| Place in a lightly oiled bowl, cover with a damp tea-towel and leave in a [[warm place]] for two hours\n}}\n\n'''The hard way'''\n* Follow the steps above, hand kneading when it comes to the automated part.\n\n'''Make the pizza'''\n* Roll into two balls then roll out into two circles, about 20 cm (8\")\n* Prick the pizza all over with a fork. This prevents it puffing up too much and burning while it is cooking.\n* Transfer to a greased baking sheets and leave in a [[warm place]] to rise again (about 1 hour)\n* Follow your pizza recipe from here...\n\n===Baking in an oven===\nBake for 10 to 15 minutes at 220\u00b0 c (425\u00b0 F - Gas 7)\n\n===Cooking on a pizza stone===\nTo obtain a nice crispy pizza base, pre-bake the pizza base on a [[pizza stone]] under a very hot grill for 2 minutes a side.  Then remove and add the toppings and cook until the cheese is bubbling. Watch carefully though as they can quickly burn in the intense heat.\n\n===Chef's notes===\nAnother advantage of preparing pizza dough in the breadmaker is that once the dough cycle is complete, the breadmaker stays warm until it is switched off, giving the dough a good place to rise. ''True for the [[Panasonic breadmaker]] anyway.''\n\nThe Panasonic recipe suggests adding milk powder to the mix but I stopped doing that years ago and the pizzas are always perfect, so I've removed that from the above recipe.\n\n===How to alter the consistency of the pizza base===\nIf the pizza dough is rolled out and baked immediately, without giving time to rise a little (''my preferred method''), the pizza base has a chewy, doughy middle with a crunchy outside, especially if cooked on a [[pizza stone]].  If the pizza dough is rolled out and left to rise for 30 minutes or more, the pizza base is much more crunch and biscuity - it's your call!\n\n===Water measures given by Panasonic===\nThis recipe in my Panasonic breadmaker book originally gave the water quantity as 210 ml, however, the same recipe in a later breadmakers has the quantity reduced to 170ml and finally to 160ml which makes dough with a perfect consistency.\n===Alternative ingredients===\n\nMakes 4 pizzas.  Apparently, the use of sparkling water (Vichy is recommended) gives a crustier base.\n*10 g easy bake dried yeast\n*450 g OO grade pizza flour\n*1 teaspoon sugar\n*10 g salt\n*25 g olive oil (will work it out in ml later)\n*220 ml sparkling bottled water\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Pizza recipes|Dough]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Breadmaker recipes]][[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#pizzadough #warmplace #dough #breadmaker #pizzastone #oregano #butter #oliveoil #panasonicbreadmaker #driedyeast #pizzas </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }

title": "Pizza Margherita",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Pizza Margherita a cheese recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#pizzamargherita #tomato #grill #tomatoes #pizza #cheese #garlic #pizzadough #fry #dough #herbs \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=The basic cheese and tomato pizza\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1487\n|PortionCalories = 743\n|DatePublished=1st November 2012\n|Author = JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 2 - makes 1 medium [[Pizza|pizza]]\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  1 hour 25 minutes<br />Includes making the dough\n|PrepTime = 1 hour 15 minutes  \n|CookTime =  10 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Pizza Margherita recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Proper pizza!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.9</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Love all those olives  Julia!</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Chef|Jerry]] </span></span>\n}}\nThe basic [[Cheese|cheese]] and [[Tomato|tomato]] [[Pizza|pizza]].  I have made this using [[User:Chef|Chef]]'s marvellous idea for using a slab of granite as a [[Pizza stone|pizza stone]], but instructions are also given for making it in the [[Oven|oven]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| Half quantity of [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]]\n| [[Garlic]], peeled and chopped, to taste\n| [[Olive oil]]\n| 1 x 400 g tin of chopped [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Tomato|tomato]] pur\u00e9e\n| [[Basil]] or other [[Herbs|herbs]], chopped, to taste\n| Polenta (for granite method)\n| 250 g [[Mozzarella cheese]], chopped or sliced\n| [[Black olives]]\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n*Roll thinly and shape the [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]], place onto a [[Baking|baking]] sheet and leave to rise until double its size.\n*If using the [[Oven|oven]], preheat it to 220\u00b0 C (425\u00b0 F - gas 7)\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Using a saucepan, lightly [[Fry|fry]] the [[Garlic|garlic]] in a little [[Oil|oil]].\n| Add the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Tomato|tomato]] pur\u00e9e and [[Herbs|herbs]].\n| Bring to the [[Boil|boil]] and allow the mixture to reduce until it is thick.\n| If using the [[Oven|oven]], spread the [[Tomato|tomato]] mixture over the top of the [[Dough|dough]], together with the [[Cheese|cheese]] and [[Olives|olives]] and [[Bake|bake]] for about 15-20 minutes.\n| If using the [[Granite pizza stone|granite pizza stone]], preheat the [[Grill|grill]] with the stone about 5-8 cm underneath it.  You can use [[Baking|baking]] tins or other heatproof objects to keep it at the correct height.\n| Sprinkle some [[Polenta|polenta]] on the hot granite, to prevent the [[Pizza|pizza]] from sticking.\n| Carefully transfer the [[Dough|dough]] to the granite and [[Grill|grill]] for a minute or two on either side.\n| Quickly spread the [[Tomato|tomato]] mixture, [[Cheese|cheese]] and [[Olives|olives]] over the top and [[Grill|grill]] until the cheese has melted.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with a nice. crisp, [[Green salad|green salad]] and [[Bread|bread]].\n===Variations===\nYou can use a mixture of [[Cheeses|cheeses]], so long as they melt properly.  Try sprinkling some [[Parmesan]] over the [[Mozzarella]].  [[Fry]] some [[Chillies|chillies]] with [[Garlic|garlic]] before adding the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]].\n===Chef's notes===\nPlease don't do what I did and place the granite on top of the [[Grill|grill]] pan.  I tried to lift it from under the grill and the weight of the granite broke the grill handle off.\n\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Pizza margherita]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes|Pizza margherita]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes|Pizza margherita]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Pizza margherita]]\n[[Category:Pizza recipes|Pizza margherita]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Pizza margherita]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#pizzamargherita #tomato #grill #tomatoes #pizza #cheese #garlic #pizzadough #fry #dough #herbs </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

of [[white flour]]\n| 250 ml of water\n}}\n'''Other ingredients:'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 250 g of [[Valtellina casera cheese|Valtellina Casera]]\n| 150 g of grated [[Parmigiano-Reggiano pasta:'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| mix the two flours with water and knead for about 5 minutes\n| with a [[rolling pin]] roll the dough to a thickness of 2-3 mm\n| cut 7-8 cm wide strips, overlap the strips and cut across the width, yielding about 5 millimeters wide sort of short noodles\n}}\n'''Cooking:'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| cut the cabbage in short strips, the potatoes in small dices and boil in salted water for 10-15 minutes\n| add the pizzoccheri and boil for about 10 minutes\n| using a [[skimmer]] make a layer of pizzoccheri (with cabbage and potatoes) in a [[baking tin]], sprinkle with grated [[Parmigiano-Reggiano cheese|Parmigiano Reggiano]] cheese and [[Valtellina casera cheese|Valtellina Casera]] cut into flakes\n| continue layering pizzoccheri and cheese\n| fry the garlic in the butter and pour it in the baking tin without mixing\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Pizzoccheri recipe II.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Pizzoccheri\nImage:Pizzoccheri recipe III.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Dried pizzoccheri\n</gallery>\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe piping hot.\n\nPizzoccheri pairs well with a full bodied local red wine: [http://www.wineloverspage.com/italwineguide/valtellina05.phtml Valtellina Superiore]\n===Variations===\n* If you do not find [[Valtellina casera cheese|Valtellina Casera]] cheese, you can try with [[Bitto Valtellina cheese|Bitto]], [[Fontina cheese|Fontina]], [[Cheddar]] or all [[Parmigiano-Reggiano cheese|Parmigiano Reggiano]] cheese instead\n* If you do not want to make the pasta, you can buy it already made\n* When you fry the garlic you can add [[Sage|sage]] as well\n* Make sure to have a little bit of cheese left for the last layer and put it in a hot (~200 \u00b0C) oven for 5 minutes before serving\n==See also==\n* http://www.accademiadelpizzocchero.it/ricetta.html\n* http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pizzoccheri\n* title": "Polenta Taragna",

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Polenta Taragna a cheese recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#polentataragna #sage #yellowcornmeal #garlic #polenta #groundmaize #butter #buckwheatflour #italy #cheese #unusualrecipes \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Polenta taragna is an old recipe from the mountains of the north Italy. It is made with a mix of yellow cornmeal (ground maize) and buckwheat flour\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 4288\n|PortionCalories = 714\n|DatePublished=21st January 2013\n|Author = JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 6\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 1 hour 10 minutes\n |PrepTime = 10 minutes\n |CookTime = 1 hour\n |Image = [[Image:Polenta Taragna recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Classic Italian</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">3.5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Slightly boring to my taste.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Polenta]] taragna is an old recipe from the mountains of the north [[Italy]]. It is made with a mix of [[Yellow cornmeal|yellow cornmeal]] ([[Ground maize|ground maize]]) and [[Buckwheat flour|buckwheat flour]]. Cooked in the classic pot ('[http://it.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paiolo paiolo]' in Italian).\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 350 g of [[Yellow cornmeal|yellow cornmeal]] ([[Ground maize|ground maize]])\n| 350 g of [[Buckwheat flour|buckwheat flour]] \n| 250 g of [[Formai de Mut dell'Alta Valle Brembana cheese]]\n| 250 g of [[Butter|butter]]\n| [[Salt|salt]], [[Sage|sage]], [[Garlic]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Polenta is often cooked in a big pot known in Italian as [http://it.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paiolo paiolo]. Boil 2 litres of water add salt and the two type of flours. \n| Stir for 45 minutes.\n| Add [[Cheese|cheese]] cut into dices and stir for 15 minutes.\n| On a separate pan, slightly [[Fry|fry]] the [[Butter|butter]] with [[Sage|sage]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] then add it to the [[Polenta|polenta]]. Stir for a few minutes and serve.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nYou can serve polenta taragna with sausages, [http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cotechino cotechino], stew or game.\n\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Polenta]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes|Polenta]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#polentataragna #sage #yellowcornmeal #garlic #polenta #groundmaize #butter #buckwheatflour #italy #cheese #unusualrecipes </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Pollo in potacchio",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Pollo in potacchio, Italian recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#chicken #garlic #sauce #rosemary #diced #onion #polloinpotacchio #tomato #celery #tomatosauce #dried \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Chicken with rosemary, garlic and tomato sauce from Le Marche region of Italy\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1429\n|PortionCalories = 357\n|DatePublished=21st January 2013\n|Author = JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = 4-6\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 8 hours\n |PrepTime = 7 hours\n |CookTime = 1 hour\n |Image = [[Image:Pollo in potacchio recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">A substantial chicken stew</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">And this great recipe was added by Julia, a vegetarian!</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Chicken]] with [[Rosemary|rosemary]], [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Tomato sauce|tomato sauce]] from Le Marche region of [[Italy]].  Unusually the [[Tomato|tomato]] [[Sauce|sauce]] is made with tomato pur\u00e9e and not actual [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]].\n\n\n'''For the [[Chicken|chicken]]:'''\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 [[Chicken|chicken]] cut into 10 pieces (see Chef's notes below)\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| Freshly [[Ground|ground]] [[White pepper|white pepper]]\n| 5 [[Rosemary#Sprigs_of_rosemary|sprigs rosemary]]\n| 60-120ml [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 1 medium [[Onion|onion]], finely chopped\n| [[Garlic]] to taste, finely [[Diced|diced]]\n| 960ml [[Dry white wine|dry white wine]]\n| 125ml [[Chicken stock (2)|chicken stock]]\n}}\n'''For the [[Sauce|sauce]]:'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 3 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 1 medium [[Onion|onion]], finely [[Diced|diced]]\n| 1 large [[Carrot|carrot]], finely [[Diced|diced]]\n| 1 stick of [[Celery|celery]], finely [[Diced|diced]]\n| [[Garlic]] to taste, crushed or finely chopped\n| 90g [[Tomato|tomato]] pur\u00e9e\n| 430ml [[Chicken stock (2)|chicken stock]]\n| &frac12; teaspoon [[Dried|dried]] or 1&frac12; teaspoons fresh [[Oregano|oregano]]\n| &frac12; teaspoon [[Dried|dried]] or 1&frac12; teaspoon fresh [[Thyme|thyme]]\n| Seasoning\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Season the [[Chicken|chicken]] pieces and place them in an airtight container or bag, with the rosmary.  \n* [[Refrigerate]] for at least 6 hours or overnight.  \n* Bring the chicken to room temperature before use, reserving the [[Rosemary|rosemary]] - about 30 minutes.\n===Method===\n\n\n'''To make the [[Sauce|sauce]]'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a pan over a medium high heat.\n| Add the [[Onion|onion]], [[Carrot|carrot]] and [[Celery|celery]] and saut\u00e9 for about 10 minutes.\n| Add the [[Garlic|garlic]] and cook for a further couple of minutes, but do not allow it to burn.\n| Add the [[Tomato|tomato]] pur\u00e9e and cook, stirring, for about 4 minutes.\n| Gradually stir in the [[Chicken stock (2)|chicken stock]] and bring to a simmer.\n| Reduce the heat and allow to [[Simmer|simmer]] gently, partially covered for 30 minutes.\n| 10 minutes before the end, season to taste and stir in the [[Herbs|herbs]].\n| When cooked, remove from the heat and allow to stand for a further 10 minutes.\n}}\n'''To cook the [[Chicken|chicken]]'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat 60ml of the [[Oil|oil]] in a large, deep pan over a medium-high heat.\n| Sear the [[Chicken|chicken]] for 4-5 minutes on each side, in two batches, or until golden [[Brown|brown]].\n| Transfer the [[Chicken|chicken]] to a plate.\n| Add the [[Onion|onion]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] and saut\u00e9 for a further 3 minutes.\n| Pour in the [[Tomato sauce|tomato sauce]] and stir continuously for 2 minutes.\n| Add the wine and [[Chicken stock (2)|chicken stock]], reducing the heat to low and return the chicken to the pan.\n| Cook for about 40 minutes, partially covered.\n| Add the [[Rosemary|rosemary]] and cook for a further 20 minutes or until the [[Chicken|chicken]] is done.\n| Discard the [[rosemary]] before serving.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Ciabatta with biga|ciabatta]].\n===Variations===\nAnother time I might try this with [[Pheasant|pheasant]] and [[Cider|cider]], rather than [[Chicken|chicken]] and [[Wine|wine]].\n===Chef's notes===\nCut the [[Chicken|chicken]] into 2 legs, 2 thighs, 2 wings and 2 breasts cut in half.\n\nFor this recipe I used 1&frac12; bulbs of [[Garlic|garlic]] for the [[Sauce|sauce]] and 2 bulbs for the [[Chicken|chicken]] - you may feel you want to reduce the quantity.\n==See also==\n* [[Jointing a chicken]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chicken #garlic #sauce #rosemary #diced #onion #polloinpotacchio #tomato #celery #tomatosauce #dried </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Potato dumplings",

They are simple and quick to make\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1530\n|PortionCalories = 255\n|DatePublished=10th February 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = [[Creamy chicken casserole with potato dumplings]]\n |Servings = Serves 6\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 35 minutes\n |PrepTime = 5 minutes\n |CookTime = 30 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Creamy chicken casserole with potato dumplings recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Makes a nice change</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.7</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Slightly heavier than flour dumplings, but rather good.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Potato dumplings.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Potato dumplings]]\n'''Potato dumplings''', '''bauchrutscher''' (belly bricks), '''kl\u00f6\u00dfe''' / kartoffelkn\u00f6del (Germany), '''kn\u00f6del''' (Austria), '''gomb\u00f3c''' (Hungary), '''kynut\u00e9 knedl\u00edky''' (Luxembourg), '''canederli''' (Italy), '''klub''' (USA), are big round poached or boiled potato or bread dumplings, made without yeast, generally savoury and often filled.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 225 g (8 oz) floury [[Potatoes|potatoes]] (Desiree, King Edward), peeled, [[Boiled|boiled]] and [[Mashed|mashed]]\n| 115 g (4 oz) [[Suet|suet]]\n| 115 g (4 oz) [[Self-raising flour|self-raising flour]]\n| 50 ml (2 fl oz) water - see notes below.\n| 2 tablespoons fresh mixed [[Herbs|herbs]], chopped or 1 teaspoon of dried mixed herbs\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| In a bowl, lightly mix the ingredients into a soft [[Dough|dough]]\n| Only add water if the mixture is too dry as there will probably be enough moisture in the potatoes already.\n| With lightly floured hands, roll into 6 or 8 balls\n| Place in a baking tray filled with 250 ml or so of hot [[chicken stock]] or [[vegetable stock]]\n| Bake at the top of an oven, preheated to 190\u00b0 C (375\u00b0 F - gas 5) for 30 to 40 minutes until crispy\n}}\n===Variations===\n\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Austrian recipes]]\n[[Category:Luxembourg recipes]]\n[[Category:German recipes]]\n[[Category:Hungarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Potato recipes]]\n[[Category:Student recipes]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Poached]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#potatodumplings #dough #herbs #vegetablestock #suet #potatoes #unusualrecipes #chickenstock #mashed </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Potato dumplings (V)",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Potato dumplings vegetarian Italian recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#dough #vegetablestock #mashed #herbs #suet #potatoes #potatodumplingsv #dumpling \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Potato dumplings are an interesting replacement for flour suet dumplings\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1530\n|PortionCalories = 255\n|DatePublished=3rd November 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = Potato dumplings, ready to boil\n |Servings = Serves 6\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 35 minutes\n |PrepTime = 5 minutes\n |CookTime = 30 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Potato dumplings.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Best stuffed with veg</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.1</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">The German ones |I've tried are stuffed with peas. Yumm!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n'''Potato dumplings''', '''bauchrutscher''' (belly bricks), '''kl\u00f6\u00dfe''' / kartoffelkn\u00f6del (Germany), '''kn\u00f6del''' (Austria), '''gomb\u00f3c''' (Hungary), '''kynut\u00e9 knedl\u00edky''' (Luxembourg), '''canederli''' (Italy), '''klub''' (USA), are big round poached or boiled potato or bread dumplings, made without yeast, generally savoury and often filled.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 225 g (8 oz) floury [[Potatoes|potatoes]] (Desiree, King Edward), peeled, [[Boiled|boiled]] and [[Mashed|mashed]]\n| 115 g (6 oz) [[Suet|suet]]\n| 115 g (4 oz) [[Self-raising flour|self-raising flour]]\n| 50 ml (2 fl oz) water\n| 2 tablespoons fresh mixed [[Herbs|herbs]], chopped\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| In a bowl, mix the [[Dumpling|dumpling]] ingredients into a soft [[Dough|dough]]\n| With lightly floured hands, roll into 6 balls\n|Place the dumpling in a large pan of boiling water, ideally they should not touch.  Reduce to a simmer and cook (don't boil) for 20 to 30 minutes\n| The dumplings will sink at first, and rise to the surface once cooked - just make one final check for 'doneness'.\n}}\n===Variations===\nPlace in a baking tray filled with 500 ml or so of hot [[vegetable stock]] (not quite covering the dumplings)and bake in an over preheated to 190\u00b0 C (375\u00b0 F - gas 5).  For a nice crispy top, finish under the grill for 5 minutes.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Austrian recipes]]\n[[Category:Luxembourg recipes]]\n[[Category:German recipes]]\n[[Category:Hungarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Potato recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Poached]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#dough #vegetablestock #mashed #herbs #suet #potatoes #potatodumplingsv #dumpling </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }

Really love the olives.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}} \nA nice Mediterranean-style [[Chicken|chicken]] recipe.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1.6kg oven ready [[Chicken|chicken]] \n| 2 sprigs fresh [[Marjoram|marjoram]], leaves only \n| A good handful of [[Thyme|thyme]], leaves only \n| 4 Cloves of [[Garlic|garlic]] \n| 5 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]] \n| 1 [[Belazu]] [[Preserved lemon|preserved lemon]], sliced thinly - (flesh discarded)\n| 175g [[Belazu]] [[Black olives|black olives]] with [[Herbs]], stoned \n| 250g [[Button mushrooms|button mushrooms]]\n| 1 green [[sweet pepper]], de-seeded and sliced\n| 40g sun-[[Dried|dried]] or sun-blush [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], soaked in hot water and drained\n| 1 medium [[Onion|onion]], sliced\n| 1 fresh [[bay leaf]]\n| 175ml [[Dry white wine|dry white wine]]\n| [[Sea salt]] & [[freshly ground black pepper]]\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 220\u00b0 C (425\u00b0 F - gas 7)\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Pot Roasted Mediterranean Chicken carved.jpg|Carving Pot Roasted Mediterranean Chicken\nImage:Pot Roasted Mediterranean Chicken, cooked.jpg|Pot Roasted Mediterranean Chicken, cooked\nImage:Pot Roasted Mediterranean Chicken.jpg|Ready for the oven\nImage:Garlic and herb rubbed.jpg|Garlic, [[olive oil]] and [[herb]] rub, the lazy way\nImage:Garlic and herb rub.jpg|Garlic and [[herb]] rub.  I added a some [[parsley]] to bulk out my meagre winter herbs\n</gallery>\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| [[Parson's nose|Remove the parson's nose]] from the chicken.\n| Season the [[Chicken|chicken]] inside and out. [[Mash]] the [[Herbs|herbs]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] with 3 tablespoons of [[Oil|oil]] to form a paste.\n| Slide your fingers between the skin and flesh of the [[Chicken|chicken]] and rub the paste as evenly as possible over the breasts. Chop half of the [[Lemon slices|lemon slices]] and mix with half the [[Olives|olives]] and half the [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]]. Stuff the cavity with this mixture. in the cavity. \n| Put the bird in a heavy [[Casserole|casserole]] (such as [[Le Creuset]]). Scatter round the [[Sun-dried tomatoes|sun-dried tomatoes]], [[green pepper]] slices, [[Onion|onion]], remaining [[Lemon|lemon]], [[olives]] and [[mushrooms]] and pour over the [[Wine|wine]] and the remaining olive oil.\n| [[Roast]] for about 1 &frac34; hours.  Covered for the first 45 minutes, remove the cover then [[Baste|baste]] every 20 minutes until the chicken is properly cooked,\n| To serve, spoon the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] from the cavity and set the [[Chicken|chicken]] on a board. \n| Skim [[Fat|fat]] off the juices in the [[Casserole|casserole]], bring to the [[Boil|boil]] and serve hot with the carved chicken. Delicious with [[barley couscous]].\n}}\n''(Orlando Murrin in The Daily Express)''\n\n\n===Serving suggestion===\nDelicious with [[barley couscous]].\n\n{{Template:Belazu attribution}}\n\n===Belazu products used in this recipe===\n* [http://www.mybelazu.com/details/black-with-herbs.html Belazu black herb olives]\n* [http://www.mybelazu.com/details/belazu-pickled-lemons.html Belazu Preserved Lemon]\n* [http://www.mybelazu.com/details/traditional-barley-couscous.html Belazu Traditional Barley Couscous]\n\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Belazu recipes|Chicken]]\n[[Category:French recipes|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes|Chicken]]\n[[Category:North African recipes|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Stews and casseroles|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Stews and casseroles|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Stewed, braised or pot roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#potroastedmediterraneanchicken #chicken #barleycouscous #herb #belazu #oliveoil #onion #mushrooms #herbs #garlic #olives </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Prawn potato bake",
                "revisions": [

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Prawn potato bake, Italian recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#potatoes #butter #sauce #prawns #prawnpotatobake #onions #blackpepper #cremefraiche #singlecream #greenvegetable #salted \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A complete meal that is a variation on Dauphinois potatoes, but with a creamy prawn sauce\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2470\n|PortionCalories = 617\n|DatePublished=1st January 2014\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  50 minutes\n|PrepTime =  10 minutes\n|CookTime =  40 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Prawn potato bake recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n}}\n\nA complete meal that is a variation on [[Dauphinois potatoes]], but with a creamy [[Prawn|prawn]] [[Sauce|sauce]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 6 [[Potatoes|potatoes]], sliced (leave the skins on if you prefer)\n| 1 small [[Onion|onion]], peeled and sliced\n| 225 g (8 oz) [[Peeled prawns|peeled prawns]] or [[Shrimp|shrimp]]\n| 2 [[Cloves of Garlic, peeled and crushed|cloves of garlic, peeled and crushed]]\n| 25g (1 oz) [[Butter|butter]]\n| 30 ml (2 tablespoons) [[Dry sherry|dry sherry]]\n| 250 ml (1 cup) [[Single cream|single cream]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]] to taste\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 4), [fan [[Oven|oven]] 160\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| [[Boil]] the sliced [[Potatoes|potatoes]] in lightly [[Salted|salted]] water for 4 minutes (once the water is [[Boiling|boiling]]).\n| Drain and pat dry.\n| Heat the half of [[Butter|butter]] in a [[Frying pan|frying pan]] and add a grind of [[Black pepper|black pepper]]\n| Saut\u00e9 the [[Onions|onions]] in the [[Butter|butter]] over a medium heat for 4 minutes\n| Add the [[Crushed garlic|crushed garlic]] and [[Prawns|prawns]] and [[Stir-fry|stir-fry]] for 2 minutes\n| Reduce the heat a little, pour in the [[Sherry|sherry]] and [[De-glaze|de-glaze]] the pan\n| Mix the [[Cream|cream]] in and stir well and cook for another minute\n| Strain the [[Sauce|sauce]] to separate the [[Prawns|prawns]] and [[Onions|onions]] \n| Pour the [[Prawns|prawns]] and [[Onions|onions]] in the base of an [[Oven|oven]]-proof dish\n| Layer the [[Potatoes|potatoes]] on top , dotting with the remaining [[Butter|butter]]\n| Season with [[Salt|salt]] and [[Black pepper|black pepper]] and pour the [[Sauce|sauce]] over the top of the [[Potatoes|potatoes]]\n| [[Bake]] for up to 35 minutes or until the [[Potatoes|potatoes]] are golden and cooked through. Check them after 25 minutes.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with a [[Green vegetable|green vegetable]] like [[Broccoli|broccoli]] or [[Peas|peas]]\n===Variations===\nUse [[Creme fraiche|creme fraiche]] instead of [[single Cream]] (it will be less likely to separate while cooking. Mix the [[Creme fraiche|creme fraiche]]  with  [[milk]] to make if pourable.\n\nUse large frozen prawns that have been defrosted, chopped into four pieces.\n\nSprinkle a few tablespoons of finely grated [[Parmesan cheese]] over the top before it is [[baked]].\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Good with crayfish too</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.8</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Recently tried this with crayfish and it was fab.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n\n\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Sea fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Shellfish recipes]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#potatoes #butter #sauce #prawns #prawnpotatobake #onions #blackpepper #cremefraiche #singlecream #greenvegetable #salted </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

I think next time I would reduce the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] and try and find pairings for all of the [[Cheeses|cheeses]]. I would keep sliced [[Chillies|chillies]] & [[Cheddar|cheddar]], crushed [[Walnuts|walnuts]] & [[St Agur]] ([[Soft Blue cheese|soft blue cheese]]) but need some for [[Somerset brie]] and [[Mozzarella|mozzarella]].  Suggestions are very welcome!\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 portion of [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]] - Makes 2 pizzas\n| 6 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 4 [[Cloves|cloves]] [[Garlic|garlic]], sliced\n| 10 halved baby [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] (sungold if you can get them/grow them)\n| Copious torn [[Basil leaves|basil leaves]]\n| 125 g [[Mozzarella cheese]] ball, torn into pieces\n| 80 g strong [[Cheddar cheese|cheddar cheese]], thinly sliced\n| 100 g [[Saint Agur Blue cheese]], crumbled\n| 90 g [[Somerset brie]], thinly sliced\n| 2 [[Green Indian chillies|green indian chillies]], cut into rings\n| 4 tablespoons of crushed [[Walnuts|walnuts]]\n| [[Fine yellow cornmeal|fine yellow cornmeal]] for dusting\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Make the [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]] as instructed\n* If using a [[pizza stone]], preheat the [[pizza stone]] under a very hot [[grill]] for about 20 minutes.  Place it about 8cm (3\") from the heat source.\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Quattro formaggi (four cheese) oven ready.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Quattro formaggi-ready for the oven\nImage:Quattro formaggi (four cheese) pizza_ingredients.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Quattro formaggi (four cheese) pizza, the ingredients\n</gallery>\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Make 1 pizza per person\n| Dust your work surface with [[Yellow cornmeal|yellow cornmeal]]\n| Divide the [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]] into two and roll out into two thin 25.5 cm (10 inch) [[Pizzas|pizzas]]\n| Prick the pizzas all over with a fork. This prevents it puffing up too much and burning while it is cooking\n| With a deft move, slide the [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]] from the [[Pizza peel|pizza peel]], on to the preheated [[Pizza stone|pizza stone]].\n| Cook on one side only for about 2 minutes or until lightly [[Browned|browned]].\n| remove from the oven, flip and add the topping.\n| Repeat for the second [[Pizza|pizza]] whilst you prepare the first.\n| Meanwhile heat the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and saut\u00e9 the sliced [[Garlic|garlic]] until it just starts to colour, no more or it will be [[Bitter|bitter]] \n| Drizzle the [[Pizza|pizza]] with the half of the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] slices.\n| Make a cross with the [[Basil leaves|basil leaves]] and top with the sliced [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n| Arrange the [[Cheeses|cheeses]] in the four quadrants-adding your chosen accompaniments to each cheeses; [[Walnuts|walnuts]] and [[Blue cheese|blue cheese]], [[Chillies|chillies]] and [[Cheddar|cheddar]], etc.\n| [[Bake]] the [[Pizza|pizza]] until the [[Cheese|cheese]] starts to melt and bubble-this only takes a few minutes under a hot [[Grill|grill]].\n| Keep the first pizza warm at the bottom of the oven whilst you make the second.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with homemade [[Cole-slaw|cole-slaw]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Pizza recipes]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#pizzadough #pizza #garlic #walnuts #cheeses #tomatoes #pizzastone #oliveoil #grill #cheese #chillies </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

[[Dried pasta]] will take longer. -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2700\n|PortionCalories = 675\n|DatePublished=24th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 50 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 35 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Red onion and blue cheese risotto recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Onion rice pudding</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span finely chopped\n| 300g/10oz [[Risotto rice|risotto rice]]\n| 2-3 [[Rosemary#Sprigs_of_rosemary|Stems fresh rosemary]], plus extra to garnish\n| 200ml/7fl oz [[White wine]]\n| 1.5 litre/2.5  [[Pints]] hot [[Vegetable Stock|vegetable stock]]\n| [[Salt]] and [[Ground black pepper|ground black pepper]]\n| 6 Slices [[Parma ham|parma ham]]\n| 150g/5oz [[Blue cheese]], such as [[Stilton|stilton]], [[St Agur]] or [[Roquefort]], rind removed, [[Diced|diced]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Melt the [[Butter|butter]] and 1 tablespoon of the [[Oil|oil]] in a large saucepan, add the [[Onions|onions]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Fry|fry]] gently for 2-3 minutes until just beginning to soften then stir in the [[Rice|rice]].\n| Strip the leaves from [[Rosemary|rosemary]] stems and add to the pan with the [[Wine|wine]], a ladleful of the hot [[Stock|stock]] and some [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]]. \n| [[Simmer]], stirring from time until the [[Rice|rice]] has absorbed the [[Stock|stock]], continue adding ladlefuls of stock as needed until the rice is soft and creamy and all, or almost all of the stock has been added. This will take about 25 minutes.\n| Heat the remaining [[Oil|oil]] in a large [[Frying pan|frying pan]], add the [[Parma ham|parma ham]] and [[Fry|fry]] for 2 minutes or until just crispy. \n| Take out of the pan with a [[Slotted spoon|slotted spoon]] and cut into thick strips on a chopping board.\n| Stir half the [[Cheese|cheese]] into the [[Risotto|risotto]], spoon into shallow [[Soup|soup]] bowls and sprinkle with the remaining cheese and [[Parma ham|parma ham]]. \n| Garnish with small sprigs of extra [[Rosemary|rosemary]] and serve at once.\n}}\n===Chef's notes===\n{{Template:ThinkPig}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British Onions recipes]]\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Rice recipes]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n{{Template:British Onions attribution}}\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#redonionandbluecheeserisotto #parmaham #garlic #rosemary #fry #rice #stock #butter #risottorice #britishonions #wine </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Risotto alla Milanese",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Risotto alla Milanese, Italian recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#risottoallamilanese #butter #rice #stock #parmesancheese #saffronstrands #onion #beef #boiledorsimmered #marrowbone #bones \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Risotto is a rich and creamy, traditional Italian rice dish\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2018\n|PortionCalories = 504\n|DatePublished=24th October 2012\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 40 minutes\n |PrepTime = 10 minutes\n |CookTime = 30 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Risotto alla Milanese recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Like the liver tip</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Good idea, I have a job getting marrow bones - the dogs get them first!</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Risotto]] is a rich and creamy, traditional Italian [[Rice|rice]] dish. It is one of the most common ways of cooking rice in Italy.\n\nIts origins are in North Italy, specifically Eastern Piedmont, Western Lombardy, and the Veneto, where [[Rice|rice]] paddies are abundant. It is one of the pillars of Milanese cuisine, of which [[Risotto alla Milanese|risotto alla Milanese]] is near the top!\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1.5 [[Litres|litres]] (50 fl oz) good [[Beef stock|beef stock]]\n| 20 g (3/4 oz) [[Beef|beef]] [[Bone marrow|bone marrow]] - see your butcher for this!\n| 80g (3 oz) [[Butter|butter]]\n| 1 small [[Onion|onion]], peeled and chopped\n| 350 g (12 oz) [[Risotto rice|risotto rice]]\n| &#189; teaspoon [[Saffron strands|saffron strands]]\n| 80 g (3 oz) freshly [[Grated|grated]] [[Parmesan cheese]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| In one pan, bring the [[Stock|stock]] to the [[Boil|boil]] and then turn out the heat\n| Heat 50 g (2 oz)  of the [[Butter|butter]] and the [[Beef|beef]] [[Marrow|marrow]] in another pan and add the [[Onion|onion]]. Saut\u00e9 the onion for 5 minutes but don't [[Brown|brown]] it\n| Add the [[Rice|rice]] to the [[Onions|onions]] and stir well to ensure all of the [[Grains|grains]] are coated in [[Butter|butter]]\n|'''Now the therapeutic part!'''\n| Add the [[Stock|stock]], 1 ladle full at a time, not adding the next ladle until the previous has been absorbed by the [[Rice|rice]]\n| Stir very frequently to prevent it sticking to the bottom of the pan\n| Adding the stock will probably take about 18 minutes\n| When you are adding the very last ladle of [[Stock|stock]], also add the [[Saffron strands|saffron strands]]\n| Season with [[Salt|salt]], add the [[Parmesan cheese]] and the remaining [[Butter|butter]] and serve.\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Risotto alla Milanese half-way.jpg|About half way through\nImage:Risotto alla Milanese coating the rice.jpg|Coat the rice\nImage:Risotto alla Milanese onions.jpg|Saut\u00e9 the onions\n</gallery>\n===Serving suggestions===\nTraditionally this would be served with [[Ossobuco alla Milanese]]\n===Chef's note===\nStruggling for time while making this at short notice I could not get [[marrowbone]] from our local supermarket, \"all the [[bones]] are removed  before we get the meat!\", so I substituted a big handful of [[chicken liver]], chopped to almost a mush.  It was a very good substitute!\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Rice recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#risottoallamilanese #butter #rice #stock #parmesancheese #saffronstrands #onion #beef #boiledorsimmered #marrowbone #bones </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Place it about 8cm from the heat source.\n* This can be made in an [[Oven|oven]] but will take about 20 to cook.  If using the oven, preheat it to 220\u00b0 C (425\u00b0 F - gas 7)\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Dust the work surface with [[Fine yellow cornmeal]]\n| Roll or stretch the [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]] into dinner-plate sized circles.  Make one pizza per person.\n| Prick the pizza all over with a fork. This prevents it puffing up too much and burning while it is cooking.\n| Slide the empty [[Pizza|pizza]] onto the [[Pizza stone|pizza stone]] using a [[Pizza peel|pizza peel]].\n| [[Bake]] for about 3 minutes on one side only until it puffs up and is slightly [[Browned|browned]]\n| Remove from the [[Oven|oven]], flip over and add the topping\n| Spread a few tablespoons of [[Tomato sauce|tomato sauce]] over the uncooked side of the base.\n| Sprinkle with the cooked [[Roast pork|roast pork]] and dab [[Apple sauce|apple sauce]] here and there.\n| Layer a few rings of finely sliced [[Onions|onions]] over the [[Pork|pork]].\n| Tear the [[mozzarella]] ball in to pieces and add to the [[Pizza|pizza]].\n| Sprinkle with chopped [[Chillies|chillies]] if using.\n| Drizzle with [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and season with [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]].\n| Slide on to the [[Pizza stone|pizza stone]] and [[Grill|grill]] until the [[Cheese|cheese]] is [[Toasted|toasted]]. This should take about 4 minutes.  Keep this pizza warm at the bottom of the oven while you make the second pizza.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with a [[Green salad|green salad]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Pizza recipes]][[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#roastporkpizza #roastpork #pizza #pizzastone #fineyellowcornmeal #grill #applesauce #oliveoil #pizzadough #mozzarellacheese #pizzapeel </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Someone's been at the cider I recon. \ud83d\ude1c</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Chef|Jerry, aka Chef]])</span></span>\n}}\nOrganic [[Spaghetti squash|spaghetti squash]] is uncannily like a pack of [[Spaghetti|spaghetti]] in a veg. Marvellous with an [[Italian]] Job lot of [[Toasted|toasted]] [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 [[Spaghetti squash|spaghetti squash]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground pepper|freshly ground pepper]]\n| 3 [[Garlic|garlic]] [[Cloves|cloves]]\n| A gloss of [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and/or a couple of blobs of [[Butter|butter]]\n| \u00bd mug of [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]]\n| 12 [[Sage leaves|sage leaves]]\n| A large handful of freshly [[Grated|grated]] [[Parmesan]]\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 200\u00b0 C (400\u00b0 F - gas 6), [fan [[Oven|oven]] 180\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Halve your [[Squash|squash]] lengthwise, giving you two identical halves. Place on a [[Baking tray|baking tray]] or in individual [[Baking|baking]] dishes. Dust with a little [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]].\n| Flatten two [[Garlic|garlic]] [[Cloves|cloves]] with the side of a knife or your [[Hand|hand]]. Keep the peel on to protect the [[Clove|clove]] from burning. Pop a [[Clove|clove]] in each [[Squash|squash]] halve. Gloss with [[Oil|oil]].\n| [[Roast]] for 45 mins to 1 hour, or till fully tender and bronzed around the edges. Let the [[Oven|oven]] cook as much water from the [[Squash|squash]] as possible, for intensely-flavoured flesh.\n| While your [[Squash|squash]] [[Roasts|roasts]], add a blob of [[Butter|butter]] or a gloss of [[Oil|oil]] to a pan. Add the 6 whole [[Sage leaves|sage leaves]]. Sizzle them in the [[Oil|oil]] or [[Butter|butter]] till just crisp on both sides this only takes a minute. Remove from the pan. Use these as a garnish. Put your pan back on the heat.\n| Finely chop the last 6 [[Sage leaves|sage leaves]] and [[Garlic clove|garlic clove]]. Mix into your [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]]. Add a little more [[Oil|oil]] or [[Butter|butter]] to your warming pan. Toss in the [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]]. Sizzle over medium heat till golden and fragrant.\n| Once the [[Squash|squash]] is done, remove the [[Garlic|garlic]] from its skin. Pop it back in the [[Squash|squash]]. Take a fork to your squash to tease out the [[Spaghetti|spaghetti]]-like strands, mixing the [[Roasted garlic|roasted garlic]] through. Scatter the [[Toasted|toasted]] crumbs over, along with a good handful of [[Parmesan|parmesan]].\n| Dot your crispy [[Sage leaves|sage leaves]] on top and grab a fork.\n}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Abel and Cole veg box recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n{{Template:Abel and Cole veg box recipes attribution}}\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#squash #breadcrumbs #butter #sageleaves #garlic #roastsquashettiwithparmesagepangratto #spaghettisquash #parmesan #spaghetti #toasted #miseenplace </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Rouladen",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Rouladen a beef recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#rouladen #onion #beef #mustard #redwine #beefstock #tomatopuree #flour #carrot #bacon #bayleaf \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Rouladen (or Rinderroulade) is a German /Hungarian meat roulade consisting of bacon, onions, mustard and pickles wrapped in thinly sliced beef and\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2560\n|PortionCalories = 1280\n|DatePublished=5th August 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 2 people, serve 2 or 3 roulades per person depending on the size\n |Difficulty = 3\n |TotalTime = 2 hours 15 minutes\n |PrepTime = 20 minutes\n |CookTime = 1 hour 55 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Rouladen recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n}}\n\n'''Rouladen''' (or '''Rinderroulade''') is a German /Hungarian [[Meat|meat]] roulade consisting of [[Bacon|bacon]], [[Onions|onions]], [[Mustard|mustard]] and [[Pickles|pickles]] wrapped in thinly sliced [[Beef|beef]] and then cooked.\n\nThe Italian versions  are called '''Braciole''' or '''Involtini''' (nothern Italy) and commonly have equal measures of pine nuts, small seedless raisins, Mozzarella cheese, Prosciutto, breadcrumbs and a little chopped parsley and salt and pepper.  They are pan fried and sometimes served with [[Sunday sauce]].\n\n[[Beef]], [[Venison|venison]], [[Wild boar|wild boar]] or [[Pork|pork]] can be used, though in this recipe we use beef.\n{{Template:HC recipes}}\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 500g [[Beef]] [[Shank|shank]] cut into very thin steaks and hammered flat - see the [[butterflying|butterfly article]] if you need hints.\n| 1 [[Onion|onion]], peeled and chopped\n| French [[Mustard|mustard]] (to taste)\n| 70g [[Home smoked bacon]] or [[Pancetta|pancetta]]\n| 1 large [[Dill pickle|dill pickle]], cut into strips\n| 2 [[Cloves|cloves]] of [[Garlic]], peeled and crushed\n| 1 [[Carrot|carrot]], peeled and sliced\n| 1 stalk of [[Celery|celery]] cut into moons\n| 1 [[Bay leaf|bay leaf]]\n| &frac12; bottle [[Red wine|red wine]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Tomato puree|tomato puree]]\n| A little [[Beef stock|beef stock]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| [[Flour]] (or [[Fine yellow cornmeal|fine yellow cornmeal]]) for dusting\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Spread the [[Mustard|mustard]] on the inside of the [[Steak|steak]]\n| Fill with a few slices of [[Onion|onion]], [[Gherkin|gherkin]] and [[Bacon|bacon]]\n| Roll up and secure with toothpicks or tie with [[kitchen string]]\n| Coat in seasoned [[Flour|flour]] and in a large pan or [[Dutch oven]], [[Fry|fry]] in a little [[Oil|oil]] until [[Browned|browned]]. Remove and reserve\n| In the same pan, saut\u00e9 the [[Onion|onion]],[[Celery|celery]], [[Carrot|carrot]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] for 6 minutes\n| Add a little [[Red wine|red wine]] and stir to [[Deglaze|deglaze]] the pan\n| Place the roulades on top of the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] and pour the remaining [[Wine|wine]] over the top\n| Heat for 5 minutes to reduce the [[Wine|wine]] a little\n| Add a little [[Beef stock|beef stock]], [[Tomato puree|tomato puree]], [[Bay leaf|bay leaf]] and season well.\n| [[Simmer]] gently for 1.5 hours\n| Strain the gravy before serving and thicken a little if needed\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe hot with [[Boiled|boiled]] or [[Mashed potatoes|mashed potatoes]], [[Carrots|carrots]] and [[Broccoli|broccoli]]\n\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Kedves!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Magyar loveliness - Szia! </span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Beef recipes]]\n[[Category:German recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes]]\n[[Category:Hungarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]][[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#rouladen #onion #beef #mustard #redwine #beefstock #tomatopuree #flour #carrot #bacon #bayleaf </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }

title": "Salami Cheese Pasta Bake using Long Life Ingredients",

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Salami Cheese Pasta Bake using Long Life Ingredients\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#pasta #cheesepowder #oliveoil #roux #plainflour #salamicheesepastabakeusinglonglifeingredients #milkpowder #whisk #sauce #salami #maincourses\n|hashtagrev=12032020\n|description=In the advent of the Coronavirus event and being mindful of cooking with long life ingredients, I thought I would do some experiments with pasta.\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|DatePublished=19th March 2020\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = 2\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  55 minutes\n|PrepTime =  15 minutes\n|CookTime =  40 minutes\n|TotalCalories = 1040\n|PortionCalories = 520\n|Image = [[Image:Salami Cheese Pasta Bake using Long Life Ingredients recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Tasty!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">I could eat this all day long. \ud83c\udf5d</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Chef|Jerry, aka Chef]])</span></span>\n}}\nIn the advent of the Coronavirus event and being mindful of cooking with long life ingredients,  I thought I would do some experiments with [[Pasta|pasta]].  This is the successful result of a few experiments.\n\nAll of the ingredients are long life and make a pretty reasonable meal even after they have been stored for many months.\n\nThe only item that might be more difficult to source is the [[Cheese powder|cheese powder]],  although [[Cheese|cheese]] can be successfully [[Frozen|frozen]], so you could use that.\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 400 ml water\n| 50 g of [[Milk powder|milk powder]]\n| or 400 ml of [[Milk]]\n| 40g of [[Taste Sensation]] [[Cheese powder|cheese powder]]\n| 40g [[Olive oil]]\n| 30g [[Plain flour|plain flour]]\n| 60 g of [[Salami|salami]] or [[pepperoni]], sliced.\n| 150 g of [[Pasta|pasta]]\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Preheat your [[Oven|oven]] to 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 4), [fan oven 160\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| [[Boil]] the [[Pasta|pasta]] in plenty of water, to which a good pinch of [[Salt|salt]] has been added.\n| Drain and reserve\n| Make up the [[Milk|milk]] from the [[Milk powder|milk powder]] by whisking the powder into the milk until combined.\n| [[Whisk]] in the [[Cheese powder|cheese powder]] to the [[Milk|milk]].\n| Add the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] to a [[Saucepan|saucepan]] and heat gently.\n| Stir in the [[Plain flour|plain flour]] until combined into a [[Roux|roux]] (a floury paste).\n| Pour the [[Milk|milk]] into the pan and [[Whisk|whisk]] to combine the [[Roux|roux]] into the cheesey milk.\n| Bring to a rolling [[Simmer|simmer]] while stirring as the [[Sauce|sauce]] thickens.\n| Mix the drained [[Pasta|pasta]] into the [[Sauce|sauce]] and pour into the sauce.\n| Pour the [[Pasta sauce|pasta sauce]] into an [[Oven|oven]] dish and dot with the [[Salami|salami]] slices.\n| Allow your cat to examine the results!\n| [[Bake]] in the middle of the [[Oven|oven]] at 180\u00b0 C for about 30 minutes.\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:baked long life cheese pasta.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Long-life salami pasta, baked\nImage:Cat examined pasta.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Allow your cat to investigate the pasta before baking!\n</gallery>\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with a [[Green vegetable|green vegetable]] if you have any.\n===Variations===\nOptionally add a chopped [[Onion|onion]] and 3 [[Cloves of garlic, crushed|cloves of garlic, crushed]] to the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and [[Fry|fry]] off before making the [[Roux|roux]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pasta recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Taste Sensation #roux #plainflour #salamicheesepastabakeusinglonglifeingredients #milkpowder #whisk #sauce #salami #maincourses</code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Salmon and prawn tagliatelle",
                "revisions": [

It's the simplest recipe I know - I\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2057\n|PortionCalories = 1028\n|DatePublished=31st January 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 2 - Would stretch to 4 with a big salad and maybe a bit more pasta\n|Difficulty = 1\n|ImageComment = Made using homemade pasta & crayfish instead of prawns\n|TotalTime = 20 minutes\n|PrepTime = 5 minutes\n|CookTime = 15 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Salmon and prawn tagliatelle.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">The Big Breakfast; I thank you.</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">I must have made this 100's of times, and it never fails to amaze.  Simplicity itself and so good.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:RecipeSalmon and prawn tagliatelle.jpg|thumb|300px|right|The ingredients without pasta]]\nI saw this recipe on The Big Breakfast (Channel 4), about 25 years ago; and have been making variations of it ever since.\n\nIt's the simplest recipe I know - I dare you to get this one wrong!\n\nThere is an even [[Salmon and prawn tagliatelle (simple version)|simpler version here]]\n\nThis is especially nice if made with [[homemade pasta]]\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 portion of [[Fresh pasta|fresh tagliatelle]] (about 250g) or 100g  of [[dried taglitelle]]\n| 1 tin [[lobster bisque soup]]\n| 2 raw [[salmon steaks]], about 175g (6 oz) each\n| 100 g (3.5 oz) fresh [[peeled prawns]]\n| 3 tablespoons [[dry sherry]]\n| 125 ml single or double [[cream]]\n| Big handful of [[parsley]], chopped - keep some whole for the garnish\n| Chopped [[chives]] (optional)\n| Squeeze of [[lemon]] juice\n| Freshly grated [[black pepper]]\n| Pinch of [[salt]]\n| Splash of [[olive oil]]\n| 2 cloves of [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled and crushed\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Remove the skin from the [[salmon]] and remove any pin-[[bones]] - [[tweezers]] are good for this\n| Cut the [[salmon]] into 1\" x 1\" chunks\n| Add a splash of olive oil and the black pepper to a large pan and sizzle the [[garlic]] for a few minutes. Add the salmon pieces and stir to coat with the garlic oil\n| Pour the soup over the garlic and [[salmon]], almost bring the soup to the boil and then immediately reduce to a simmer\n| Place the [[salmon]] chunks in the soup and simmer for 4 minutes\n| Cook the pasta as directed, drain and cover\n| Add the [[prawns]], [[cream]], [[sherry]], chopped [[parsley]], [[salt]] and stir for a minute or so\n| Pour the pasta into the soup, mix well, serve with [[parsley]] garnish\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe hot, maybe with a salad if you need to stretch it to four people.  There is enough here for two gluttons though!\n\n===Variations===\nThis works well with a few crushed [[bird's' eye chillies]] crushed and added with the [[garlic]].  Mind you, if you love your [[chili]] you probably don't need to be told this!\n==See also==\n{{Template:Lobster recipes}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Pasta recipes]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Shellfish recipes|Prawn]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#salmonandprawntagliatelle #salmon #parsley #garlic #cream #drysherry #boiledorsimmered #chili #blackpepper #oliveoil #lemon </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Sausage, bean and radicchio hash an Italian recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#sausagebeanandradicchiohash #tomatopuree #radicchio #tomatoes #sausage #chickenstock #fry #chilliflakes #oliveoil #redwine #beans \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=In our attempt to reach our 5 a day target, we're getting a weekly vegetable box from Abel &amp; Cole, which is making us\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2381\n|PortionCalories = 396\n|DatePublished=14th April 2014\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 6\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  1 hour 40 minutes\n|PrepTime =  10 minutes\n|CookTime =  1 hour 30 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Sausage, bean and radicchio hash recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Spicy soup</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Great for a fireside snack</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Carla_Cancio-Bello,_J.D.,_on_behalf_of_Cuban_Cuisine_UK|Carla]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Sausage, bean and radicchio hash on the hob.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Simmering on the hob]]\nIn our attempt to to reach our [[5 a day]] target, we're getting a weekly vegetable box from [[Abel & Cole]], which is making us use vegetables that we might not normally use.  The [[radicchio]] is a good example of this.  The spicy pork sausages and beans should go well with the bitter leaved radicchio.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 3 [[Cloves of Garlic, peeled and crushed|cloves of garlic, peeled and crushed]]\n| 2 [[Red onions|red onions]], peeled and sliced\n| 2 tablespoons of [[Olive oil]]\n| Splash of [[red wine]] (optional)\n| 1 x 200g Mattessons [[Smoked pork|smoked pork]] horseshoe [[Sausage|sausage]], [[Sliced on the diagonal|sliced on the diagonal]]\n| 1 x 225g (8 oz) hot [[Chorizo sausage|chorizo sausage]], sliced\n| 1 x 400g can of [[Cannellini beans|cannellini beans]], rinsed well and drained\n| 1 x 400g can of [[Flageolet beans|flageolet beans]], rinsed well and drained\n| 2 x 400g tinned [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Tomato puree|tomato puree]]\n| 300 ml (1/2 pint) [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]]\n| pinch of [[Chilli flakes|chilli flakes]]\n| pinch of mixed [[herbs]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Tomato puree|tomato puree]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| 1 450 g (1 lb) [[Radicchio|radicchio]], cored and [[Shredded|shredded]]\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Heat the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] in a heavy based pan and add a good pinch of [[Black pepper|black pepper]]\n| Gently [[Saute|saute]] the [[Onions|onions]] for 5 minutes, add the [[Garlic|garlic]] for the last 2 minutes.  Don't let the [[Garlic|garlic]] burn\n| Deglaze the pan with the [[red wine]], if using.\n| Add the [[Chorizo sausage|chorizo sausage]] and [[Fry|fry]] for 3 minutes, turning often\n| Add the horseshoe [[Sausage|sausage]] and [[Fry|fry]] until [[Browned|browned]].\n| Tip in the [[Beans|beans]], tinned [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Tomato puree|tomato puree]], [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]] and the [[Chilli flakes|chilli flakes]], mixed herbs and stir well, bring to the [[Boil|boil]], reduce the heat and [[Simmer|simmer]] for 45 minutes\n| After 45 minutes, add the sliced [[radicchio]], cover and simmer for a further 30 minutes.\n| Check for seasoning and serve.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with crusty [[bread]] or a [[bread roll]] to dip into the sauce.\n\n[[Pasta]], [[rice]] or [[boiled potatoes]] would be nice, but remember that this is very filling and a little goes a long way.\n===Variations===\nUse any variety of [[Cabbage|cabbage]]and any variety of canned [[beans]]. Reconstituted [[dried beans]] would be great providing you leave time to rehydrate them.\n\nI added a sliced up [[courgette]] 30 minutes before the end, as we had one spare. \n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Abel and Cole veg box recipes]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#sausagebeanandradicchiohash #tomatopuree #radicchio #tomatoes #sausage #chickenstock #fry #chilliflakes #oliveoil #redwine #beans </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">In Autumn!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis is a very hearty and filling [[cassoulet]] and perfectly suited to slow cooking.\n\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 3 [[Cloves of Garlic,
