[[Smoked pork|smoked pork]] horseshoe [[Sausage|sausage]], [[Sliced on the diagonal|sliced on the diagonal]]\n| 1 225g (8 oz) hot [[Chorizo sausage|chorizo sausage]], sliced\n| 1 400g can of [[Cannellini beans|cannellini beans]], rinsed well and drained\n| 1 400g can of [[Flageolet beans|flageolet beans]], rinsed well and drained\n| 2 400g tinned [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Tomato puree|tomato puree]]\n| 300 ml (1/2 pint) [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]]\n| Pinch of [[Chilli flakes|chilli flakes]]\n| Pinch of mixed [[herbs]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Tomato puree|tomato [[Shredded|shredded]]\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Heat the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] in a heavy based pan and add a good pinch of [[Black pepper|black pepper]]\n| Gently [[Saute|saute]] the [[Onions|onions]] for 5 minutes, add the [[Garlic|garlic]] for the last 2 minutes.  Don't let the [[Garlic|garlic]] burn\n| Deglaze the pan with the [[red wine]], if using.\n| Reserve the [[onions]] and [[garlic]] to the [[slow cooker]] and add the [[Chorizo sausage|chorizo sausage]] and [[Fry|fry]] for 3 minutes, turning often\n| Add the horseshoe [[Sausage|sausage]] and [[Fry|fry]] until [[Browned|browned]].\n| Add the cooked [[sausages]] to the [[slow cooker]]\n| Tip in the [[Beans|beans]], tinned [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Tomato puree|tomato puree]], [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]] and the [[Chilli flakes|chilli flakes]], mixed herbs and stir well.\n| Add the sliced [[radicchio]], cover and cook on low for 4 hours\n| Check for seasoning and serve.\n}}\n===Variations===\nUse any variety of [[Cabbage|cabbage]]and any variety of canned [[beans]]. Reconstituted [[dried beans]] would be great providing you leave time to rehydrate them.\n\nI added a sliced up [[courgette]] 30 minutes before the end, as we had one spare.\n===Chef's notes===\nIf you like your [[cabbage]] with a little bite, and time allows, add the cabbage during the last 30 minutes of cooking. \n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Slow cooker recipes]]\n[[Category:Slow cooked]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#tomatopuree #garlic #cabbage #redwine #onions #chilliflakes #oliveoil #sausage #chickenstock #tomatoes #fry </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

This recipe is allergy free.\n\nRecipe created by Natural Chef, Ceri Jones and reproduced on [[Cookipedia]] by courtesy of [[Debbie&andrew's sausages|debbie&andrew's sausages]].\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 2 teaspoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 2 [[Cloves garlic, minced|cloves garlic, minced]] \n| 1 teaspoon [[Fennel seeds|fennel seeds]]\n| \u00bd teaspoon [[Dried|dried]] [[Chilli flakes|chilli flakes]] \n| 4 debbie&andrew\u0092s [[Harrogate 97% Pork Sausages]], chopped \n| 10 [[Cherry tomatoes|cherry tomatoes]], quartered \n| 2 large [[Courgettes|courgettes]], [[Julienned|julienned]] (reserve the cores, [[Dice|dice]] them and add to the [[Sauce|sauce]])\n| 25g fresh [[Rocket|rocket]], [[Black pepper|black pepper]] and [[Parmesan cheese]] to serve\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Heat the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] in a large [[Frying pan|frying pan]]. Add the [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Chilli flakes|chilli flakes]], and [[Fennel seeds|fennel seeds]] and [[Fry|fry]] for 30 seconds before adding the raw chopped [[Sausage|sausage]].\n| Cook till the mixture starts to [[Brown|brown]].\n| Next add the [[Diced|diced]] [[Courgette|courgette]] cores along with the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] and cook over a medium heat until the [[Sausages|sausages]] are cooked through, approximately a further 7-8 minutes\n| When the [[Sausages|sausages]] are cooked add the [[Julienned|julienned]] [[Courgette|courgette]] and stir through the [[Sauce|sauce]]. Let the [[Courgettes|courgettes]] warm in the sauce for 2-3 minutes until softened.\n| Plate up and dress with fresh [[Rocket|rocket]], a good dose of [[Black pepper|black pepper]] and a shaving of [[Parmesan cheese]].\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nPlate up and dress with fresh [[Rocket|rocket]], a good dose of [[Black pepper|black pepper]] and a shaving of [[Parmesan cheese]].\n===Chef's notes===\nYou can use a [[Julienne|julienne]] [[Peeler|peeler]] or [[Spiralizer|spiralizer]] to create your [[Courgette spaghetti|courgette spaghetti]]. If you have neither, use a standard peeler to create wider ribbons of [[Courgette|courgette]] instead. Depending on your method there may or may not be any courgette cores for the [[Sauce|sauce]].\n===See also ===\n* [[Oxo Good Grips Julienne peeler]]\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Gluten free recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Debbie&andrew's sausage recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n{{Template:DebbieAndAndrew attribution}}\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#courgettes #sauce #parmesancheese #blackpepper #rocket #courgette #sausages #julienned #peeler #spiralizer #julienne </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Just 3 sausages make 18 meatballs - more than enough for two pizzas! \n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|DatePublished=11th February 2017\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  1 hour, 42 minutes\n|PrepTime =  1 hour, 30 minutes\n|CookTime =  12 minutes\n|TotalCalories = 2380\n|PortionCalories = 1190\n|Image = [[Image:Sausage meatball pizza recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Glorious!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Looks and tastes divine. Fabulous pizza topping.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nYet another [[Pizza|pizza]] recipe!\n[[Image:Meatballs from sausages recipe.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Cooking the meatballs]]\n\nWe got some lovely [[Italian]]-style [[Sausages|sausages]] from [[Gourmet sausage maker - Bexley]] ([[Hall Place Farmers' Market, Bexley, Kent]]), but this time, instead of using them as sausages we would extract the [[Sausagemeat|sausagemeat]] from the sausages and make [[Meatballs|meatballs]] from them to top the [[Pizza|pizza]].\n\nWe managed to get 35 [[Meatballs|meatballs]] from 6 [[Sausages|sausages]]! The 'recipe' is here: [[Meatballs from sausages]]\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| Pinch of [[Black pepper|black pepper]]\n| 2 tablespoons of [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 1 small [[Onion|onion]], very finely chopped\n| Cooked [[Meatballs|meatballs]] from 3 meaty [[Sausages|sausages]]\n| 1 portion of [[Pizza dough]] (makes 2 [[Pizzas|pizzas]])\n| About 6 tablespoons of [[Tomato sauce for pizza]] or [[Passata|passata]]\n| 2 balls [[Mozzarella cheese|mozzarella cheese]] torn into small pieces(about 250g in total)\n| Fresh [[Basil leaves|basil leaves]], chopped finely\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| Half of a Polish pickled red pepper, chopped, ''optional''\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Dust your work surface with [[Fine yellow cornmeal|fine yellow cornmeal]]\n| Divide the [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]] into two and roll out into two thin 25.5 cm (10 inch) [[Pizzas|pizzas]]\n| You can leave them in a [[Warm place|warm place]] for an hour or so to rise. I quite like them cooked immediately they are rolled out for a more crispy finish.\n| Prick the [[Pizza|pizza]] all over with a fork. This prevents it puffing up too much and burning while it is cooking\n| With a deft move, slide the [[Pizza|pizza]] from the [[Pizza peel|pizza peel]], on to the preheated [[Pizza stone|pizza stone]].\n| Cook on one side only for about 2 minutes or until lightly [[Browned|browned]].\n| Remove from the [[Oven|oven]] and distribute a ball of torn [[Mozzarella cheese|mozzarella cheese]] over the  [[Pizza|pizza]].\n| Spread the [[Tomato sauce|tomato sauce]] over the top of the [[Cheese|cheese]] -  this helps to keep the [[Pizza|pizza]] base dry and crispy.\n| Crumble the [[Meatballs|meatballs]] and arrange over the topping and drizzle with [[Olive oil|olive oil]] - preferably the [[Oil|oil]] the meatballs were cooked in.\n| Return to the [[Oven|oven]] and [[Bake|bake]] until the [[Cheese|cheese]] is nicely melted. This should take about 4 minutes under a [[Grill|grill]] on a [[Pizza stone|pizza stone]], if oven [[Baking|baking]], about 15 minutes in the middle of the oven.\n| Repeat for the second [[Pizza|pizza]].\n| Keep the first [[Pizza|pizza]] warm at the bottom of the [[Oven|oven]] whilst you make the second.\n}}\n===Chef's notes===\nUse a little extra [[Olive oil|olive oil]] when cooking the [[Sausage|sausage]] [[Meatballs|meatballs]] and use this flavored [[Oil|oil]] to top the [[Pizza|pizza]] before it is [[Baked|baked]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Pizza recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#pizza #meatballs #oliveoil #sausages #pizzadough #pizzastone #pizzas #cheese #mozzarellacheese #sausagemeatballpizza #panfried </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Savoy cabbage pretend pasta bake\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#cabbage #oliveoil #salami #pasta #panko #mozzarella #parsley #savoycabbage #bake #breadcrumbs #blackcurrantjam \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=For a change, I thought I would make our regular pasta bake, using salami and mozzarella, but use Savoy savoy cabbage instead of actual pasta.\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|DatePublished=17th October 2019\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = Served with scrumptious roasties.\n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  55 minutes\n|PrepTime =  15 minutes\n|CookTime =  40 minutes\n|TotalCalories = 1740\n|PortionCalories = 870\n|Image = [[Image:Savoy cabbage pasta bake recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Delish!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">What a grand idea!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nFor a change, I thought I would make our regular [[Pasta|pasta]] [[Bake|bake]], using [[Salami|salami]] and [[Mozzarella|mozzarella]], but use [[Savoy cabbage|savoy cabbage]] instead of actual [[pasta]].\nTo balance the saltiness of the salami I added a good few tablespoons of [[blackcurrant jam]].  It might seem unusual, but it worked really well and shall be made again. \n\n\nWe served it with air-[[Fried|fried]] [[Roast potatoes|roast potatoes]] to make up for the missing carbs!\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| Two thirds of a small [[Savoy cabbage|savoy cabbage]], tender leaves, finely chopped.\n| A [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]] cube\n| 6 scant teaspoons of [[blackcurrant jam]]\n| 2 125g balls of [[Mozzarella cheese|mozzarella cheese]]\n| 150g [[Salami|salami]], sliced fairly thinly and then chopped\n| A handful of [[Panko]] [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]]\n| Fresh [[Parsley|parsley]], chopped\n| [[Olive oil]]\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Preheat your [[Oven|oven]] to 200\u00b0 C (400\u00b0 F - gas 6), [fan oven 180\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| [[Blanch]] the chopped [[Cabbage|cabbage]] for 4 minutes in [[Boiling|boiling]] water to which the [[Stock cube|stock cube]] has been added.\n| While the [[Cabbage|cabbage]] is cooking, drain the mozarella, tear it into small pieces and allow it to drain over a [[Sieve|sieve]] to remove excess water.\n| Drain the [[Cabbage|cabbage]]\n| Oli the [[Baking tray|baking tray]] / dish with [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| Spread the chopped [[Cabbage|cabbage]] into the dish and sprinkle with chopped [[Parsley|parsley]] and [[Black pepper|black pepper]].\n| Layer the [[Mozzarella|mozzarella]] and [[Salami|salami]], leaving a layer of salami on the top. We like crispy salami!\n| Top with [[Panko]] [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]] and a quick [[Spray|spray]] of [[Olive oil|olive oil]].\n| [[Bake]] for about 40 minutes, checking after 25.\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:SavoyCabbagePastaBaked.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Baked and crispy\nImage:SavoyCabbagePastaReadyToBake.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Raedy for the oven\n</gallery>\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Air fried roast potatoes|air fried roast potatoes]]\n===Recipe source===\n\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pasta recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#cabbage #oliveoil #salami #pasta #panko #mozzarella #parsley #savoycabbage #bake #breadcrumbs #blackcurrantjam </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Sciatt",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Sciatt a cheese recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#sciatt #cheese #fontinacheese #grappa #buckwheatflour #flour #batter #dough #deepfried #beer #bittovaltellinacheese \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Sciatt is a dish typical of Valtellina, Italy\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2584\n|PortionCalories = 430\n|DatePublished=23rd October 2012\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 6\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  1 hour, 30 minutes\n|PrepTime =  1 hour, 15 minutes\n|CookTime =  15 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Sciatt recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Tasty Toad</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.2</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Fried cheesy beery-dough balls - Wow!!!</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Chef|Jerry, aka Chef]]</span></span>\n}}\nSciatt is a dish typical of Valtellina, [[Italy]]. In the local Valtellina dialect it means toad (becaue it is ugly).\n\nSciatt are round crispy [[Dough|dough]] balls made of [[Buckwheat|buckwheat]] with a heart of melted [[Cheese|cheese]], served on a bed of [[Chicory|chicory]].  The [[Cheese|cheese]] is usually [[Bitto Valtellina cheese]].  [[Fontina cheese]] makes a good substitute.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 100 g [[Buckwheat flour|buckwheat flour]]\n| 175 ml Castello Red [[Beer|beer]]\n| 20 ml [[Grappa|grappa]]\n| 500 g [[Fontina cheese|fontina cheese]] or bitto cheese, cut into 2 cm cubes\n| [[Plain flour]] for dusting\n| [[Salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| [[Sunflower oil]] for [[Deep frying|deep frying]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add the [[Buckwheat flour|buckwheat flour]] to a bowl\n| Add the [[Grappa|grappa]]\n| Gradually add the beer whilst whisking until you have a smooth thick [[Batter|batter]] with the consistency of thick [[Whipped cream|whipped cream]]\n| Cover and [[Rest for|rest for]] 1 hour at room temperature\n| Season the [[Flour|flour]] with [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]]\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] to 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F)\n| In small batches, roll each piece of [[Cheese|cheese]] in seasoned [[Flour|flour]], [[Dip|dip]] into the [[Batter|batter]] and [[Deep fry|deep fry]] for about 2 minutes until they are crisp on the outside\n| Drain on kitchen paper\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe on a bed of finely sliced [[Raddichio|raddichio]]\n===Variations===\nUse [[Peroni Red beer]] or any [[Lager|lager]] as a substitute for Castello\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cooking with beer]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Deep fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#sciatt #cheese #fontinacheese #grappa #buckwheatflour #flour #batter #dough #deepfried #beer #bittovaltellinacheese </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

class=\"reviewTitle\">Nice spag. dish Julia</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.7</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span resembling a spiral seashell and this this recipe it is [[Baked|baked]] after being [[Boiled|boiled]].\n[[Image:Sconcigli.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Sconcigli]]\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 100g sconcigli\n| A little [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 1 small [[Onion|onion]], finely sliced\n| 1 stick of [[Celery|celery]], sliced\n| 1 medium yellow or [[Green pepper|green pepper]]\n| [[Garlic]] to taste, finely [[Diced|diced]]\n| 40 g [[Pine nuts|pine nuts]]\n| 1 tin chopped [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n| 100 g [[Sweetcorn|sweetcorn]]\n| 100 g [[Spring greens|spring greens]], [[Shredded|shredded]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Dried oregano|dried oregano]]\n| Seasoning\n| 100g of mixed [[Cheese|cheese]], eg [[Parmesan]], [[Grana Padano cheese|Grana Padano]], [[Fontina]], [[Grated|grated]]\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 200\u00b0 C (400\u00b0 F - gas 6)\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| [[Boil]] the sconcigli for about 12-15 minutes in plenty of [[Salted|salted]], [[Boiling|boiling]] water.\n| When cooked, drain and run onder a cold tap. \n| Meanwhile, heat some [[Olive oil|olive oil]] in a pan and add the [[Onion|onion]], [[Celery|celery]] stick and [[Pepper|pepper]].\n| Cook over a medium heat until the [[Vegetable|vegetable]] begin to soften.\n| Add the [[Garlic|garlic]] and the [[Pine nuts|pine nuts]] and [[Fry|fry]] for a further minute or two.\n| Stir in the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Sweetcorn|sweetcorn]], [[Spring greens|spring greens]] and [[Oregano|oregano]].\n| Bring to the [[Boil|boil]], reduce heat and [[Simmer|simmer]] gently for 5 minutes.\n| Season to taste - under rather than over as the [[Cheese|cheese]] will be salty.\n| Stir in the [[Pasta|pasta]] and mix well.\n| Pour into a greased [[Baking|baking]] dish and sprinkle the [[Cheese|cheese]] over the top.\n| Bake for about 25 minutes.\n}}\n===Variations===\nUse any combination for [[Vegetables|vegetables]], but keep the [[Onion|onion]], [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]].\n\nI like to use [[Vegetable Stock|vegetable stock]] to [[Boil|boil]] [[Pasta|pasta]] for this type of recipe.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian Add the [[Onion|onion]], [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Fennel seeds|fennel seeds]] and cook for 5 minutes until soft.\n| Then add the [[Sausages|sausages]] and [[Brown|brown]] evenly for 8 minutes or so.\n| Stir in the [[Carrots|carrots]] and [[Celery|celery]] and cook for another 5 minutes until the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] start to colour and soften.\n| Stir in the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Parsley|parsley]], [[Oregano|oregano]] and [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]]. A generous sprinkling of fresh dill would make an\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 777\n|PortionCalories = 388\n|DatePublished=7th January 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  1 hour, 16 minutes\n|PrepTime =  1 hour\n|CookTime =  16 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Smoked salmon and blue cheese pizza recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Great mix!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.8</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Never seen this in Pizza Hut! [[Dried|Dried]] [[Herbs|herbs]] are not a good substitute.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 150g of good [[Blue cheese|blue cheese]] - I used [[Saint Agur Blue cheese|Saint Agur]] - nice and creamy\n| 100g thinly sliced [[Smoked salmon|smoked salmon]]\n| 1 small [[Onion|onion]], thinly sliced\n| [[Extra virgin olive oil]]\n| [[Sea Salt|Sea salt]]\n| [[Freshly ground black pepper]]\n| Freshly chopped [[Dill|dill]] to garnish\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Make the [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]] as instructed.\n* If using a [[Pizza stone|pizza stone]], preheat the [[Pizza stone|pizza stone]] under a very hot [[Grill|grill]] for about 20 minutes. Place it about 8cm (3\") from the heat source.\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Make 1 [[Pizza|pizza]] per person\n| Dust your work surface with [[Fine yellow cornmeal|fine yellow cornmeal]]\n| Divide the [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]] into two and roll out into two thin 25.5 cm (10 inch) [[Pizzas|pizzas]]\n| Prick the pizzas all over with a fork. This prevents it puffing up too much and burning while it is cooking\n| With a deft move, slide the [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]] from the [[Pizza peel|pizza peel]], on to the preheated [[Pizza stone|pizza stone]].\n| Cook on one side only for about 2 minutes or until lightly [[Browned|browned]].\n| remove from the [[Oven|oven]], flip over and add the sliced [[Onions|onions]] and a good drizzle of [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and a grind of [[Black pepper|black pepper]].\n| Slide under the [[Grill|grill]] and allow cook for about 3 minutes, just enough for the heat and the [[Oil|oil]] to take the 'edge' off the [[Onions|onions]].\n| Remove from the [[Oven|oven]] and add the crumbled [[Blue cheese|blue cheese]] and the [[Smoked salmon|smoked salmon]].\n| Return to the [[Oven|oven]] just long enough for the [[Cheese|cheese]] to melt.\n| Repeat for the second [[Pizza|pizza]] whilst you prepare the first.\n| Keep the first [[Pizza|pizza]] warm at the bottom of the [[Oven|oven]] whilst you make the second.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with a [[Green salad|green salad]].\n===Variations===\nI used a little [[Truffle oil|truffle oil]] instead of the [[Olive oil|olive oil]], though I have to admit I didn't notice the flavour when eating the [[Pizza|pizza]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Freshwater fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Pizza recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#pizza #smokedsalmonandbluecheesepizza #dill #pizzastone #pizzadough #grill #smokedsalmon #bluecheese #onions #oliveoil #herbs </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Crisp Parmesan cheese lattice nests recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#cheese #solidcrispycheesewafers #rollingpin #parmesan #spain #wafers #pancake #grated #tacos #cookipedia #recipesfromothersites \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=The recipe was created for D\u017eiugas cheeses by the famous food virtuoso from Spain, Mark Audibert\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 646\n|PortionCalories = 323\n|DatePublished=6th November 2015\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime =  20 minutes\n|PrepTime =  5 minutes\n|CookTime =  15 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Solid crispy cheese wafers recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Not so good looking</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">They didn't look like this when I made them the second time, but they tasted fab.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n\n}}\n\nThe recipe was created for [[D\u017eiugas cheeses]] by the famous food virtuoso from [[Spain]], Mark Audibert.  [[D\u017eiugas cheeses]] have kindly given [[Cookipedia]] permission to use this recipe.\n\nAs well as looking stunning, these solid [[Cheese|cheese]] crips also taste fantastic. They look like solid cheese [[Tacos|tacos]] - mmm, now there's an idea!\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 150 g [[D\u017eiugas cheese]], finely [[Grated|grated]]\n| Spray of [[olive oil]]\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Finely grate the [[D\u017eiugas cheese]]\n| Heat a small non-stick [[Frying pan|frying pan]], ''the same size that you want the [[Wafers|wafers]] to be''.\n| Add a small spray of [[olive oil]]\n| Once the pan is hot enough to melt the [[Cheese|cheese]], sprinkle the cheese evenly over the surface of the pan in a thin layer.\n| Once the [[Cheese|cheese]] has crisped up, invert the pan over a [[Rolling pin|rolling pin]] and tap the cheese ''[[Pancake|pancake]] out on to the roller and allow it to cool and harden.\n}}\n===Variations===\nIf you cannot obtain [[D\u017eiugas cheese]], a good quality [[Parmesan]] will work equally well.\n===Chef's notes===\nThe [[Tefal one egg wonder 12 cm mini frying pan]] is absolutely the perfect size for this recipe.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:D\u017eiugas cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#cheese #solidcrispycheesewafers #rollingpin #parmesan #spain #wafers #pancake #grated #tacos #cookipedia #recipesfromothersites </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

[[Vegetables|vegetables]] and seasoning into a saucepan and bring to the [[Boil|boil]].\n| When the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] are almost cooked, st the [[Pasta|pasta]] and cook over a low heat.\n| In the meantime, [[Blend|blend]] the [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Basil|basil]], [[Oil|oil]] and 2 tablespoons of the cooking [[Stock|stock]].\n| When the [[Pasta|pasta]] is cooked, mix in the blended ingredients.\n| Pour into a [[Soup|soup]] tureen and sprinkle with the [[Parmesan]].\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with good [[Bread|bread]]\n===Recipe source===\n\n* Adapted from a recipe in title": "Sourdough bread pizza recipe",

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=No dough Sourdough bread pizza recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#sourdoughbreadpizzarecipe #pizza #salami #redpepper #cheese #lemon #sourdoughbread #oliveoil #bread #sourdough #bake \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Not a true pizza, but this simple idea made a brilliant meal. I used sliced sourdough bread instead of pizza dough.\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|DatePublished=12th March 2017\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime =  45 minutes\n|PrepTime =  30 minutes\n|CookTime =  15 minutes\n|TotalCalories = 1606\n|PortionCalories = 803\n|Image = [[Image:Sourdough bread pizza recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">It's a cheat!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">But a great cheat \ud83e\udd21\ud83e\udd21\ud83e\udd21!</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Chef|Jerry, aka Chef]])</span></span>\n}}\nA no-dough [[pizza]] using sliced sourdough bread and goodies from the fridge.  This made a brilliant meal.\n\nI thought I would make a [[Pizza|pizza]] using a [[Sourdough|sourdough]] loaf instead of [[dough]].  This was fantastic and will be made again and again.\n\nEach [[Pizza|pizza]] was made in a non-stick 20cm x 5cm flan flan tin which is deep enough to hold all that lovely runny [[Cheese|cheese]].\n\nDon't completely fill the base with bread or it will remain quite wet - you need to leave some space around so it can get crispy.\n\nUse whatever ingredients you fancy - [[Salami|salami]] worked well as the flavours run into the [[Bread|bread]].  Though it sounds odd, the slices of [[Lemon|lemon]] tempered the fatty [[Meat|meat]] and the [[Cheese|cheese]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 6 thick slices of white [[Sourdough bread|sourdough bread]] - crusts left on\n| 2 balls of [[Mozzarella cheese|mozzarella cheese]], drained and torn into pieces\n| 150g sliced [[Meat|meat]] such as [[Salami|salami]]\n| 4 very thick slices of [[Lemon|lemon]], skin on but pips removed\n| 1 [[Red pepper|red pepper]] from a bottle of jarred [[Roasted red peppers|roasted red peppers]], chopped into small pieces\n| Lots of freshly torn [[Basil leaves|basil leaves]] - almost &#190; of the plant pictures went into the 2 [[Pizzas|pizzas]]\n| [[Freshly ground black pepper]]\n| Lots of [[Extra virgin Olive oil|extra virgin olive oil]]\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Preheat your [[Oven|oven]] to 200\u00b0 C (400\u00b0 F - gas 6), [fan oven 180\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Sourdough bread pizza ready to bake.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Assembled, ready to bake\nImage:Sourdough bread pizza recipe ingredients.jpg|thumb|300px|right|The ingredients, the nectarine was unused in the end.\n</gallery>\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Lightly [[Oil|oil]] the base of the [[Pie|pie]] / flan dishes\n| Place 3 slices of [[Sourdough bread|sourdough bread]] in each tin\n| Drizzle with [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and sprinkle with [[Black pepper|black pepper]]\n| Layer the sliced [[Meat|meat]], chopped [[Red pepper|red pepper]] and torn [[Mozzarella|mozzarella]] to fill the tin, finding places to bury the [[Lemon slices|lemon slices]]\n| Drizzle with [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| [[Bake]] for 15 minutes in the middle of the [[Oven|oven]] set to 200\u00b0 C (400\u00b0 F - gas 6)\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with a [[Green salad|green salad]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Fruit recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Cookery cheats]]\n[[Category:Pizza recipes]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#sourdoughbreadpizzarecipe #pizza #salami #redpepper #cheese #lemon #sourdoughbread #oliveoil #bread #sourdough #bake </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Sous vide duck pizza",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Sous vide duck pizza recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#pizza #sousvideduckpizza #duck #hoisinsauce #pizzas #pizzadough #sauce #sousvide #mozzarella #cheese #oliveoil \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Any excuse to use my homemade sous-vide cooker because it makes meat so tender. duck is a great candidate for this method of cooking\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 5358\n|PortionCalories = 1339\n|DatePublished=8th April 2015\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = Just enough for one, leaving the last quarter for tomorrow's snack.\n|Servings = Serves 4 - Makes 2 pizzas\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  3 hours, 30 minutes\n|PrepTime =  20 minutes\n|CookTime =  3 hours, 10 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Sous vide duck pizza recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Wow!!!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">That looks SO good!</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nAny excuse to use my homemade [[Homemade sous-vide slow cooker conversion kit|homemade sous vide sous vide cooker]] because it makes [[Meat|meat]] so tender.  [[Duck|duck]] is a great candidate for this as I find sometimes if it's cooked rare, it can be a bit chewy.  This has been [[Sous vide|sous vide]]  cooked for 3 hours at 56.5\u00b0C (''133.7\u00b0F'').  [[Seared]], skin side only to release excess [[Fat|fat]] and then allowed to cool and then sliced thinly and added to the [[Pizza|pizza]]. It was a lot of work but it was delicious. \n\nOne 170g [[Duck|duck]] breast was enough for two [[Pizzas|pizzas]], I [[Sous vide|sous vide]] cooked two and froze the unused one for next weeks duck [[Pizza|pizza]].\n\nI added a teaspoon of [[Hoisin sauce|hoisin sauce]] to the vacuum bag as I think it goes so well with [[Duck|duck]].  That's a personal taste so I guess it is optional.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 170g [[Duck|duck]] breast, skin on.\n| 1 teaspoon [[Hoisin sauce|hoisin sauce]]\n| 1 portion [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]]\n| 4 tablespoons of [[Tomato sauce for pizza|tomato sauce for pizzas]]\n| 250g [[Mozzarella cheese|mozzarella cheese]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| A pinch of [[Dried oregano|dried oregano]]\n| A drizzle of [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\nIf using a pizza stone, preheat the pizza stone under a very hot grill for about 20 minutes. Place it about 8cm (3\") from the heat source.\n\nIf using the oven, preheat it to 220\u00b0 C (425\u00b0 F - gas 7)\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Sous vide duck pizza.jpg|Fresh out of the oven\nImage:Sous vide duck pizza tomato topping.jpg|Spreading out the topping\nImage:Sous vide duck pizza ready for the oven.jpg|Ready for the oven\nImage:Sous vide duck pizza one breast.jpg|One breast, two pizzas\nImage:Sous vide duck pizza seared.jpg|Duck breast seared\n</gallery>\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| [[Vacuum seal]] the [[Duck|duck]] breast together with 1 teaspoon of [[Hoisin sauce|hoisin sauce]]\n| Cook in a [[Sous vide bath|sous vide bath]] for 3 hours at 56.5\u00b0C\n| Remove from the vacuum bag, discarding the [[Sauce|sauce]], it will have done its job and flavoured the [[Meat|meat]].\n| Allow to [[Rest for|rest for]] 10 minutes.\n| Heat a [[Frying pan|frying pan]] over a medium high flame\n| Wipe any [[Sauce|sauce]] from the skin side of the [[Duck|duck]] breast and [[Sear|sear]] (skin side only) in the hot pan for 3 minutes without adding any extra [[Oil|oil]].\n| Allow to cool and slice thinly.  This can all be done way ahead of cooking the [[Pizza|pizza]].\n| Dust your work surface with [[Fine yellow cornmeal|fine yellow cornmeal]]\n| Divide the [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]] into two and roll out into two thin 25.5 cm (10 inch) [[Pizzas|pizzas]]\n| You can leave them in a [[Warm place|warm place]] for an hour or so to rise. I quite like them cooked immediately they are rolled out for a more crispy finish.\n| Prick the [[Pizza|pizza]] all over with a fork. This prevents it puffing up too much and burning while it is cooking\n| With a deft move, slide the [[Pizza|pizza]] from the [[Pizza peel|pizza peel]], on to the preheated [[Pizza stone|pizza stone]].\n| Cook on one side only for about 2 minutes or until lightly [[Browned|browned]].\n| Repeat for the other side.\n| Remove from the [[Oven|oven]] and spread the pizza with 2 tablespoons of [[Tomato sauce for pizza|tomato sauce for pizza]].\n| Crumble a ball of [[mozzarella]] cheese over the pizza and top with the sliced duck.\n| Season with salt, pepper a drizzle of olive oil and a pinch of oregano.\n| Return to the [[Oven|oven]] and bake until the [[Cheese|cheese]] is nicely melted. This should take about 4 minutes under a grill on a pizza stone, if oven baking, about 15 minutes in the middle of the oven.\n| Repeat for the second [[Pizza|pizza]].\n| Keep the first [[Pizza|pizza]] warm at the bottom of the [[Oven|oven]] whilst you make the second.\n}}\n===See also===\n* [[Sous vide hoisin duck pizza]]\n* [[Crispy duck and hoisin pizza]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Pizza recipes]]\n[[Category:Sous vide recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Sous vide cooking]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#pizza #sousvideduckpizza #duck #hoisinsauce #pizzas #pizzadough #sauce #sousvide #mozzarella #cheese #oliveoil </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Sous vide duck pizza hosin sauce mozzarella cheese recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#hoisinsauce #pizza #pizzadough #pizzas #chillioil #cherrytomatoes #sousvidecooking #mozzarellacheese #sousvide #sauce #warmplace \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Sous vide duck is cooked to medium then crisped on a pizza base under the grill.\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2843\n|PortionCalories = 710\n|DatePublished=23rd march 2016\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment =\n|Servings = Serves 4 - Makes 2 pizzas\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  3 hours, 30 minutes\n|PrepTime =  20 minutes\n|CookTime =  3 hours, 10 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Sous vide duck pizza alt recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Perfect!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">If you like pizza and you like Chinese, you'll just love this!</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Chef|Jerry, aka Chef]])</span></span>\n}}\nWe've made [[sous vide]] duck [[pizzas]] before but the difference to this one was using [[hoisin sauce]] in place of the tomato topping. Very ''[[Chinese]]''!\n[[Image:Sous vide duck pizza alt.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Sous vide hoisin duck pizza, ready to bake]]\n\nWe used the [[Gressingham duck breast portions]] which are quite small at 125g each and also end up quite wet.  Fresh duck breast is quite dry and firm.  Still an exceptionally good pizza. \n\n'''for the sous vide duck breasts'''\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 pack [[Gressingham duck breast portions]] (2 x 125g duck breasts)\n| 1 tablespoon hoisin sauce \n}}\n\n'''for the pizza'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 1 portion [[pizza dough]]\n| 30 ml [[Hoisin sauce|hoisin sauce]]\n| 1 portion [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]]\n| 2 sliced sous vide duck breasts\n| 8 [[cherry tomatoes]]\n| 2 balls of [[Mozzarella cheese|mozzarella cheese]]\n| [[Sea salt]]\n| Freshly ground [[black pepper]]\n| 2 teaspoons [[Chilli oil]]\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\nIf using a pizza stone, preheat the pizza stone under a very hot grill for about 20 minutes. Place it about 8cm (3\") from the heat source.\n\nIf using the oven, preheat it to 220\u00b0 C (425\u00b0 F - gas 7)\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| [[Vacuum seal]] the [[Duck|duck]] breasts together with 1 tablespoon easpoon of [[Hoisin sauce|hoisin sauce]]\n| Cook in a [[Sous vide bath|sous vide bath]] for 3 hours at 61\u00b0C [141\u00b0F]\n| Remove from the vacuum bag, discarding the [[Sauce|sauce]], it will have done its job and flavoured the [[Meat|meat]].\n| Slice the duck breast and lay on a paper towel to remove any excess water - these packaged duck breasts seem to be pumped full of water\n| Dust your work surface with [[Fine yellow cornmeal|fine yellow cornmeal]]\n| Divide the [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]] into two and roll out into two thin 25.5 cm (10 inch) [[Pizzas|pizzas]]\n| You can leave them in a [[Warm place|warm place]] for an hour or so to rise. I quite like them cooked immediately they are rolled out for a more crispy finish.\n| Prick the [[Pizza|pizza]] all over with a fork. This prevents it puffing up too much and burning while it is cooking\n| With a deft move, slide the [[Pizza|pizza]] from the [[Pizza peel|pizza peel]], on to the preheated [[Pizza stone|pizza stone]].\n| Cook on one side only for about 2 minutes or until lightly [[Browned|browned]].\n| Repeat for the other side.\n| Remove from the [[Oven|oven]] and cover the pizza base with a good drizzle of [[hoisin sauce]]\n| Crumble a ball of [[mozzarella]] cheese over the pizza\n| Top with the sliced duck and 4 halved [[cherry tomatoes]]\n| Season with salt, pepper a drizzle of [[chilli oil]]olive\n| Return to the [[Oven|oven]] and bake until the [[Cheese|cheese]] is nicely melted. This should take about 4 minutes under a grill on a pizza stone, if oven baking, about 15 minutes in the middle of the oven.\n| Repeat for the second [[Pizza|pizza]].\n| Keep the first [[Pizza|pizza]] warm at the bottom of the [[Oven|oven]] whilst you make the second.\n}}\nOnce the pizzas had been cooked a lot of water was released from the duck.  I just mopped this up with a [[paper towel]] and the pizza was still fabulous.  Fresh duck breasts would not do this.\n===See also===\n*[[Sous vide duck pizza]]\n* [[Crispy duck and hoisin pizza]], similar but with tomato topping\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Pizza recipes]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Sous vide recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Sous vide cooking]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#hoisinsauce #pizza #pizzadough #pizzas #chillioil #cherrytomatoes #sousvidecooking #mozzarellacheese #sousvide #sauce #warmplace </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                "revisions": [

#parsley #sauce #colander #beef #onions #simmer \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=An old favourite which was very popular in the UK in the 1960s and 1970s\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 3855\n|PortionCalories = 963\n|DatePublished=25th October 2012\n|Author = JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = Spaghetti alla Bolognese\n |Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 1 hour 45 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 1 hour 30 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Spaghetti alla Bolognese style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Absolutely fabulous, saucy and scrummy.</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nAn old favourite which was very popular in the UK in the 1960s and 1970s.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 50 ml [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 2 medium [[Carrots|carrots]], scraped and finely [[Diced|diced]]\n| 2 [[Celery|celery]] sticks, finely [[Diced|diced]] (include the leaves is you have them)\n| 2 medium [[Red onions|red onions]], peeled and coarsely [[Diced|diced]]\n| 4 bulbs of [[Garlic]], (or as much as you like), peeled and finely [[Diced|diced]]\n| 4 tablespoons fresh [[Parsley|parsley]], finely chopped\n| 450 g [[Beef|beef]], [[Minced|minced]]\n| 40 g [[Butter|butter]]\n| 2 x 400 g tins chopped [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n| seasoning\n| 1 teaspoon [[Sugar|sugar]]\n| 400 g [[Spaghetti|spaghetti]]\n| 25g [[Parmesan cheese]], freshly [[Grated|grated]] (optional)\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a deep saut\u00e9 or [[Frying pan|frying pan]] on a high heat.\n| When hot, but not [[Smoking|smoking]], add the [[Carrots|carrots]], [[Celery|celery]], [[Onions|onions]], [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Parsley|parsley]].\n| Reduce the heat to medium and  cook until the [[Onions|onions]] are soft.\n| Add the [[Beef|beef]] and when [[Brown|brown]], add the [[Butter|butter]] and the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]].\n| Cover and [[Simmer|simmer]] for 1 hour.\n| Add the [[Sugar|sugar]] and [[Simmer|simmer]] gently for a further 30 minutes.\n| Meanwhile, [[Boil|boil]] up three kettles-full of water and pour into a large saucepan.\n| Once the water is [[Boiling|boiling]], add the [[Spaghetti|spaghetti]] and cook for 7-8 minutes.  Place a metal [[Colander|colander]] over the pan containing the spaghetti to warm it up.\n| When the [[Spaghetti|spaghetti]] is cooked, remove the [[Colander|colander]] and place over ab large bowl or the sink. \n| Drain the [[Pasta|pasta]] and plate it immediately.\n| Cover with the [[Sauce|sauce]] and serve, sprinkled with [[Grated|grated]] [[Parmesan]] if desired.\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:In the pan.jpg|thumb|300px|right|In the pan\nImage:Diced herbs and vegetables.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Diced herbs and vegetables\n</gallery>\n===Serving suggestions===\nGreat on its own, but decent [[Bread|bread]] and a crisp [[Salad|salad]] would make excellent accompaniments for the hungry or greedy.\n===Variations===\nI don't think that you can vary this recipe too much and still call it '[[Spaghetti]] alla Bolognese'.  The Italians seem to have a different name for each variation!\n===Chef's notes===\nI think you can use any [[Pasta|pasta]] of the [[Spaghetti|spaghetti]] type, but do avoid thick, short pasta such as penne, [[Macaroni|macaroni]] etc as the [[Sauce|sauce]] is not suited to it.\n\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Spaghetti alla bolognese]]\n[[Category:Beef recipes|Spaghetti alla bolognese]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes|Spaghetti alla bolognese]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Spaghetti alla bolognese]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes|Spaghetti alla bolognese]]\n[[Category:Pasta recipes|Spaghetti alla bolognese]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes|Spaghetti alla bolognese]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]][[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#spaghetti #diced #spaghettiallabologneserecipe #celery #garlic #parsley #sauce #colander #beef #onions #simmer </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Spaghetti alla carbonara",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Spaghetti alla carbonara a cheese recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#spaghettiallacarbonara #pancetta #grated #garlic #parsley #boil #eggs #pecorinosardo #cheese #oliveoil #spaghetti \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=The classic Italian - Spaghetti alla Carbonara literally means \"Spaghetti in the Manner of the Charcoal Maker\"\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2864\n|PortionCalories = 716\n|DatePublished=25th October 2012\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime = 25 minutes\n|PrepTime = 10 minutes\n|CookTime = 15 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Spaghetti alla carbonara recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">A household staple</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.7</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">We have this weekly - with LOTS of Parmesan</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Carla_Cancio-Bello,_J.D.,_on_behalf_of_Cuban_Cuisine_UK|Carla]] </span></span>\n}}\n\nThe classic Italian - '''Spaghetti alla Carbonara''' literally means \"[[Spaghetti]] in the Manner of the Charcoal Maker\". Some believe that the dish was once popular with Charcoal makers who lived on the Mountains near Rome because the ingredients were easily portable and cooking was fairly uncomplicated. Others believe the dish derives its name from all the freshly ground pepper that is added to the spaghetti at the last minute. Actually, the origin of the dish is quite recent, since it was unknown before Second World War. The dish uses [[pancetta]] or [[guanciale]], which are similar to [[bacon]]. If you want to stay true to the Roman heritage of the dish, you must use grated [[Pecorino Romano]] cheese, but it can be substituted by [[Pecorino sardo]] or [[Parmesan]]. A mix of the two cheeses is also common.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 400 g (14 oz) [[dried spaghetti]]\n| 175 g (6&frac14; oz) piece [[Smoked|smoked]] [[Pancetta|pancetta]] with the rind removed or of course, [[Home smoked bacon|home smoked bacon]]!\n| 2 tablespoons [[Extra virgin olive oil|extra virgin olive oil]]\n| 3 [[Garlic cloves, peeled and crushed|garlic cloves, peeled and crushed]]\n| A good handful of [[Parsley|parsley]], stalks removed and finely chopped\n| 3 large free-range [[Eggs|eggs]], beaten\n| 50 g (1&frac34; oz) [[Pecorino sardo]], finely [[Grated|grated]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| [[Boil]] 4.5 [[Litres|litres]] (8 [[Pints|pints]]) of water in a large pot and add 2 teaspoons of [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| Add the spaghetti and cook for ten minutes - timed once it returns to the [[Boil|boil]]\n| Meanwhile, cut the [[Pancetta|pancetta]] into bite-size pieces \n| Heat a large [[Frying pan|frying pan]] or [[Wok|wok]] over a medium-high heat, add the [[Oil|oil]] and [[Pancetta|pancetta]] and [[Fry|fry]] for a few minutes\n| Add the [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Parsley|parsley]] and cook for long enough to colour the [[Garlic|garlic]], being careful not to burn it. Set aside\n| Drain the spaghetti then pour into the [[Frying pan|frying pan]] with the [[Pancetta|pancetta]], [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Parsley|parsley]] and a little splash of [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| Stir in the beaten [[Eggs|eggs]] and half of the [[Grated|grated]] [[Cheese|cheese]] and mix together well\n| Season with a little [[Salt|salt]] and [[Black pepper|black pepper]]\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\n\nServe hot, garnished with the remaining [[Grated|grated]] [[Cheese|cheese]]\n\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Pasta recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]][[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#spaghettiallacarbonara #pancetta #grated #garlic #parsley #boil #eggs #pecorinosardo #cheese #oliveoil #spaghetti </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }

It's quite a soupy version, with a rich winey flavour\"\nThis [[Freeze|freeze]]s really well, so make the lot and freeze what you don't eat.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 kg good quality very lean [[Minced beef|minced beef]], or 500g very lean [[Minced|minced]] [[Beef|beef]] and 500g very lean minced [[Pork|pork]]\n| 1 tablespoon of [[butter]]\n| 1 tablespoon of [[olive oil]]\n| 1 large [[Onion|onion]]\n| 1 [[Clove|clove]] [[Garlic|garlic]] or to taste.\n| 250g chopped [[Button mushrooms|button mushrooms]], or 6 finely chopped [[Dried|dried]] [[Porcini|porcini]] [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]] or [[shiitake mushrooms]] soaked in [[Milk|milk]] for 20 minutes\n| 2.5 tablespoons of [[Plain flour|plain flour]]\n| 1 &#189; tins of [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n| 300mls good [[Red wine|red wine]]\n| 200mls [[Beef Stock|beef stock]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[tomato pur\u00e9e]]\n| 2 tablespoons chopped curly leaf [[Parsley|parsley]] (other [[Herbs|herbs]] can be added)\n| [[Sea salt]] and freshly ground [[black pepper]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Gently [[Fry|fry]] [[Onions|onions]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] in [[Oil|oil]] and [[Butter|butter]] for 10 minutes until melting\n| Add [[Mince|mince]] slowly, turning and stirring gently until cooked thoroughly, keeping the mixture dry\n| Add [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]] and cook till soft\n| Mix in [[Flour|flour]] and cook through for a minute or so\n| Add tomatoes, salt and pepper, &#190; of the [[Parsley|parsley]] and the [[tomato pur\u00e9e]] , and stir well. Cook for 3 - 4 minutes. Add [[Wine|wine]] and [[Beef Stock|beef stock]], cover wth a lid and [[Simmer|simmer]] very gently for 60 minutes, checking every now and then to make sure it's not catching. The [[Sauce|sauce]] should still be fairly liquid at the end of cooking\n| Serve with [[Spaghetti|spaghetti]], more chopped [[Parsley|parsley]], and [[Parmesan]]\n}}\n===Chef's notes===\nThe only change I would make to this recipe is to add a [[Bay leaf|bay leaf]] while [[Simmering|simmering]] and to garnish with plenty of chopped fresh [[Basil|basil]].\n===Chef's notes===\n{{Template:ThinkPig}}\n\n{{Template:YoutubePastaDough}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Beef recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pasta recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Nik and Edwina's Cookbook recipes]]\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]][[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#parsley #butter #beefstock #mushrooms #garlic #fry #pork #buttonmushrooms #mincedbeef #wine #dried </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

682\n|DatePublished=7th November 2012\n|Author = JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 1 hour 30 minutes\n |PrepTime = 30 minutes (porcini soaking etc)\n |CookTime = 1 hour\n |Image = [[Image:Spaghetti tutto mare recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Looks perfect Julia!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Mine didn't look as good as yours, but it was lovely.</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Spaghetti]] with [[Seafood|seafood]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 500g total [[Squid|squid]] and pre cooked and shelled [[Mussels|mussels]]\n| 90ml [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 250ml [[Dry white wine|dry white wine]]\n| 400g tinned [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], liquidised\n| [[Chilli]], chopped or [[Bird's eye chilli paste|bird's eye chilli paste]] to taste\n| Seasoning\n| 40g [[Dried|dried]] [[Porcini|porcini]] [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]], soaked and thinly sliced\n| 1 small [[Carrot|carrot]], chopped\n| 1 small [[Onion|onion]], chopped\n| [[Garlic]] to taste, finely [[Diced|diced]]\n| 1 tablespoon dried [[Oregano|oregano]]\n| 400g [[Spaghetti|spaghetti]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat half the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and add the [[Squid|squid]].\n| [[Brown]] gently, then increase the heat and add half the [[Wine|wine]].\n| Allow the [[Wine|wine]] to reduce, lower the heat and add the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Chilli|chilli]] and a little [[Salt|salt]].\n| [[Simmer]] until the [[Squid|squid]] is tender.\n| Add the [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]] and cook for a further 15 minutes.\n| Meanwhile, heat the rest of the [[Oil|oil]] in another pan and [[Fry|fry]] the [[Onion|onion]] and [[Carrot|carrot]] until the onion is soft, adding the [[Garlic|garlic]], a couple of minutes before the end of the cooking time.\n| Add the [[Mussels|mussels]] and the remaining [[Wine|wine]] and cook over a high heat for 5-10 minutes.\n| At the same time, [[Boil|boil]] the [[Spaghetti|spaghetti]] in [[Salted|salted]] water, drain and transfer to a warm bowl.\n| Mix the [[Squid|squid]] and [[Mussel|mussel]] mixtures together, season, and pour over the [[Spaghetti|spaghetti]].\n| Mix well and serve immediately, garnished with the [[oregano]].\n}}\n===Variations===\nYou can also include shelled [[Prawns|prawns]] in the [[Mussel|mussel]] mixture.\n===Chef's notes===\nI don't mess about with shells on [[Fish|fish]], so I used some excellent [[Frozen|frozen]], cooked and shelled [[Mussels|mussels]].  If you do this, then the cooking time will need to be adjusted accordingly.\n\nI used [[Bird's eye chilli paste|bird's eye chilli paste]] and found that a good &frac14; teaspoon per person was about right.  I allowed 1 bulb of [[Garlic|garlic]] per person, but use as much or as little as you like.\n\n{{Template:YoutubePastaDough}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Pasta recipes]]\n[[Category:Sea fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]][[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#squid #spaghetti #wine #garlic #mussels #spaghettituttomare #chilli #mussel #carrot #mushrooms #oliveoil </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Spaghetti with garlic, courgettes, Parmesan and lemon recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe us recently and it was so good that I scribbled the recipe ideas down and have attempted to reproduce it here.\n\nIt's a quick and easy recipe that makes interesting use of [[Courgettes|courgettes]], spaghetti|dried spaghetti]]\n| [[Zest]] from 1 [[Grapefruit|grapefruit]] or 2 [[Lemons|lemons]]\n| 3 [[Courgettes|courgettes]], [[Grated|grated]]\n| Bunch of fresh [[Parsley|parsley]], chopped\n| 70g crushed]]\n| 2 fresh [[Green Indian chillies|green indian chillies]], finely chopped (de-seeded if you dont want this too hot)\n}}\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Cook the [[Spaghetti|spaghetti]] in lightly [[Salted|salted]] [[Boiling|boiling]] water until [[Al-dente|al-dente]] (about 7 to 10 minutes)\n| While the [[Pasta|pasta]] is cooking, heat the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] in a [[Frying pan|frying pan]] or a [[Wok|wok]] and add a good grind of [[Black pepper|black pepper]]\n| [[Fry]] the [[Garlic|garlic]] for 3 minutes, don't let it [[Brown|brown]]\n| Add the [[Lemon zest|lemon zest]] and [[Grated|grated]] [[Courgettes|courgettes]] and cook until softened or done to your liking.\n| Cooking the [[courgettes]] produces a lot of liquid.  Ideally try reduce this a little over a high heat.  If there is too much then drain some of it, but not all as it makes a very good sauce.  \n| Add the chopped [[Chillies|chillies]] and [[Stir fry|stir fry]] for a few seconds, then add the drained [[Pasta|pasta]].\n| Add the chopped [[Parsley|parsley]], mix well and serve\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Grated|grated]] [[Parmesan cheese]]\n===Recipe source===\n* Jack and Maureen\n===Chef's notes===\nFollowing comments made by [[Julia]] that there were not enough [[courgettes]], I've amended the recipe for 2 people, by reducing the pasta quantity and slightly reducing the amount of courgettes, but keeping the remaining ingredients the same. I thought this made a good balanced meal.  It will be made again. \nIf you don't cut the [[Citrus fruit|citrus fruit]] once you have removed the [[Zest|zest]], they will be good for juicing for a few days, so they won't be wasted.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Stir fried]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#courgettes #grated #spaghettiwithgarliccourgettesparmesanandlemon #pasta #zest #spaghetti #oliveoil #parsley #parmesancheese #fry #wok </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Spam pizza",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Spam pizza a cheese recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#spam #fineyellowcornmeal #pizzapeel #spampizza #pizzastone #oliveoil #pizzadough #bake #ham #pizza #cheese \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=I just love Spam so this is a must-make\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2107\n|PortionCalories = 526\n|DatePublished=1st November 2012\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 4 - Makes 2 [[Pizzas|pizzas]]\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  1 hour 25 minutes<br />Includes making the dough\n|PrepTime = 1 hour 15 minutes  \n|CookTime =  10 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Spam pizza recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">SPAM - Perfect on a pizza</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Despite its bad name (in food and in email), Spam can be so brilliant on a pizza. It also tastes much less greasy when hot.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nI just love [[Spam]] so this is a must-make. [[Spam]] cooks up really well when grilled at a very high heat so is ideal for a [[Stone baked pizza]].\n\nIf you really don't like the idea of using [[Spam]], use fresh [[ham]] instead.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 portion [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]] - Makes 2 pizzas\n| 150 g ball of [[Mozzarella cheese|mozzarella cheese]], torn into pieces\n| 1 340 g can of [[Spam]] original (chopped pork and ham), cut into thin strips.\n| [[Extra virgin olive oil]] for drizzling\n| 1 cup [[Spicy tomato sauce|spicy tomato sauce]]\n| Handful of [[Basil leaves|basil leaves]], torn\n| 1 tablespoon [[Fine yellow cornmeal|cornmeal]]\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Make the [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]] as instructed\n* If using a [[pizza stone]], preheat the [[pizza stone]] under a very hot [[grill]] for about 20 minutes.  Place it about 8cm (3\") from the heat source.\n\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Make 1 pizza per person\n| Dust the work surface with [[Fine yellow cornmeal|fine yellow cornmeal]]\n| Stretch or roll the [[Dough|dough]] into two thin rounds\n| Prick the pizza all over with a fork. This prevents it puffing up too much and burning while it is cooking\n| Place the pizza dough on a [[pizza peel]] that has been dusted with [[Fine yellow cornmeal|fine yellow cornmeal]]\n| With a deft move, slide the pizza dough from the [[pizza peel]], on to the [[pizza stone]].\n| Cook for about 2 minutes on one side only or until lightly browned.\n| Remove from the oven, flip over and add the topping.\n| Repeat for the second pizza whilst you prepare the first.\n| Drizzle the [[Pizza|pizza]] with [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and spread the pizza with &frac12; of the [[Tomato sauce|tomato sauce]]\n| Top with torn [[Mozzarella|mozzarella]] and sliced [[Spam]].\n| Add a final drizzle of [[olive oil]] or for a spicy touch, some [[chili oil]].\n| [[Bake]] for 3 or 4  minutes or until the [[Cheese|cheese]] browns a little - watch it carefully as it can burn easily.\n| Remove and sprinkle with torn [[Basil|basil]].\n| Keep the fist pizza warm at the bottom of the oven whilst you make the second.\n| Serve hot\n}}\n===Chef's note===\nIf you don't have a [[pizza peel]] use an upturned plate or a flat baking tray, dusted with [[Fine yellow cornmeal|fine yellow cornmeal]] and some deft handwork to slide the dough onto the stone.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Pizza recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#spam #fineyellowcornmeal #pizzapeel #spampizza #pizzastone #oliveoil #pizzadough #bake #ham #pizza #cheese </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }

Because the [[Ravioli|ravioli]] is cooked in the sauce, rather than water, it does not matter so much if they leak a little, which they usually do.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 10 large [[King prawns|king prawns]], shelled and de-veined (mine were [[Frozen|frozen]] and [[defrosted]])\n| Splash of [[Nam pla|nam pla]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Ghee|ghee]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 3 [[Fat|fat]] Cloves of [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled and crushed\n| 2.5 cm [[Ginger|ginger]], peeled and finely chopped\n| Big splash of [[Louisiana Hot Pepper Sauce|Louisiana hot pepper sauce]] ([[Tabasco]] does just as well)\n| Pinch of [[Salt|salt]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Cornflour|cornflour]] - see Chef's notes\n| Home made [[Pasta|pasta]] (100 g [[Flour|flour]], 3 [[Egg yolks|egg yolks]], pinch [[Salt|salt]], 1 teaspoon [[Dried|dried]] [[Parsley|parsley]]\n| Leave the pasta in the [[Fridge|fridge]] for a few hours before rolling out\n| Roll out into quite thick sheets, the middle setting on our [[Imperia pasta machine]])\n}}\n'''[[Sauce]]'''\n* 1 can [[Lobster|lobster]] biqsue\n* 150 ml [[Single cream|single cream]]\n* 40 ml [[dry sherry]]\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:12 Spicy prawn ravioli.jpg|12 of the best!\nImage:making spicy prawn ravioli.jpg|Wet the edges for a better join\nImage:Ginger and garlic prawns with chilli.jpg|Garlic and ginger prawns and a big splash of Louisiana hot pepper sauce\n</gallery>\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| [[Fresh pasta|Make the fresh pasta as shown here]], adding 1 tablespoon [[Dried|dried]] [[Parsley|parsley]] - fresh would be better but ours is a bit mangy this time of year.  I left the pasta in the [[Fridge|fridge]] for a good while in the hope the parsley would rehydrate a little.\n| Soak the [[Prawns|prawns]] in the [[Nam pla|nam pla]] for an hour or so.  I like to do this as it makes them even fishier.  You could omit this if you don't have the inclination!\n| Blitz the [[Prawns|prawns]] for a few seconds in a [[Food processor|food processor]] (or [[Delia's chopper]] - ordered but not yet arrived!) - The resulting mix should be [[Rice|rice]]-[[Grain|grain]] sized pieces of [[Prawn|prawn]], not pur\u00e9e.\n| Heat the [[Ghee|ghee]] and [[Olive oil|olive oil]], add the [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Ginger|ginger]] and [[Fry|fry]] off until it just starts to colour, stir in the [[Prawn|prawn]] mixture and stir constantly so it mixes well and cooks evenly\n| When the [[Prawn|prawn]] stars to colour, remove from the heat, add a pinch of salt and the hot pepper sauce.  I added a little [[Cornflour|cornflour]] to thicken at this stage, though there may be better ways.  Allow to cool a little.\n| Roll out the [[Pasta|pasta]] using the middle setting on an [[Imperia pasta machine]] - too thin and the [[Ravioli|ravioli]] has a tendency to leak\n| Cut the [[Pasta|pasta]] into strips about 4 cm wide\n| Place just under a tablespoon of the mix on the [[Pasta|pasta]], avoid getting [[Oil|oil]] on the edges as they won't stick well\n| Wet the edges of the [[Ravioli|ravioli]] fold over, press together with your fingers, finishing with the back of a fork.\n| Place on a lightly floured plate\n| Add the [[Sherry|sherry]] to the [[Lobster bisque|lobster bisque]] and gently heat in a large pan until [[Simmering|simmering]], add the [[Ravioli|ravioli]] and [[Simmer|simmer]], covered, for another 8 minutes\n| remove from the heat, gently stir in the [[Cream|cream]] and serve immediately\n}}\n===Chef's notes===\nI used [[Cornflour|cornflour]] to thicken the [[Prawn|prawn]] mixture as there was quite a lot of liquid which I wanted to keep.  There may be better ways of doing this but cornflour worked.\n===Variations===\nIt might be nice to add a little [[Mascarpone cheese|mascarpone cheese]] to the mixture for a really rich meal!\n==See also==\n{{Template:PeelingGinger}}\n{{Template:Lobster recipes}}\n\n{{Template:YoutubePastaDough}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Pasta recipes]]\n[[Category:Sea fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Shellfish recipes]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#ravioli #pasta #prawn #spicyprawnravioliinlobsterbisque #cornflour #oliveoil #nampla #ginger #fridge #imperiapastamachine #prawns </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

TM31 users may need to reduce the ingredient\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 986\n|PortionCalories = 39\n|DatePublished=20th October 2014\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Servings: 25 - Makes  about 1.8 litres\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  1 hour 55 minutes\n|PrepTime =  15 minutes\n|Cook time = 1 hour 40 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Spicy tomato sauce for pizzas.jpg|alt=Electus]] \n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Thanks Julia!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">It's an absolute honour for you to say this about my recipe!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Chef|Jerry]] </span></span>\n\n}}\nThis [[Sauce|sauce]] is excellent for [[Pizzas|pizzas]], but can also be used with [[Pasta|pasta]]. title": "Stromboli",

teaspoons [[Salt|salt]]\n| Pinch of [[Sugar|sugar]]\n| 15g [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n}}\n'''For the filling'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 3 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| [[Garlic]] to taste, finely chopped\n| 50g [[Sun dried tomatoes|sun dried tomatoes]], chopped\n| A handful of [[Basil leaves|basil leaves]]\n| 250g [[Smoked|smoked]] [[Scamorza cheese|scamorza cheese]]\n| 125g [[Mozzarella cheese|mozzarella cheese]]\n}}\n'''For the topping'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 1 tablespoon [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Coarse sea salt|coarse sea salt]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| [[Crumble]] and dissolve the [[Yeast|yeast]] in half of the water.\n| [[Sieve]] the [[Flour|flour]] and [[Salt|salt]] into a mixing bowl.\n| When the [[Yeast|yeast]] has dissolved mix it in with the [[Flour|flour]] and add the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and the rest of the water as needed to form a moist [[Dough|dough]] - it is better for the dough to be a little bit too wet than too dry.\n| Leave to rest for 10 minutes.\n| Lightly [[Flour|flour]] a work surface and your hands and [[Knead|knead]] the [[Dough|dough]] for about 10 minutes until smooth and elastic.  Don't worry about the dough sticking to your hands as it will become less moist as you work it.\n| Shape into a ball, place in an oiled bowl and cover with [[Clingfilm|clingfilm]].\n| Leave until the [[Dough|dough]] has almost doubled in size (about an hour).\n| Gently [[Knock back|knock back]] with your finger tips and repeat steps 6 and 7, but the [[Proving|proving]] should only take about 45 minutes.\n| Generously [[Flour|flour]] your worksurface and using a [[Rolling pin|rolling pin]], roll out the [[Dough|dough]] into a rectangle about 1cm thick.\n| [[Brush]] the [[Dough|dough]] with the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and sprinkle with the [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Sun dried tomatoes|sun dried tomatoes]], the [[Basil leaves|basil leaves]] and the [[Cheeses|cheeses]].\n| Roll up the [[Dough|dough]] like a [[Swiss]] roll, stretching the dough if necessary to ensure that the filling ingredients are completely encased.\n| Place on a [[Baking tray|baking tray]] and allow to prove until almost doubled in size.\n| Make some holes in the top of the [[Dough|dough]] so that he [[Cheese|cheese]] erupts through them.\n| [[Brush]] with a tablespoon of [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and sprinkle with the [[Sea Salt|sea salt]].\n| [[Bake]] at 190\u00b0 C (375\u00b0 F - gas 5), [fan [[Oven|oven]] 170\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour] for 25 minutes and turn the baking tray around.\n| Increase the temperature to 220\u00b0 C (425\u00b0 F - gas 7), [fan oven 200\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour] and bake for a further 20 minutes.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nLovely on its own, or with [[Salad|salad]].\n===Variations===\nYou could also add 6 slices of [[Parma ham]].\n===Chef's notes===\nMake sure the holes are big enough or they will close during baking.\n==See also==\n* '''[[Focaccia Stromboli]]'''\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]][[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#dough #stromboli #oliveoil #flour #yeast #cheese #garlic #sundriedtomatoes #brush #basilleaves #smoked </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Stuffed mushrooms with Parmesan and bacon",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Stuffed mushrooms with Parmesan and bacon an Italian recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#mushrooms #homesmokedbacon #stuffedmushroomswithparmesanandbacon #oliveoil #garlic #breadcrumbs #brandy #springonions #sherry #bacon #mushroom \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=These make a great starter or an accompaniment to a main meal. Beware, they are moorish and very filling\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 790\n|PortionCalories = 395\n|DatePublished=20th January 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 2\n |Difficulty = 2\n |ImageComment = Ready for the oven\n |TotalTime = 30 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 15 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Stuffed mushrooms with Parmesan and bacon.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n }}\n\nThese make a great starter or an accompaniment to a main meal.  Beware, they are moorish and very filling.  I was in such a rush to eat these that I couldn't wait long enough to photograph the finished product! Next time...\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 2 large breakfast or [[portobello mushroom]]s\n}}\n'''Stuffing'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 1 tablespoon of [[Butter|butter]]\n| 2 tablespoons of [[Olive oil]]\n| 4 [[spring onions]]\n| 2 cloves of [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled and finely crushed\n| [[Sea salt]] and freshly ground [[black pepper]] to taste\n| 50g [[home smoked bacon]], chopped into nibble sized pieces\n| 4 tablespoons of [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]], or more depending upon the size of the mushrooms\n| 2 tablespoons of freshly grated [[Parmesan cheese]]\n| 2 tablespoons of freshly chopped [[parsley]]\n| 30ml of [[brandy]] or [[sherry]]\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the  [[oven]] to 175\u00b0C (350\u00b0F - gas 4)\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| [[Brush]] the [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]] clean, don't wash them.\n| Remove the stems from the [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]] and finely chop them.\n| Combine the butter,a Jamie Oliver sized glug of [[olive oil]] and the [[Garlic|garlic]] in a small pan and heat until it foams, reduce the heat and [[saut\u00e9]] for a few minutes, don't let it burn.\n| Add the [[Spring onions|spring onions]] and [[Mushroom|mushroom]] stems and gently [[Fry|fry]] for about 3 minutes.\n| Stir in the [[home smoked bacon]] and [[breadcrumbs]] and heat for a minute\n| Remove from the heat and stir in the parsley\n| Pack the [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]] with this mixture and top with Parmesan cheese then lay them out on a greased oven tray.\n| Pour a capful of [[brandy]] or [[sherry]] in each and top with a pinch of salt and a glug of [[olive oil]]\n| [[Bake]] for 15 minutes\n| Serve immediately\n}}\n===Variations===\nInstead of [[home smoked bacon]] you can use a similar good quality ready-to-eat meat such as [[parma ham]], [[Prosciutto]] or even [[salami]].  \n\nYou can also use normal [[bacon]]. If you do,  cook it properly first by frying with the mushrooms. Use dry cured bacon though, or you will find everything swimming in water!\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Moorish</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">I always make these too big, then eat them all.
